---
name: Ubuzima bwite kuri Bitcoin.
goal: Gutahura no kumenya neza ingingo ngenderwako zo kurinda ubuzima bwite igihe ukoresha Bitcoin.
objectives: 


  - Sigura ivyiyumviro vy'inyigisho bikenewe kugira ngo umuntu atahure ibibazo vy'ubuzima bwite
  - Kumenya no kugabanya ingorane zijanye n'ugutakaza ibanga ry'abakoresha Bitcoin
  - Gukoresha uburyo n’ibikoresho vyo kurinda ubuzima bwite bwawe kuri Bitcoin.
  - Gutahura uburyo bwo gusesangura uruzitiro no gutegura ingamba zo kwikingira


---
# Ukingire ubuzima bwite bwawe kuri Bitcoin.


Mu isi aho ibanga ry’ibikorwa vy’amahera ririko rigenda rihinduka ikintu c’agaciro, gutahura no kumenya neza ingingo ngenderwako zo kurinda ubuzima bwite igihe ukoresha Bitcoin ni ngombwa cane. Iryo shure riguha imfunguruzo zose, zo mu vyiyumviro no mu bikorwa, kugira ngo ivyo ubishikeko wigenga.


Ubu, kuri Bitcoin, amashirahamwe yizeye cane gusesangura Blockchain. Ivyo bakora canecane ni ukwinjira mu vyo ukora, kugira ngo bashobore guhungabanya ibanga ry’ivyo ukora. Mu vy'ukuri, nta kintu nk'ico "uburenganzira bwo kwirinda" kiri muri Bitcoin. Rero ni wewe ukoresha, ushobora kwemeza uburenganzira bwawe bwa kavukire no kurinda ibanga ry’amahera ukoresha, kuko nta wundi azobigukorera.


Iryo shure ryateguwe kugira ngo ribe ry’ibintu vyose kandi ry’ibintu rusangi. Iciyumviro cose c’ubuhinga kiravugwa mu buryo burambuye kandi gishigikirwa n’ibishushanyo vy’insobanuro. Intumbero ni ugutuma ubumenyi bushikira bose. BTC204 rero irashoboka ku batangura n’abayikoresha hagati. Iryo shure kandi ritanga agaciro kongerewe ku bahinga cane mu vy’ubuhinga bwa bitcoin, uko twinjira cane mu vyiyumviro bimwebimwe vy’ubuhinga akenshi bitatahurwa nabi.


Twifatanye natwe kugira ngo uhindure uko ukoresha Bitcoin maze ube umukoresha afise amakuru, ashobora gutahura ibibazo bijanye n’ibanga no kurinda ubuzima bwite bwawe.


+++
# Imenyekanisha


<partId>e17474a8-8899-4bdb-a7f8-bc52ddb01440</partId>


## Incamake y'amashure


<chapterId>08ba1933-f393-4fb5-8279-777d874caedb</chapterId>


Murakaze mu nyigisho ya BTC204!


Mu isi aho ibanga ry’ibikorwa vy’amahera ririko rigenda rihinduka ikintu c’agaciro, gutahura no kumenya neza ingingo ngenderwako zo kurinda ubuzima bwite igihe ukoresha Bitcoin ni ngombwa cane. Iryo shure riguha imfunguruzo zose, zo mu vyiyumviro no mu bikorwa, kugira ngo ivyo ubishikeko wigenga.


Ubu, kuri Bitcoin, amashirahamwe yizeye cane gusesangura Blockchain. Ivyo bakora canecane ni ukwinjira mu vyo ukora, kugira ngo bashobore guhungabanya ibanga ry’ivyo ukora. Mu vy'ukuri, nta kintu nk'ico "uburenganzira bwo kwirinda" kiri muri Bitcoin. Rero ni wewe ukoresha, ushobora kwemeza uburenganzira bwawe bwa kavukire no kurinda ibanga ry’amahera ukoresha, kuko nta wundi azobigukorera.


Bitcoin si "Number Go Up" gusa no kuzigama agaciro k'amahera uzigamye. Kubera ibiranga n’amateka yayo bidasanzwe, ni co gikoresho ca mbere c’ubutunzi bwo guhangana n’ubutunzi. Uciye kuri iyo nkuru iteye ubwoba, urashobora gukoresha amahera yawe mu mwidegemvyo, ukayakoresha kandi ukayarundanya, ata n’umwe ashobora kuguhagarika.


Bitcoin itanga ubuhungiro bw’amahoro ku ngǒgo ya Leta, ikaguha uburenganzira bwo kwinovora bimwe bishitse uburenganzira bwawe bwa kavukire, budashobora gushirwako umukono n’amategeko yashinzwe. Kubera ubuhinga bwa Satoshi Nakamoto, urafise ububasha bwo gutuma abantu bubaha umutungo wawe bwite no gusubira kuronka umwidegemvyo kuri Contract.


Ariko rero, Bitcoin ntabwo ari ikintu kitamenyekana, ivyo bikaba bishobora gutera ingorane abantu bifatanya n’ubutunzi, cane cane mu turere turi munsi y’ubutegetsi bw’agahomerabunwa. Ariko ivyo si vyo vyonyene bitera akaga. Kubera ko Bitcoin ari ikintu c’agaciro kandi kidashobora gushirwako umutima, gishobora kuba ikintu abasuma bashobora gutera. Rero kurinda ubuzima bwite bwawe na vyo nyene bica bihinduka ikibazo c’umutekano: birashobora kugufasha kwirinda gukubitwa n’abantu n’ugukubitwa ku mubiri.


Nk’uko tuzobibona, naho iyo porotokole itanga uburinzi bumwe bumwe bw’ibanga mu buryo bwayo bwite, birahambaye cane gukoresha ibindi bikoresho kugira ngo ukoreshe neza kandi ukingire iryo banga.


Iryo shure ryagenewe gutanga inyishu rusangi, yuzuye ku bibazo bijanye n’ibanga rya Bitcoin. Iciyumviro cose c’ubuhinga kiravugwa mu buryo burambuye, gishigikiwe n’ibishushanyo vy’insobanuro. Intumbero ni ugutuma ubwo bumenyi bushikira umuntu wese, mbere n’abatangura n’abari hagati. Ku ba Bitcoiners bamenyereye cane, turavuga kandi ivyiyumviro vy’ubuhinga bwinshi kandi rimwe na rimwe bitazwi cane mu nyigisho yose, kugira ngo dutahure cane icigwa cose.


Intumbero y’iri shure si iyo kukugira uwutamenyekana rwose mu gukoresha Bitcoin, ahubwo ni iyo kuguha ibikoresho vy’ingenzi vyo kumenya ingene wokingira ibanga ryawe bivanye n’intumbero zawe bwite. Uzogira umwidegemvyo wo guhitamwo mu vyiyumviro n’ibikoresho vyashikirijwe kugira ngo utegure ingamba zawe bwite, zihuye n’intumbero zawe n’ivyo ukeneye.


**Igice ca 1: Insobanuro n'ivyiyumviro nyamukuru**


Kugira ngo dutangure, turaza gusubiramwo ingingo ngenderwako z’ishimikiro zigenga ingene Bitcoin ikora, kugira ngo dushobore gutorera umuti ivyiyumviro bijanye n’ibanga. Ni ngombwa ko umenya neza ivyiyumviro bikeyi vy’ishimikiro, nka UTXO, kwakira amaderesi n’inyandiko, imbere y’uko ushobora gutahura neza ivyiyumviro tuzovuga mu bice bikurikira. Tuzozana kandi uburyo bwo gucungera ibanga rusangi bwa Bitcoin, nk’uko bwavyiyumviriye na Satoshi Nakamoto, buzotuma dushobora gutahura ingorane n’ingorane zijanye n’ivyo.


![BTC204](assets/rn/001.webp)


**Igice ca 2: Gutahura no kwikingira isesengura ry'uruzitiro**


Mu gice ca kabiri, turaba ubuhinga bukoreshwa n'amashirahamwe y'isesengura rya Blockchain kugira ngo akurikirane igikorwa cawe kuri Bitcoin. Gutahura ubwo buryo ni ikintu gihambaye cane kugira ngo ukomeze uburinzi bwawe bw’ibanga. Intumbero y’iki gice ni ugusuzuma ingamba z’abatera kugira ngo dutahure neza ingorane zishobora gushika no gutegura ubuhinga tuzokwiga mu bice bikurikira. Tuzosuzuma uburyo bwo gucuruza, ubuhinga bwo mu mutima n’ubwo hanze, n’insobanuro zishobora kuba z’ivyo bice. Uretse inyigisho, tuzokwiga ingene twokoresha Block explorer mu gusesangura uruhererekane, biciye ku ngero n’imyimenyerezo ngirakamaro.


![BTC204](assets/rn/002.webp)


**Igice ca 3: Kumenya neza ingendo nziza zo kurinda ubuzima bwite bwawe**


Mu gice ca gatatu c’inyigisho yacu, turamanuka ku bintu bitobito: kwimenyereza! Intumbero ni ukumenya neza ingendo nziza zose z’ingenzi zikwiye kuba ivyiyumviro vy’akameremere ku muntu wese akoresha Bitcoin. Tuzoba turiko turavuga ku gukoresha amaderesi ataco avuga, gushiramwo ibimenyetso, gushiramwo, gukoresha ama node yuzuye, hamwe n’uburyo bwo gukora KYC n’uburyo bwo kuronka. Intumbero ni ukuguha inyishu yuzuye y’imitego yo kwirinda kugira ngo dushireho umushinge ukomeye mu kurondera kwacu kwo kurinda ubuzima bwite. Ku bimwebimwe muri ivyo bikorwa, uzorongorwa n’inyigisho yihariye yerekeye ingene wobishira mu ngiro.


![BTC204](assets/rn/003.webp)


**Igice ca 4: Gutahura ibikorwa vya CoinJoin**


None twovuga gute ivyerekeye ubuzima bwite kuri Bitcoin tutavuze ama coinjoins? Mu gice ca 4, uzosanga ivyo ukeneye kumenya vyose ku bijanye n’ubu buryo bwo kuvanga. Uzomenya ivyo coinjoins arivyo, amateka yavyo n’intumbero zavyo, hamwe n’ubwoko butandukanye bwa CoinJoin buriho. Ubwa nyuma, ku muntu afise ubumenyi bwinshi, turaza kuraba ivyo anonsets na entropy ari vyo, n’ingene twobiharura.


![BTC204](assets/rn/004.webp)


**Igice ca 5: Gutahura ingorane z’ubundi buhinga buteye imbere bwo gucungera ibanga**


Mu gice ca gatanu, turaza kuraba ubundi buryo bwose bwo kurinda ubuzima bwite bwawe kuri Bitcoin, uretse CoinJoin. Mu myaka iheze, abahinguzi b’ibikoresho baragaragaje ubuhinga budasanzwe mu guhingura ibikoresho vyerekeye ubuzima bwite. Turaza kuraba ubwo buryo bwose, nka PayJoin, ubufatanye, Coin Swap na Atomic Swap, tuzodondora neza ingene bukora, intumbero zabwo n’intege nke zose zifise.


Turaza kandi kuraba ubuzima bwite ku rugero rw’uruzitiro rw’ibihimba n’ugukwiragira kw’ibikorwa. Turaza kandi kuganira ku mirongo ngenderwako itandukanye yashikirijwe mu myaka iheze kugira ngo yongere ubuzima bwite bw’abakoresha kuri Bitcoin, harimwo n’imirongo ngenderwako ya Address idahinduka.


![BTC204](assets/rn/005.webp)

Ni mwiteguye gutohoza ivy’ubuzima bwite kuri Bitcoin? Reka tugende!


# Insobanuro n'ivyiyumviro nyamukuru


<partId>b9bbbde3-34c0-4851-83e8-e2ffb029cf31</partId>


## Igishushanyo ca Bitcoin ca UTXO


<chapterId>8d6b50c5-bf74-44f4-922b-25204991cb75</chapterId>



Bitcoin ni amafaranga mbere na mbere, ariko mu vy’ukuri woba uzi ingene BTC ziserukirwa kuri protocole?


### UTXOs kuri Bitcoin: ni ibiki?


Itegeko rya Bitcoin rishingiye ku citegererezo ca UTXO, risobanura "Igisubizo c'Ibikorwa Bitakoreshejwe".


Ico kigereranyo gitandukanye cane n’uburyo bwa kera bwo gukoresha amabanki, bushingiye ku buryo bwo gukurikirana ingene amahera agenda. Nkako, mu bijanye n’amabanki, amahera y’umuntu ku giti ciwe aguma mu makonti afatanye n’akaranga. Nk’akarorero, iyo uguze umukate ku muntu akora umukate, banki yawe irakura gusa amahera waguze kuri konti yawe, ivyo bikaba bigabanya amahera usigaranye, mu gihe kuri konti y’uwukora umukate na ho hashirwako ayo mahera nyene, ivyo bikaba bituma amahera asigaye arushirizaho. Muri iyo nzira, nta ciyumviro c’uko hariho isano hagati y’amahera yinjira muri konti yawe n’amahera asohoka muri yo, uretse amakuru y’ibikorwa.


![BTC204](assets/rn/006.webp)


Bitcoin ikora mu buryo butandukanye. Iciyumviro ca konti ntaco kiriho, kandi amafaranga ntacungirwa biciye ku bipimo, ahubwo biciye ku ma UTXO. UTXO igereranya umubare wihariye w'ama bitcoins atarakoreshwa, gutyo bikaba bikora "igice ca Bitcoin", gishobora kuba kinini canke gito. Nk’akarorero, UTXO imwe yoshobora kuba ifise agaciro ka `500 BTC` canke gusa `700 Sats`.


**Icibutso:** Satoshi, akenshi ivugwa mu buryo bugufi ngo sat, ni igice gitoyi kuruta ibindi vyose ca Bitcoin, kigereranywa n’isenti mu mafaranga y’amahera.


```plaintext
1 BTC = 100 000 000 SATS
```


Mu vy’impwemu, UTXO imwe irashobora guserukira agaciro ako ari ko kose mu bitcoins, kuva ku sat gushika ku vyiyumviro vy’agaciro kanini cane hafi miliyoni 21 BTC. Ariko rero, birashoboka ko umuntu afise amafaranga yose y’ama bitcoins miliyoni 21, kandi hariho urugero rw’ubutunzi ruri hasi rwitwa "Dust", munsi yarwo UTXO ibonwa ko ata nyungu ifise mu vy’ubutunzi iyo umuntu akoresheje.


**Wari ubizi?** UTXO nini kuruta izindi zose zari zaremwe kuri Bitcoin zari zifise agaciro ka `500.000 BTC`. Yaremwe n’urubuga rwa MtGox mu gihe c’igikorwa co gukoranya ibintu mu kwezi kwa 11/2011: [29a3efd3ef04f9153d47a990bd7b048a4b2d213daaa5fb8ed670fb85f13bdbcf] -50.ikibanza/tx/29a3efd3ef04f9153d47a990bd7b048a4b2d213daaa5fb8ed670fb85f13bdbcf)


### UTXOs n'ingene amafaranga akoreshwa


UTXOs ni ibikoresho vya Exchange kuri Bitcoin. Igikorwa cose kivamwo ugukoresha ama UTXO nk’ibintu vy’injizwa no kurema ama UTXO mashasha nk’ibintu bisohoka. Iyo igikorwa co gucuruza kirangiye, ama UTXO akoreshwa nk'ibintu vy'injiza afatwa ko "yakoreshejwe", maze ama UTXO mashasha aravyarwa agahabwa abayaronka yerekanwa mu biva mu gicuruzwa. Gutyo, UTXO igereranya gusa umusaruro w’ibikorwa bitakoreshejwe, kandi rero umubare w’ama bitcoins ari ay’umuntu akoresha mu gihe kinaka.


![BTC204](assets/rn/007.webp)


UTXO zose zikingiwe n’inyandiko zisobanura ingene zishobora gukoreshwa. Kugira ngo umuntu akoreshe UTXO, ategerezwa kwereka urubuga ko yuzuza ibisabwa n'inyandiko icungera iyo UTXO. Mu bisanzwe, UTXOs zikingirwa n’urufunguzo rwa bose (canke Address yakira iserukira urwo rufunguzo rwa bose). Kugira ngo umuntu akoreshe UTXO ifatanye n’urwo rufunguzo rwa bose, ategerezwa kwemeza ko afise urufunguzo rw’ibanga rujanye n’urwo rufunguzo, mu gutanga umukono wa digitale wakozwe n’urwo rufunguzo. Ni co gituma tuvuga ko Bitcoin Wallet yawe mu vy’ukuri idafise ama bitcoins, ariko ibika imfunguruzo zawe z’ibanga, ivyo navyo bikaba biguha uburenganzira bwo gushika ku ma UTXO yawe, kandi, mu kwagura, ku ma bitcoins aserukira.


![BTC204](assets/rn/008.webp)


Kubera ko ata ciyumviro c'uko hariho konti muri Bitcoin, umubare w'amahera ya Wallet ni umubare w'agaciro k'ama UTXO yose ashobora gukoresha. Nk’akarorero, nimba Bitcoin Wallet yawe ishobora gukoresha UTXO 4 zikurikira:


```plaintext
- 2 BTC
- 8 BTC
- 5 BTC
- 2 BTC
```


Igitigiri cose c'ama Wallet yawe coba `17 BTC`.


![BTC204](assets/rn/009.webp)


## Imiterere y'ibikorwa vya Bitcoin


<chapterId>29d3aaab-de2e-4746-ab40-c9748898850c</chapterId>



### Ivyinjizwa n'ibisohoka mu gucuruza


Igikoresho ca Bitcoin ni igikorwa canditswe kuri Blockchain kirungika Ownership y’ama bitcoins kuva ku muntu umwe kikaja ku wundi. Mu buryo bubereye, kuko turi ku citegererezo ca UTXO kandi ata makonti ariho, iyo nzira y’ugucuruza iraheza igashitsa ivyangombwa vy’ugukoresha amahera vyari vyarakingiye UTXO imwe canke nyinshi, ikazirya kandi bingana n’ivyo irema UTXO nshasha zifise ivyangombwa bishasha vyo gukoresha amahera. Muri make, ugucuruza bikura bitcoins mu nyandiko yuzuye bikaja mu nyandiko nshasha yagenewe kuyakingira.


![BTC204](assets/rn/010.webp)


Igicuruzwa cose ca Bitcoin rero gifise ikintu kimwe canke vyinshi vyinjizwa n’ikintu kimwe canke vyinshi bisohoka. Ivyinjizwa ni UTXOs zikoreshwa n’ugucuruza ku bisohoka vya generate. Ivyiza biva ni UTXO nshasha zishobora gukoreshwa nk’ibintu vy’injiza mu bikorwa vyo muri kazoza.


![BTC204](assets/rn/011.webp)


**Wari uzi?** Mu vyiyumviro, igikorwa ca Bitcoin coshobora kugira umubare udahera w’ibintu vyinjizwa n’ibisohoka. Igitigiri conyene ni ubunini bw’ibarabara burengeye ubundi bwose.


Ivyo winjiza vyose mu gucuruza Bitcoin vyerekeye UTXO itakoreshejwe mbere. Kugira ngo umuntu akoreshe UTXO nk’inyungu, uwuyifise ategerezwa kwerekana ko ari we afise uburenganzira bwo kuyikoresha mu kwemeza inyandiko ijana na yo, ni ukuvuga mu gushitsa ivyangombwa vyo gukoresha amahera vyategekanijwe. Muri rusangi, ivyo bisigura gutanga umukono wa digitale ukoresheje urufunguzo rw'ibanga rujanye n'urufunguzo rwa bose rwabanje gukingira uru UTXO. Ico canditswe rero gishingiye ku kugenzura ko iyo sinyatire ihuye n’urufunguzo rwa bose rwakoreshejwe igihe amahera yaronswa.


![BTC204](assets/rn/012.webp)


Igisohoka cose, na co nyene, kigaragaza umubare w’ama bitcoins azorungikwa, hamwe n’uwuzoyakira. Ico ca nyuma gisobanurwa n’inyandiko nshasha, akenshi ibuza UTXO iherutse kuremwa n’i Address yakira canke urufunguzo rushasha rwa bose.


Kugira ngo igikorwa gifatwe ko gifise akamaro hakurikijwe amategeko y’uguhurizako, umusaruro wose utegerezwa kuba muto canke ungana n’umusaruro wose. Mu yandi majambo, umubare w’ama UTXO mashasha aterwa n’ugucuruza ntutegerezwa kurenga umubare w’ama UTXO akoreshwa nk’ibintu vy’inyungu. Iryo hame rirabereye: iyo ufise `500.000 Sats` gusa, ntushobora kugura `700.000 Sats`.


### Exchange no gufatanya mu gucuruza Bitcoin


Ico gikorwa c'ugucuruza Bitcoin kuri UTXO rero gishobora kugereranywa no gusubira gukora Coin y'inzahabu. Nkako, UTXO ntishobora kugabanywa, ahubwo irashobora gusenyuka gusa. Ivyo bisigura ko uwukoresha adashobora gusa kugabanya UTXO iserukira umubare kanaka mu ma bitcoins mu UTXO ntoyi nyinshi. Ategerezwa kuyikoresha yose mu gucuruza kugira ngo areme UTXO imwe canke nyinshi nshasha z’agaciro k’ububisha mu bisohoka, zitegerezwa kuba ziri munsi canke zingana n’agaciro k’intango.


Ubwo buryo busa n’ubw’inzahabu Coin. Reka tuvuge ko ufise Coin y’ama ounce 2 ugashaka kwishura ama ounce 1, twiyumvira ko uwugurisha adashobora kuguha amahera yo guhindura. Wobwirizwa gufukura Coin yawe ugatera 2 nshasha zifise ounce 1 kuri imwe yose.


Bitcoin na yo ikora mu buryo nk’ubwo nyene. Reka twiyumvire ko Alice ifise UTXO ya `10.000 Sats` kandi yipfuza kugura umukate ugura `4.000 Sats`. Alice izokora ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji n’amashanyarazi 1 UTXO ya `10.000 Sats` nk’ivyo azokoresha, ivyo azobikoresha vyose, n’ama UTXO 2 y’amashanyarazi `4.000 Sats` na `6.000 Sats` nk’ivyo azosohora. UTXO ya `4.000 Sats` izorungikirwa umutetsi mu kwishura baguette, mu gihe UTXO ya `6.000 Sats` izosubira kuri Alice mu buryo bw’ihinduka. Iyi UTXO, isubira ku muntu yatanze iyo nzira, izwi kw'izina rya "Exchange" mu rurimi rwa Bitcoin.


![BTC204](assets/rn/013.webp)


None reka twiyumvire ko Alice idafise UTXO imwe y’amashanyarazi `10.000 Sats`, ahubwo ifise UTXO zibiri z’amashanyarazi `3.000 Sats` imwe yose. Muri ivyo, nta n'imwe muri UTXOs ku giti cayo ihagije kugira ngo ishobore gushinga `4.000 Sats` y'inkoni. Alice rero ategerezwa gukoresha icarimwe izo UTXO 2 za `3.000 Sats` nk’ivyo akoresha mu gucuruza kwiwe. Muri ubwo buryo, umubare wose w’ibikoresho uzoshika ku `6.000 Sats`, bimushoboze guhazwa n’amahera `4.000 Sats` yari yarihaye umutetsi. Ubu buryo, aho UTXO nyinshi zihurizwa hamwe nk'inyungu mu gucuruza, akenshi bwitwa "gufatanya".


![BTC204](assets/rn/014.webp)


### Amafaranga y'ugucuruza


Mu buryo bw’ubuhinga, umuntu yoshobora kwiyumvira ko ibiciro vy’ugucuruza na vyo nyene bigereranya umusaruro w’ugucuruza. Ariko mu vy’ukuri, ivyo si ko biri. Ibiciro vy’ugucuruza bigereranya itandukaniro hagati y’ivyo vyose bishirwamwo n’ivyo vyose bisohoka. Ivyo bisigura ko, inyuma yo gukoresha igice c’agaciro k’ibintu vyinjijwe kugira ngo umuntu apfuke ibintu vyipfuzwa mu gucuruza, umubare kanaka w’ibintu vyinjijwe uguma udakoreshwa. Iryo shirahamwe ry’amasigarira ni ryo rigize amahera y’ugucuruza.


```plaintext
Frais = total inputs - total outputs
```


Reka dufate akarorero ka Alice, afise UTXO ya `10.000 Sats`, ashaka kugura umukate ku `4.000 Sats`. Alice irema ubucuruzi na UTXO yiwe ya `10.000 Sats` nk’inyungu. Araheza akazana umusaruro w’amafaranga `4.000 Sats` kugira ngo umutetsi ashobore kwishura iyo baguette. Kugira ngo abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro bashire ibikorwa vyiwe mu gice, Alice itanga `200 Sats` mu mahera. Araheza akarema igisubizo ca kabiri, ihinduka, rizosubirwamwo, ringana na `5.800 Sats`.


![BTC204](assets/rn/015.webp)


Dukoresheje uburyo bw’amahera, turabona ko vy’ukuri hariho `200 Sats` zisigaye ku bana bato:


```plaintext
Frais = total inputs - total outputs
Frais = 10 000 - (4 000 + 5 800)
Frais = 10 000 - 9 800
Frais = 200
```


Iyo Miner ashoboye kwemeza ububiko, arafise uburenganzira bwo gutora ayo mahera ku bikorwa vyose biri muri bubiko bwiwe, biciye ku vyo bita "coinbase" transaction.


### Gukora UTXOs kuri Bitcoin


Niba warakurikiye neza ibice vyabanje, ubu uzomenya ko UTXO zishobora kuremwa gusa mu kurya izindi UTXO zihari. Muri ubwo buryo, ibiceri vya Bitcoin birakora uruzitiro rudahengeshanya. Ariko rero, woshobora kuba uriko uribaza ingene ibihimba vya mbere vyo muri urwo ruhererekane vyabayeho. Ivyo bivyura ingorane isa n’iy’inkoko n’igi: izo UTXO z’intango zavuye hehe?


Inyishu iri mu **coinbase y’ibikorwa**.


Igikoresho c’amahera ni ubwoko bwihariye bw’ugucuruza kwa Bitcoin, ari bwo budasanzwe kuri buri bubiko kandi buhora ari ubwa mbere muri ivyo. Bituma Miner yaronse Proof of Work ibereye aronka Block reward yiwe. Iryo shimwe rigizwe n’ama Elements abiri: **block grant** na **amahera y’ugucuruza**, twavuze mu gice ca mbere.


Coinbase Transaction ni yo yihariye kuko ari yo yonyene ishobora kurema bitcoins ex nihilo, ata nkenerwa yo gukoresha ivyinjijwe ku bisohoka vya generate. Ivyo bice bishasha vyaremwe nivyo twokwita "UTXOs z'umwimerere".


![BTC204](assets/rn/016.webp)


Block-subsidized bitcoins ni BTC nshasha yaremwe kuva mu ntango, hakurikijwe urutonde rwo gutanga rwashinzwe imbere y’igihe mu mategeko y’uguhurizako. Infashanyo y'amabarabara igabanywa igice c'amabarabara 210.000, ni ukuvuga hafi buri myaka ine, mu buryo buzwi nka "Halving". Mu ntango, ama bitcoins 50 yararemwa n’infashanyo imwe imwe, ariko iyo nsiguro yaragabanutse buhoro buhoro; ubu, ni 3.125 bitcoins ku bubiko.


Naho ku bijanye n’amahera y’ibikorwa, naho nyene aserukira BTC nshasha yaremwe, ntashobora kurenga itandukaniro hagati y’ivyo vyose vyinjizwa n’ivyo bisohoka vy’ibikorwa vyose biri mu gice. Twarabonye mbere ko ayo mahera aserukira igice c’ibintu vyinjizwa bidakoreshwa mu biva mu bikorwa vy’ubudandaji. Ico gice "kirazimangana" mu buryo bw'ubuhinga mu gihe c'ugucuruza, kandi Miner irafise uburenganzira bwo gusubira kurema ako gaciro mu buryo bw'i UTXO imwe canke nyinshi nshasha. Ivyo ni uguhindura agaciro hagati y'uwutanga amafaranga n'uwa Miner ariyongera kuri Blockchain.


**Wari uzi?** Ama Bitcoins akomoka kuri Coinbase Transaction afise igihe co gukura c'ama blocks 100, muri ico gihe ntashobora gukoreshwa na Miner. Iri tegeko ryagenewe kwirinda ingorane zijanye n’ugukoresha ama bitcoins mashasha yaremwe ku ruzitiro rwoshobora guhinduka ubusa.


### Inkurikizi z'ikigereranyo ca UTXO


Mbere na mbere, urugero rwa UTXO ruragira ico rukoze ata guca ku ruhande ku mahera y’ugucuruza ya Bitcoin. Kubera ko ubushobozi bw’ibarabara rimwe rimwe ari buke, abacukuzi barakunda ibikorwa bitanga amahera meza kuruta ayandi yose ugereranije n’ahantu bazofata muri iryo barabara. Nkako, uko igikorwa gishiramwo ama UTXO menshi mu vyo yinjiza n’ivyo asohora, ni ko iremera, rero isaba amahera menshi. Iyi ni imwe mu mpamvu zituma kenshi tugerageza kugabanya igitigiri c’ama UTXO muri Wallet yacu, ivyo na vyo nyene bishobora gutuma habaho ibanga, ikintu tuzokwihweza mu buryo burambuye mu gice ca gatatu c’iri shure.


Ica kabiri, nk’uko vyavuzwe mu bice vyabanje, ibiceri vya Bitcoin mu vy’ukuri ni uruhererekane rw’ama UTXO. Igicuruzwa cose rero kiratuma habaho isano hagati ya UTXO ya kera n’iya UTXO izoza. UTXOs rero zituma bishoboka gukurikira mu buryo butomoye inzira ya Bitcoins kuva yaremwa gushika aho ikoresha ubu. Ukwo guseruka gushobora kubonwa neza, kuko gutuma uwukoresha wese ashobora kumenya neza ukuri kw’amahera ya bitcoins yaronse. Ariko kandi, ni kuri iyo ngingo ngenderwako y’ugukurikirana no gusuzuma ni ho isesengura rya Blockchain rishingiye, umugenzo ugamije gutuma ibanga ryawe rihungabana. Tuzoba turiko turaraba neza cane iyo ngeso mu gice ca kabiri c’amashure.


## Igishushanyo c'ubuzima bwite bwa Bitcoin


<chapterId>769d8963-3ed5-4094-b21d-9203c7d9e465</chapterId>



### Amahera: ukuri, ubunyankamugayo n'ugukoresha kabiri


Kimwe mu bikorwa vy’amahera ni ugutorera umuti ingorane y’uguhuza kabiri kw’ivyo umuntu akeneye. Mu buryo bushingiye ku guhinduranya, guheza Exchange ntibisaba gusa kurondera umuntu ariko aratanga ikintu gihuye n’ivyo nkeneye, ariko kandi no kumuha ikintu c’agaciro kangana kihaza ivyo we ubwiwe akeneye. Gushika kuri ubwo buringanire ni ikintu kigoye cane.


![BTC204](assets/rn/017.webp)


Ni co gituma dukoresha amahera kugira ngo twimure agaciro mu kibanza no mu gihe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/018.webp)


Kugira ngo amafaranga y’ibiceri atore umuti w’ico kibazo, birahambaye ko uwutanga ikintu canke igikorwa yemera neza ko afise ubushobozi bwo gukoresha ayo mahera mu nyuma. Gutyo, umuntu wese afise ivyiyumviro vyiza yipfuza kwemera Coin, yaba iyo kuri digitale canke iyo mu mubiri, azokwitwararika ko ihuye n’ingingo zibiri z’ishimikiro:


- Ico gice kigomba kuba gifise ubunyankamugayo n'ukuri;
- kandi ntibitegerezwa gukoreshwa kabiri.


Niba uriko urakoresha amafaranga y’umubiri, ni co kintu ca mbere kigoye cane kwemeza. Mu bihe bitandukanye vyo muri kahise, ubutungane bw’ibiceri vy’ivyuma bwarashikiwe kenshi n’imigenzo nk’ugukata canke gutobora. Nk’akarorero, i Roma ya kera, vyari bimenyerewe ko abanyagihugu bakaraba ku mpande z’ibiceri vy’inzahabu kugira ngo baronke utugingo ngengabuzima dutoduto tw’agaciro, mu gihe bakabizigama kugira ngo bazobikoreshe mu gihe kizoza. Agaciro k’imbere muri Coin rero karagabanutse, ariko agaciro kayo k’imbere karaguma ari uko nyene. Ivyo ni bimwe mu vyatumye uruhande rw’indege Coin rwaheza rugaterwa n’imirongo.


Ubunyakuri na bwo ni ikintu kigoye kugenzura ku buryo bw’amahera buboneka. Ubuhinga bwo kurwanya amahera y’ibinyoma bwo muri iki gihe buragenda burarushiriza kugorana, ivyo bikaba bituma abagurisha ibintu bashiramwo amahera menshi mu buryo bwo kugenzura amahera menshi.


Ku rundi ruhande, kubera kamere yavyo, gukoresha amahera incuro zibiri si ingorane ku mahera y’umubiri. Iyo nguhaye amafaranga y’amayero 10, arava mu vyo mfise ataco ahinduye, yinjira mu vyawe, ivyo bikaba bikuraho ubushobozi bwo gukoresha kenshi amafaranga afise. Muri make, sinzosubira gukoresha iyi fagitire y’amayero 10.


![BTC204](assets/rn/019.webp)


Ku mafaranga y’ubuhinga bwa none, ingorane ni itandukanye. Kumenya neza ko igitabu Coin ari ic’ukuri kandi ko kitagira agasembwa akenshi biroroshe. Nk’uko twabibonye mu gice ca mbere, igishushanyo ca Bitcoin ca UTXO kiratuma bishoboka gukurikirana Coin gushika aho yakomotse, gutyo bigasuzumwa ko vy’ukuri yaremwe na Miner hakurikijwe amategeko y’uguhurizako.


Ku rundi ruhande, kumenya neza ko ata Double-spending iriho biragoye cane, kuko ibintu vyose vy’ubuhinga bwa none ari amakuru nyayo. Amakuru atandukanye n’ibintu vy’umubiri, ntagabanywa iyo ahinduwe, ahubwo arakwiragira mu kugwiza. Nk’akarorero, iyo nkurungikiye inyandiko kuri e-mail, irakwisubirwamwo. Ntushobora kwemera neza ko nafuse inyandiko y’umwimerere.


![BTC204](assets/rn/020.webp)


### Gukingira gukoresha amahera kabiri kuri Bitcoin


Uburyo bumwe rudende bwo kwirinda iyo nzira yo kwisubiriza umutungo w’ubuhinga bwa none ni ukumenya ivy’uguhinduranya vyose kuri iyo sisitemu. Muri ubwo buryo, turashobora kumenya uwufise iki no guhindura ivyo umuntu wese afise bivanye n’ivyo akora. Ivyo ni vyo bishika nk’akarorero ku mahera y’ivyanditswe mu bijanye n’amabanki. Iyo urishe umucuruzi €10 ukoresheje ikarita y’inguzanyo, banki irandika Exchange maze igahindura igitabu ca konti.


![BTC204](assets/rn/021.webp)


Ku Bitcoin, Double-spending na yo irabujijwe muri ubwo buryo nyene. Turarondera kwemeza ko ata gicuruzwa camaze gukoresha ivyo biceri bivugwa. Nimba ivyo biceri bitigeze bikoreshwa, rero turashobora kwemera tudakeka ko ata n’umwe azokoresha amahera kabiri. Iryo hame ryadondowe na Satoshi Nakamoto mu gitabu cera n’amajambo azwi cane ngo:


**Uburyo bwonyene bwo kwemeza ko ata n'imwe igurishwa ni ukumenya ibikorwa vyose**


Ariko bitandukanye n'akarorero ka banki, ntidushaka kwizigira ikigo gikuru ku Bitcoin. Rero abakoresha bose barakeneye kumenya kwemeza uku kutagira amahera akoreshwa incuro zibiri, batizigiye uwundi muntu. Rero umuntu wese arakeneye kumenya amafaranga yose akoreshwa muri Bitcoin. Ni co gituma amafaranga y'ubudandaji ya Bitcoin atangazwa ku mugaragaro ku nzira zose z'urubuga kandi yandikwa mu nyandiko zitomoye kuri Blockchain.


Ukwo gukwiragiza amakuru ku mugaragaro ni kwo nyene gutuma ugukingira ubuzima bwite muri Bitcoin bigorana. Mu nzira ya kera y’amabanki, mu vyiyumviro, ikigo c’ivy’imari conyene ni co kimenya amafaranga akoreshwa. Ku rundi ruhande, na Bitcoin, abakoresha bose baramenyeshwa ivy’ibikorwa vyose, biciye ku nzira zabo.


### Icogereranyo c'ibanga: uburyo bwa banki n'uburyo bwa Bitcoin


Mu buryo bwa kera, konti yawe yo muri banki irahuye n’akaranga kawe. Uwo mukozi wa banki arashobora kumenya konti ya banki y’umukiriya uwuhe, n’amahera ajanye na yo. Ariko rero, iyo nzira y’amakuru iracika hagati ya banki n’ivy’abantu bose. Mu yandi majambo, ntibishoboka kumenya amahera asigaye n’amahera akoreshwa kuri konti ya banki y’uwundi muntu. Banki yonyene ni yo ishobora kuronka ayo makuru.


![BTC204](assets/rn/022.webp)


Nk’akarorero, umukozi wawe wo muri banki arazi ko ugura baguette yawe buri gitondo ku mutetsi wo mu karere kawe, mugabo umubanyi wawe ntaco azi ku bijanye n’ico gikorwa. Muri ubwo buryo, uruja n’uruza rw’amakuru rurashikirwa n’ababijejwe, cane cane banki, ariko ntirushikira abanyamahanga.


![BTC204](assets/rn/023.webp)


Kubera ingorane zo gukwiragiza amafaranga y’ubudandaji mu bantu bose twabonye mu gice ca mbere, uburyo bwo gucungera ibanga bwa Bitcoin ntibushobora gukurikira uburyo bwo gukoresha amabanki. Mu bijanye na Bitcoin, kubera ko uruja n’uruza rw’amakuru rudashobora guca hagati y’ibikorwa n’ivy’abantu bose, **akarorero k’ubuzima bwite bwishingikiriza ku gutandukanya akaranga k’ukoresha n’ibikorwa** ubwavyo.


![BTC204](assets/rn/024.webp)


Nk’akarorero, iyo uguze umukate ku mutetsi, uriha muri BTC, umubanyi wawe afise Full node yiwe bwite, arashobora kubona ingene amafaranga yawe agenda, nk’uko nyene ashobora kubona ayandi mafaranga yose ari muri iyo sisitemu. Ariko rero, nimba ingingo ngenderwako z’ibanga zikurikizwa, ntakwiye kuba ashoboye guhuza iyo nzira yihariye n’akaranga kawe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/025.webp)


Ariko kubera ko amafaranga y’ubudandaji ya Bitcoin amenyeshwa abantu bose, birashoboka ko habaho amasano hagati yayo kugira ngo haboneke amakuru yerekeye ababigiramwo uruhara. Ico gikorwa mbere ni ikintu kidasanzwe mu burenganzira bwaco bwite, kizwi nka "isesengura rya Blockchain". Mu gice gikurikira c’amashure, ndabatumiye gutohoza ivy’ishimikiro vy’isesengura rya Blockchain, kugira ngo mushobore gutahura ingene ama bitcoins yanyu akurikiranywa no kwikingira neza.


# Gutahura no kwikingira isesengura ry'uruzitiro


<partId>4739371e-9fef-45b0-bcaa-b7a4df6b4470</partId>


## None isesengura ry’uruzitiro rwa Bitcoin ni iki?


<chapterId>7d198ba6-4af2-4f24-86cb-3c79cb25627e</chapterId>



### Insobanuro n'imikorere


Blockchain isesengura ni umugenzo wo gukurikirana uruja n'uruza rw'ama bitcoins kuri Blockchain. Muri rusangi, isesengura ry’uruzitiro rishingiye ku kwihweza ibiranga mu ngero z’ibikorwa vya kera. Bica biva ku kumenya ivyo bimenyetso nyene ku bijanye n’ugucuruza twipfuza gusuzuma, no kubikuramwo insobanuro zishoboka. Ubu buryo bwo gutorera umuti ingorane, bushingiye ku buryo bukora bwo kuronka umuti mwiza uhagije, buzwi nka "heuristic".


Mu majambo y’abanyabwenge, hariho intambwe zitatu nyamukuru mu gusesangura uruhererekane:


1. **Kwihweza Blockchain;**


2. **Ukumenya ibiranga bizwi;**


3. **Ugukuraho ivyiyumviro**


![BTC204](assets/rn/026.webp)


Isesengura rya Blockchain rishobora gukorwa n’umuntu wese. Ico ukeneye ni ukuronka amakuru ya bose ya Blockchain biciye ku Full node kugira ngo wihweze ingene amafaranga agenda no gukora ivyiyumviro. Hariho kandi ibikoresho vy’ubuntu vyorohereza iyo nseguro, nka [OXT.me](https://oxt.me/), tuzovyihweza mu buryo burambuye mu bice bibiri vya nyuma vy’iki gice. Ariko rero, ingorane nyamukuru yo gukingira ibanga iva ku masosiyete yizeye mu gusesangura imirongo. Izo sosiyete zatwaye isesengura rya Blockchain ku rugero rw’inganda, zigurisha ibikorwa vyazo ku bigo vy’imari na Leta. Muri izo sosiyete, Chainalysis ni yo izwi cane ata gukeka.


### Intumbero z'isesengura ry'uruhererekane


Kimwe mu ntumbero z’isesengura rya Blockchain ni ugushira hamwe ibikorwa bitandukanye kuri Bitcoin kugira ngo hamenyekane ubudasa bw’uwubikoresha yabikoze. Hanyuma, bizoba bishoboka kugerageza guhuza iryo tsinda ry’ibikorwa n’akaranga nyakuri.


![BTC204](assets/rn/027.webp)


Niwiyumvire ikigabane c’imbere. Nasiguye igituma uburyo bwo gucungera ubuzima bwite bwa Bitcoin bwari bushingiye ku gutandukanya akaranga k’ukoresha n’ibikorwa. Vyoshobora rero kuba ari ikigeragezo kwiyumvira ko isesengura rya Blockchain ata co rimaze, kuko naho twoshobora gukoranya ibikorwa vy’uruzitiro, ntidushobora kubifatanya n’akaranga nyakuri.


Mu vy’impwemu, iyo mvugo ni ukuri. Mu gice ca mbere c'iri shure, twabonye ko amafunguro abiri akoreshwa mu gushinga ivyangombwa kuri UTXO. Mu vy’ukuri, izo nzira zibiri z’ingenzi ntizitangaza amakuru yerekeye akaranga k’abazifise. Rero, naho twoshobora gukoranya ibikorwa bijanye n’imigwi itandukanye y’ingenzi, ivyo ntaco bitubwira ku bijanye n’ikigo kiri inyuma y’ivyo bikorwa.


![BTC204](assets/rn/028.webp)


Ariko rero, ukuri kw’ibikorwa ni ugukomeye kuruta. Hariho inyifato nyinshi zishobora guhuza akaranga nyakuri n’igikorwa c’uruzitiro. Mu gusesangura, ivyo vyitwa ikibanza co kwinjiramwo, kandi hariho ubwinshi bwavyo.


Igisanzwe ni KYC (*Menya Umukiriya Wawe*). Iyo ukuye Bitcoins zawe ku rubuga rutegekanijwe kuri imwe mu ma aderesi yawe bwite, rero hari abantu bashobora guhuza akaranga kawe n’iyo Address. Mu buryo bwagutse, ikibanza co kwinjiramwo gishobora kuba uburyo bwose bwo gukorana hagati y’ubuzima bwawe nyakuri n’ugucuruza kwa Bitcoin. Nk’akarorero, iyo usohoye Address y’ukwakira ku mbuga ngurukanabumenyi zawe, ivyo vyoshobora kuba ikintu co kwinjiramwo co gusuzuma. Iyo urishe mu Bitcoins umufumbi wawe, azoshobora gufatanya mu maso hawe (igice c’akaranga kawe) na Bitcoin Address.


Ivyo bibanza vyo kwinjiramwo ni nk'ibidashobora kwirindwa iyo ukoresheje Bitcoin. Naho tworondera guhagarika urugero rwavyo, bazokwama bariho. Ni co gituma bihambaye cane gufatanya uburyo bugamije kuzigama ubuzima bwite bwawe. Naho kuguma utandukanya akaranga kawe nyakuri n’ivyo ukora ari uburyo bushimishije, buracari ubudahagije muri iki gihe. Nkako, nimba ibikorwa vyawe vyose vyo kuri onchain bishobora gushirwa hamwe, rero n’aho winjira hatoyi cane birashobora gutuma Layer imwe gusa y’ibanga washizeho ihungabana.


![BTC204](assets/rn/029.webp)


### Kwikingira isesengura ry'uruzitiro


Rero turakeneye kandi kumenya guhangana n'isesengura rya Blockchain mu gukoresha kwacu Bitcoin. Mu kubigira, turashobora kugabanya ugukorana kw’ibikorwa vyacu no kugabanya ingaruka z’aho twinjira ku buzima bwacu bwite.


![BTC204](assets/rn/030.webp)


Ni ubuhe buryo bwiza bwo kurwanya isesengura rya Blockchain kuruta kumenya uburyo bukoreshwa muri ryo? Niba ushaka kumenya ingene wokwongerera ubushobozi ubuzima bwite bwawe kuri Bitcoin, urakeneye gutahura ubwo buryo. Ivyo bizotuma utahura neza ubuhinga nka CoinJoin canke PayJoin (ubuhinga tuzorabira mu bice vya nyuma vy’amashure), kandi ugabanye amakosa woshobora gukora.


https://planb.network/tutorials/privacy/on-chain/coinjoin-samourai-wallet-e566803d-ab3f-4d98-9136-5462009262ef

https://planb.network/tutorials/privacy/on-chain/payjoin-848b6a23-deb2-4c5f-a27e-93e2f842140f

Muri ivyo, turashobora gushushanya n’ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru n’ugusesangura amakuru. Umuhinga mu vy’amabanga ni mbere na mbere umuhinga mu vy’amabanga. Kugira ngo utegure ubuhinga bushasha bwo gupfuka amakuru, urakeneye kumenya ibitero buzohura navyo, kandi ukiga n’igituma ubuhinga bwa kera bwacitse. Iryo hame nyene rirakora no ku bijanye n’ubuzima bwite bwa Bitcoin. Gutahura uburyo bwo gusesangura Blockchain ni urufunguruzo rwo kuvyikingira. Ni co gituma muri iri shure nashizemwo igice cose c’isesengura rya on chain.


### Uburyo bwo gusesangura uruhererekane


Ni vyiza gutahura ko gusesangura imirongo atari ubuhinga nyabwo. Ishingiye ku buhinga bwo gutahura ibintu (heuristics) buva ku vyo umuntu yabonye mbere canke ku nsobanuro zijanye n’ubwenge. Aya mategeko aratuma turonka ibisubizo vyizigirwa, ariko ntitwigere turonka ivyo turonka mu buryo butagiramwo amahinyu. Mu yandi majambo, **isesengura ry’uruzitiro ryama rifise urugero rw’ibishoboka mu nsozero zishitsweko**. Nk’akarorero, birashoboka ko umuntu agereranya ata gukeka ko amaderesi abiri ari ay’ikigo kimwe, mugabo ukudakeka kwose kuzokwama kutaboneka.


Iciyumviro cose c’isesengura ry’uruzitiro kiri mu gukoranya ubuhinga butandukanye kugira ngo hagabanuke ingorane zo gukora amakosa. Mu buryo bumwe, ni ukwirundanira ibimenyamenya bituma twegera ukuri.


Ivyo bimenyetso bizwi cane bishobora gushirwa mu mice itandukanye, ivyo tuzobidondora mu buryo burambuye aha hepfo:




- Uburyo bwo gucuruza;
- Ivyiyumviro vy'imbere mu bikorwa vy'ubudandaji;
- Ivyiyumviro vyo hanze y'ugucuruza.


### Satoshi Nakamoto n'isesengura ry'uruzitiro


Ivyo bimenyetso bibiri vya mbere vy’ugusesangura uruhererekane vyavumbuwe na Satoshi Nakamoto ubwiwe. Arabivuga mu gice ca 10 c’Igitabu Cera ca Bitcoin. Ni:




- cIOH (*Ivyinjira rusangi Ownership Ivyiyumviro*);
- na Address gusubira gukoresha.


![BTC204](assets/rn/031.webp)


Inkomoko: S. Nakamoto, "Bitcoin: Uburyo bwo gutanga amafaranga y'ubuhinga bwa none", 2009.


Tuzobona ivyo ari vyo mu bice bikurikira, ariko birasanzwe bishimishije kumenya ko izo nzira zibiri ziguma zifise akamaro kanini mu gusesangura uruhererekane muri iki gihe.


## Uburyo bwo gucuruza


<chapterId>d365a101-2d37-46a5-bfb9-3c51e37bf96b</chapterId>



Igishushanyo c’ugucuruza ni gusa ikigereranyo rusangi canke imiterere y’ugucuruza gusanzwe, bishobora kuboneka kuri Blockchain, kandi insobanuro yavyo ishobora kuba izwi. Igihe twiga ivyerekanwa, twibanda ku gikorwa kimwe gusa maze tukagisuzuma ku rugero rwo hejuru.


Mu yandi majambo, tugiye kuraba gusa umubare wa UTXO mu vyo twinjiza n’umubare wa UTXO mu vyo usohoka, tutagumye ku bintu vyihariye canke ibidukikije vy’ugucuruza. Dushingiye ku citegererezo twabonye, ​​turashobora gusobanura kamere y’ugucuruza. Tuzoheza turonde ibiranga imiterere yayo maze dushiremwo insobanuro.


![BTC204](assets/rn/032.webp)


Muri iki gice, tuzorabira hamwe ivyerekanwa nyamukuru vy’ugucuruza bihura n’ugusesangura uruhererekane, kandi ku vyerekanwa vyose, nzoguha insobanuro ishoboka y’iyi mibumbe, hamwe n’akarorero nyako.


### Ugurungika rimwe (canke kwishura rimwe)


Reka dutangure n’ikigereranyo gisanzwe cane, kuko ari co kigaragara ku mahera menshi ya Bitcoin. Uburyo bwo kwishura bworoshe burangwa n’ugukoresha UTXO imwe canke nyinshi nk’ibintu vy’injiza no gukora UTXO 2 nk’ibintu vy’injiza. Iyi modele rero isa n’iyi:


![BTC204](assets/rn/033.webp)


Iyo tubonye iyo nzira y’ugucuruza kuri Blockchain, turashobora guca dufata insobanuro. Nk’uko izina ryayo rivyerekana, iyo nzira yerekana ko turi mu gihe hariho igikorwa co kohereza canke co kwishura. Uwukoresha yakoresheje UTXO yiwe bwite mu vyo yinjiza kugira ngo ahaze mu vyo asohora UTXO y’ukwishura n’ihinduka UTXO (amahera asubizwa uwo mukoresha nyene).


Turazi rero ko uwukoresha yihwejwe kumbure atagifise imwe muri izo UTXO zibiri zisohoka (ivyo kwishura UTXO), ariko akaba agifise iyindi UTXO (ihinduka UTXO).


Kugeza ubu, ntidushobora gusobanura igisohoka giserukira UTXO iyihe, kuko iyo si yo ntumbero y’inyigisho y’akarorero. Tuzoshikayo twizigiye ubuhinga bwo kumenya ibintu (heuristics) tuzokwiga mu bice bikurikira. Muri iyi ntambwe, intumbero yacu ni iyo kumenya gusa uburyo bw’ugucuruza buvugwa, muri iki gihe ni ugutuma kworoshe.


Nk'akarorero, ng'iyi igikorwa ca Bitcoin gikoresha uburyo bworoshe bwo kohereza:


```plaintext
b6cc79f45fd2d7669ff94db5cb14c45f1f879ea0ba4c6e3d16ad53a18c34b769
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/034.webp)


Inkomoko: [Mempool.ikibanza](b6cc79f45fd2d7669ff94db5cb14c45f1f879ea0ba4c6e3d16ad53a18c34b769)


Inyuma y'akarorero ka mbere, ushobora gutahura neza ico bisobanura kwiga "akarorero k'ugucuruza". Turasuzuma igikorwa co gucuruza mu kwibanda gusa ku mibumbe yaco, tutazirikanye ibidukikije canke ido n’ido ry’ico gicuruzwa. Muri iyi ntambwe ya mbere, turiko turaraba gusa ishusho nini.


None ko mwatahuye ico ari co, reka tujane ku bindi bigereranyo biriho.


### Gukubura


Ico kigereranyo ca kabiri kirangwa n’ugukoresha UTXO imwe nk’inyungu n’uguhingura UTXO imwe nk’isohoka.


![BTC204](assets/rn/035.webp)


Insobanuro y’iki kigereranyo ni uko turi mu kubaho kw’ukwihindura. Uwukoresha yari yimuriye ama bitcoins yiwe, ayashira mu yindi Address yiwe. Kubera ko ata mpinduka iriho ku bijanye n’ugucuruza, birashoboka cane ko tuba turi mu gihe c’ugutanga amahera. Nkako, iyo umuntu yishuye, biragoye cane ko uwuyishuye agira urupapuro rwa UTXO rujanye n’amahera asabwa n’uwugurisha, akongerako amahera yo gucuruza. Muri rusangi, uwuriha rero ategerezwa gutanga umusaruro w’ihinduka.


Turamenya rero ko uwukoresha iyo UTXO ashobora kuba agifise. Mu bijanye n’isesengura ry’uruhererekane, nitwamenya ko UTXO ikoreshwa nk’inyungu mu gucuruza ari iya Alice, turashobora kwiyumvira ko UTXO ikoreshwa nk’isohoka na yo nyene ari iyawe. Icozoca gishimishije mu nyuma ni ukurondera ubuhinga bwo gukorana n’abantu bushobora gukomeza ivyo vyiyumviro (tuzobiraba mu kigabane ca 3.3).


Nk’akarorero, ng’iyi igikorwa co gucuruza Bitcoin gikoresha uburyo bwo gukubura:


```plaintext
35f1072a0fda5ae106efb4fda871ab40e1f8023c6c47f396441ad4b995ea693d
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/036.webp)


Inkomoko: [Mempool.ikibanza](Mempool.ikibanza/tx/35f1072a0fda5ae106efb4fda871ab40e1f8023c6c47f396441ad4b995ea693d)


Ariko rero, urabe neza ko ubwo bwoko bw’akarorero bushobora kandi guhishura ukwimurirwa kuri konti y’urubuga rw’amahera y’ibanga Exchange. Ni inyigisho y’amaderesi azwi n’aho ivy’ugucuruza bizotubwira nimba ari uguca ku nzira y’ukwicungera Wallet canke gukura ku rubuga. Nkako, akenshi amaderesi y’ibibanza vyo gukoreramwo Exchange aramenyekana bitagoranye.


Reka dusubire gufata akarorero ka Alice: iyo iyo scanner ijana kuri Address izwi ku rubuga (nk’akarorero Binance), ivyo bishobora gusobanura ko izo bitcoins zari zavuye mu maboko ya Alice ataco akora, kumbure n’intumbero yo kuzigurisha canke kuzibika kuri uru rubuga. Ku rundi ruhande, nimba aho Address ija itazwi, birabereye kwiyumvira ko ari uwundi Wallet ukiri uwa Alice. Ariko ubwo bwoko bw’inyigisho buri mu rwego rw’ubuhinga bwo kumenya ibintu kuruta ubuhinga bwo kumenya ibintu.


### Gushiramwo


Ico kigereranyo kirangwa no gukoresha UTXO nyinshi ku nzira y’injiza no gukora UTXO imwe ku nzira y’isohoka.


![BTC204](assets/rn/037.webp)


Insobanuro y’ico kigereranyo ni uko turi mu kubaho kw’ugushikama. Ivyo ni umugenzo usanzwe mu bakoresha Bitcoin, bigamije gufatanya UTXO nyinshi mu kwitega ko amafaranga y’ugucuruza yoshobora kwongerekana. Mu gukora iyo nzira mu kiringo amahera ari make, birashoboka ko umuntu azigama amahera azotanga muri kazoza. Tuzovuga vyinshi kuri iyo ngeso mu kigabane ca 4.3.


Turashobora gufata ingingo y’uko uwukoresha inyuma y’iyi nzira y’ugucuruza yari afise kumbure ama UTXO yose mu vyo yinjiza kandi aracari afise UTXO mu vyo asohora. Rero birashoboka ko ari uguhindura umuntu.


Cokimwe n’ugukubura, ubwo bwoko bw’akarorero burashobora kandi guhishura ukwimurirwa ku nkuru y’urubuga rwa Exchange. Ni inyigisho y’amaderesi azwi n’aho ivy’ugucuruza bizotubwira nimba ari ugushira hamwe ku Wallet y’ukwicungera canke ugukura ku rubuga.


Nk’akarorero, ng’iki igikorwa ca Bitcoin gikoresha uburyo bwo gushiramwo:


```plaintext
77c16914211e237a9bd51a7ce0b1a7368631caed515fe51b081d220590589e94
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/038.webp)


Inkomoko: [Mempool.ikibanza](Mempool.ikibanza/tx/77c16914211e237a9bd51a7ce0b1a7368631caed515fe51b081d220590589e94)


Mu gusesangura uruhererekane, iyo nzira irashobora guhishura amakuru menshi cane. Nk’akarorero, nitwamenya ko kimwe mu vyo twinjiza ari ica Alice, twoshobora kwiyumvira ko ibindi vyose vyinjizwa n’ivyo biva muri iyo nzira na vyo nyene ari ivyiwe. Ivyo vyiyumviro vyotuma rero bishoboka gusubira mu ruhererekane rw'ibikorwa vya kera kugira ngo umuntu abone kandi asesengure ibindi bikorwa bishobora kuba bifitaniye isano na Alice.


![BTC204](assets/rn/039.webp)


### Amafaranga yashizwe hamwe


Ico kigereranyo kirangwa n’ugukoresha ama UTXO makeyi nk’ibintu bikoreshwa (kenshi kimwe gusa) no gukora ama UTXO menshi nk’ibintu bisohoka.


![BTC204](assets/rn/040.webp)


Insobanuro y’iki kigereranyo ni uko turi mu kubaho kw’amahera akoreshwa mu migwi. Ni umugenzo kumbure ugaragaza igikorwa kinini cane c’ubutunzi, nk’urubuga rwa Exchange. Gukoresha amahera mu migwi biratuma izo nzego zishobora kuzigama amahera mu gufatanya amahera zikoresha mu gikorwa kimwe.


Turashobora gukura muri iyo nzira ko UTXO mu vyo kwinjiza iva mw’ishirahamwe rifise ibikorwa vy’ubutunzi vy’agaciro kanini, kandi ko UTXOs mu vyo gusohora zizokwiragizwa. Benshi bazoba ari abo bakiriya b’iyo sosiyete bakuye ama bitcoins kuri iyo nzira. Abandi boshobora kuja mu mashirahamwe bafatanya. Ubwa nyuma, nta gukeka ko hazoba ihinduka rimwe canke menshi rizosubira ku sosiyete yatanze.


Nk'akarorero, ng'iyi igikorwa ca Bitcoin gikoresha uburyo bwo gukoresha amahera (bishoboka ko ari igikorwa casohowe n'urubuga rwa Bybit):


```plaintext
8a7288758b6e5d550897beedd13c70bcbaba8709af01a7dbcc1f574b89176b43
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/041.webp)


Inkomoko: [Mempool.ikibanza](8a7288758b6e5d550897beedd13c70bcbaba8709af01a7dbcc1f574b89176b43)


### Ibikorwa vyihariye vy'amasezerano


Mu mice y’ugucuruza, turashobora kandi kumenya iyo yerekana ikoreshwa ry’umurongo kanaka. Nk’akarorero, ama coinjoins ya Whirlpool (yavuzwe mu gice ca 5) azogira ubuhinga bwo kumenya bitagoranye buzoyatandukanya n’ibindi bikoresho bisanzwe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/042.webp)


Isesengura ry’ico kigereranyo rirerekana ko bishoboka ko tuba turi mu kubaho kw’ugukorana n’abandi. Birashoboka kandi ko umuntu abona CoinJoin. Iyo iki ciyumviro ca nyuma kigaragaye ko ari ukuri, rero igitigiri c'abasohoka coshobora kuduha ingereranyo y'igitigiri c'abazoja muri CoinJoin.


Nk’akarorero, ng’iyi igikorwa co gucuruza ca Bitcoin gikoresha uburyo bwo gucuruza bwa CoinJoin:


```plaintext
00601af905bede31086d9b1b79ee8399bd60c97e9c5bba197bdebeee028b9bea
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/043.webp)


Inkomoko: [Mempool.ikibanza](Mempool.ikibanza/tx/00601af905bede31086d9b1b79ee8399bd60c97e9c5bba197bdebeee028b9bea)


Hariho n’izindi protocoles nyinshi zifise imiterere yazo yihariye. Nk’akarorero, hariho amafaranga y’i Wabisabi, amafaranga y’ibidodo n’amafaranga y’ama Runes.


Kubera izo nzira z’ugucuruza, turashobora gusobanura amakuru amwamwe yerekeye ugucuruza kanaka. Ariko imiterere y’ibikorwa si yo yonyene isoko y’amakuru yo gusesangura. Turashobora kandi kwiga ido n’ido ryaryo. Ivyo bintu vy'imbere nivyo nkunda kwita "internal heuristics", kandi tuzobiraba mu kigabane gikurikira.


## Ivyiyumviro vyo mu mutima


<chapterId>c54b5abe-872f-40f4-a0d0-c59faff228ba</chapterId>



Heuristic internal ni ikintu kidasanzwe tubona mu gikorwa ubwaco, tutakeneye gusuzuma ibidukikije vyaco, kandi kidushoboza gukuraho. Mu buryo butandukanye n’ibigereranyo, vyibanda ku mibumbe rusangi y’ugucuruza ku rugero rwo hejuru, ubuhinga bwo kumenya imbere mu mutima bushingiye ku makuru ashobora gukurwamwo. Ivyo birimwo:




- Amafaranga y’ama UTXO atandukanye yinjira n’asohoka;
- Ivyo vyose bijanye n'inyandiko: aderesi zo kwakira, guhindura, ibihe vyo gufunga..


Muri rusangi, ubwo bwoko bw’ubuhinga buzodushoboza kumenya ihinduka riri mu gicuruzwa kinaka. Mu kubigira, turashobora rero gukomeza gukurikirana ikintu ku bikorwa bitandukanye. Nkako, iyo tumenye UTXO y’umukoresha twipfuza gukurikirana, birahambaye cane kumenya, igihe akora igikorwa, ni igisohoka ikihe carungitswe ku wundi mukozi n’ico gisohoka giserukira ihinduka, rero kiguma mu minwe yiwe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/044.webp)


Reka nongere ndabibutse ko izo heuristics zitari nziza rwose. Iyo zifashwe umwumwe wese ku giti ciwe, zituma gusa tumenya ibintu bishobora gushika. Ni ukwirundanira kw’ibintu vyinshi bifasha kugabanya ukudakeka, ata n’umwe ashobora kubikuraho burundu.


### Ibisa n'ivyo mu mutima


Iryo koraniro ry’ubuhinga ryitwa heuristic ririmwo inyigisho y’ibintu bisa hagati y’ibintu vyinjizwa n’ibintu bisohoka mu gikorwa kimwe. Iyo iyo kamere nyene ibonetse ku bintu vyinjizwa no kuri kimwe gusa mu bisohoka vy’ugucuruza, rero birashoboka ko ico gisohoka ari co gihindura.


Ikintu kigaragara cane ni ugusubira gukoresha Address yakira muri iyo nzira nyene.


![BTC204](assets/rn/045.webp)


Iryo heuristic ntirisiga ikibanza kinini co gukekeranya. Keretse iyo afise urufunguzo rwiwe rw’ibanga rwaciwe, uwo nyene kwakira Address birahishura vy’ukuri igikorwa c’ukoresha umwe. Insobanuro ivamwo ni uko ihinduka ry’ugucuruza ari igisohoka gifise Address imwe n’iyinjira. Turashobora rero kubandanya gukurikirana uwo muntu kuva kuri iryo hinduka.


Nk'akarorero, ng'iyi igikorwa aho iyi heuristic ishobora gukoreshwa:


```plaintext
54364146665bfc453a55eae4bfb8fdf7c721d02cb96aadc480c8b16bdeb8d6d0
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/046.webp)


Inkomoko: [Mempool.ikibanza](Mempool.ikibanza/tx/54364146665bfc453a55eae4bfb8fdf7c721d02cb96aadc480c8b16bdeb8d6d0)


Ivyo bisa hagati y’ivyo winjiza n’ivyo usohora ntibihagarara ku gusubira gukoresha Address. Ivyo vyose bisa mu gukoresha inyandiko birashobora gukoreshwa mu gukoresha heuristic. Nk’akarorero, rimwe na rimwe turashobora kubona ubuhinga bumwe hagati y’ivyo twinjiza n’ivyo dusohora.


![BTC204](assets/rn/047.webp)


Kuri iki kigereranyo, turashobora kubona ko injiza n° 0 ifungura inyandiko ya P2WPKH (SegWit V0 itangura na `bc1q`). Igisohoka n° 0 gikoresha ubwoko bumwe bw'inyandiko. Igisohoka n° 1, ku rundi ruhande, gikoresha inyandiko ya P2TR (SegWit V1 itangura na `bc1p`). Insobanuro y'iki kintu ni uko bishoboka ko Address ifise verisiyo imwe n'iyo yinjijwe ari ihinduka Address. Vyoba rero vyama ari ivy’uwubikoresha umwe.


Aha niho hari ugucuruza aho iyi heuristic ishobora gukoreshwa:


```plaintext
db07516288771ce5d0a06b275962ec4af1b74500739f168e5800cbcb0e9dd578
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/048.webp)


Inkomoko: [Mempool.ikibanza](Mempool.ikibanza/tx/db07516288771ce5d06b275962ec4af1b74500739f168e5800cbcb0e9dd578)


Ku bijanye n’ivyo vya nyuma, turashobora kubona ko input no. 0 n’isohoka no. 1 ikoresha inyandiko za P2WPKH (SegWit V0), mu gihe igisohoka no. 0 ikoresha inyandiko itandukanye ya P2PKH (Iragi).


Mu ntango z’imyaka ya 2010, iyo heuristic ishingiye ku guhindura inyandiko ntiyari ifise akamaro kubera ubwoko buke bw’inyandiko bwariho. Ariko rero, uko igihe cagenda kirarenga be n’uko Bitcoin yagenda irahindurwa, harashizweho ubwoko bwinshi bw’inyandiko. Iyi heuristic rero iriko irarushiriza kuba ngirakamaro, nk’uko mu gihe c’ubwoko bwinshi bw’inyandiko, abakoresha bagabanya mu migwi mito mito, gutyo bikongera amahirwe yo gukoresha iyi heuristic yo gusubira gukoresha versioning y’imbere. Kubera iyo mpamvu, uhereye ku bijanye n’ibanga gusa, ni vyiza guhitamwo ubwoko bw’inyandiko busanzwe. Nk’akarorero, uko ndiko ndandika iyi mirongo, inyandiko za Taproot (`bc1p`) zikoreshwa cane kuruta inyandiko za SegWit V0 (`bc1q`). Naho ivya mbere bitanga inyungu mu vy’ubutunzi no mu vy’ibanga mu bihe bimwebimwe vyihariye, ku bijanye n’ugukoresha umukono umwe mu buryo busanzwe, vyoshobora kuba vyiza umuntu agumye ku ngingo ngenderwako ya kera kubera imvo z’ibanga, gushika iyo ngingo ngenderwako nshasha yemejwe cane.


### Igitigiri c'ukwishyura


Iyindi heuristic yo mu mutima ishobora kudufasha kumenya ihinduka ni heuristic y’umubare uzunguruka. Muri rusangi, iyo umuntu ahanganye n’uburyo bwo kwishura bworoshe (1 input na 2 outputs), iyo kimwe muri ivyo bisohoka gikoresheje amahera azunguruka, rero ivyo bigereranya ukwishura.


![BTC204](assets/rn/049.webp)


Mu gukuraho, iyo umusaruro umwe ugereranya ukwishyura, uwundi ugereranya uguhinduka. Bishobora rero gusobanurwamwo ko bishoboka ko uwukoresha inyungu yama afise igisohoka kigaragazwa nk’ihinduka.


Hakwiye gushimikwako ko iyo heuristic idahora ikoreshwa, kuko amahera menshi yishurwa aguma akoreshwa mu bice vy’ivy’ubuhinga. Nkako, iyo umucuruzi wo mu Bufaransa yemeye Bitcoin, muri rusangi ntazokwerekana ibiciro bihoraho mu Sats. Ahubwo azohitamwo guhindura hagati y’igiciro kiri mu ma euro n’amahera azorihwa mu ma bitcoins. Nta mibare rero izunguruka ikwiye kubaho ku mpera y’ugucuruza.


Naho ari ukwo, umuhinga mu vy’ugusesangura yoshobora kugerageza gukora iyo mpinduka azirikana igipimo ca Exchange cariho igihe iyo nzira yatangazwa ku rubuga. Reka dufate akarorero k’isoko rifise inyungu ya `97.552 Sats` n’inyungu zibiri, imwe ya `31.085 Sats` iyindi ya `64.152 Sats`. Umuntu aravye neza, iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ntiyiboneka ko irimwo amahera azunguruka. Ariko rero, dukoresheje igipimo ca Exchange c’amayero 64.339 igihe c’ugucuruza, turaronka uguhindura mu mayero nk’uko bikurikira:




- Ivyo winjiza ni €62,76;
- Igisohoka c’amayero 20;
- Ivyo bivako ni €41.27.


Iyo ihinduwe mu mafaranga y’amahera, iyo nzira ishobora gukoreshwa mu gukoresha ubuhinga bwo kwishura amahera azunguruka. Ivyo €20 vyasohotse birashoboka ko vyagiye ku mudandaza, canke n’imiburiburi vyahinduye Ownership. Mu gukuraho, umusaruro w’amayero 41,27 birashoboka ko wagumye mu minwe y’uwawukoresheje mbere.


![BTC204](assets/rn/050.webp)


Iyo, umusi umwe, Bitcoin ibaye igice c’ikonti gikundwa cane mu guhanahana kwacu, iyo heuristic yoshobora mbere kuba ngirakamaro mu gusesangura.


Nk'akarorero, ng'iki igikorwa co gucuruza iyo heuristic ishobora gukoreshwako:


```plaintext
2bcb42fab7fba17ac1b176060e7d7d7730a7b807d470815f5034d52e96d2828a
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/051.webp)


Inkomoko: [Mempool.ikibanza](2bcb42fab7fba17ac176060e7d7d7730a7b807d470815f5034d52e96d2828a)


### Igisohoka kinini kuruta ibindi vyose


Iyo tubonye itandukaniro rinini rihagije hagati y’ibiva mu bikorwa 2 vy’ugucuruza ku buryo bworoshe bwo kwishura, turashobora kugereranya ko umusaruro munini cane ushobora kuba ari wo mpinduka.


![BTC204](assets/rn/052.webp)


Iyi heuristic y’umusaruro nini kuruta izindi ni yo ata gukeka idatomoye kuruta izindi zose. Ku bwavyo, ni vyiza cane bigoyagoya. Ariko rero, ico kintu gishobora gufatanywa n’ibindi bimenyetso vy’ubuhinga (heuristics) kugira ngo bigabanye ukudakeka kw’insobanuro yacu.


Nk’akarorero, nimba turiko turaraba igikorwa gifise ukwishura gukikuje n’ukwishura kwinshi, gukoresha ubuhinga bwo kwishura buzunguruka n’ubuhinga bwo kwishura bunini hamwe bigabanya urugero rwacu rw’ukudakeka.


Nk'akarorero, ng'iyi igikorwa aho iyi heuristic ishobora gukoreshwa:


```plaintext
b79d8f8e4756d34bbb26c659ab88314c220834c7a8b781c047a3916b56d14dcf
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/053.webp)


Inkomoko: [Mempool.ikibanza](b79d8f8e4756d34bbb26c659ab88314c220834c7a8b781c047a3916b56d14dcf)


## Ivyiyumviro vyo hanze


<chapterId>4a170e3b-200d-431a-8285-18a23ff617ba</chapterId>



Ivyigwa vy’ubuhinga bwo hanze bisigura gusuzuma ivyo bisa, uburyo n’ibiranga Elements zimwe zimwe zidasanzwe ku bijanye n’ugucuruza ubwavyo. Mu yandi majambo, naho mbere twari twigarukiye ku gukoresha Elements iri mu mutima w’ugucuruza n’ubuhinga bwo mu mutima, ubu turiko turagwiza igice cacu c’isesengura kugira ngo tushiremwo ibidukikije vy’ugucuruza, bivuye ku buhinga bwo hanze.


### Address gusubira gukoresha


Iyi ni imwe mu nzira zizwi cane z’aba bitcoiners. Gusubira gukoresha Address bituma bishoboka gushinga uruja n’uruza hagati y’ibikorwa bitandukanye n’ama UTXO atandukanye. Bishika iyo Bitcoin yakira Address ikoreshejwe incuro nyinshi.


Gutyo, birashoboka gukoresha Address gusubira gukoresha mu gihe c’ugucuruza kumwe nk’ubuhinga bwo kumenya ihinduka (nk’uko twabibonye mu kigabane c’imbere). Ariko Address gusubira gukoresha birashobora kandi gukoreshwa nk’ubuhinga bwo hanze kugira ngo umuntu amenye ubudasa bw’ikintu kiri inyuma y’ibikorwa vyinshi.


Insobanuro yo gusubira gukoresha Address ni uko UTXO zose zibujijwe kuri iyo Address ziri (canke zari ziri) z’ikigo kimwe. Iryo heuristic risiga umwanya mutoyi w’ukudakeka. Iyo bimaze kumenyekana, insobanuro ivamwo birashoboka ko ihuye n’ukuri. Bituma rero habaho ugushira mu mirwi ibikorwa bitandukanye vyo ku ruzitiro.


![BTC204](assets/rn/054.webp)


Nk’uko vyasiguwe mu ntangamarara y’igice ca 3, iyo heuristic yavumbuwe na Satoshi Nakamoto ubwiwe. Mu gitabu cera, avuga umuti wo gufasha abakoresha kwirinda kugitanga, ni ukuvuga gusa gukoresha Address ata co ivuga ku bijanye n’ugucuruza gushasha kwose:


"_Nk'uruhome rw'umuriro rw'inyongera, urufunguzo rushasha rushobora gukoreshwa kuri buri gucuruza kugira ngo rugume rudahuye na nyen'urufunguzo rusangi._"


![BTC204](assets/rn/055.webp)


Inkomoko: S. Nakamoto, "Bitcoin: Uburyo bwo gutanga amafaranga y'ubuhinga bwa none", 2009.


Nk’akarorero, ng’iyi Address isubira gukoreshwa mu bikorwa vyinshi:


```plaintext
bc1qqtmeu0eyvem9a85l3sghuhral8tk0ar7m4a0a0
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/056.webp)


Inkomoko: [Mempool.ikibanza](Mempool.ikibanza/Address/bc1qqtmeu0eyvem9a85l3sghural8tk0ar7m4a0a0)


### Ugusa n'inyandiko n'icapa rya Wallet


Uretse gusubira gukoresha Address, hariho n’ibindi bimenyetso vyinshi bigufasha guhuza ibikorwa n’ikigwi kimwe ca Wallet canke Address.


Ica mbere, umusesanguzi arashobora kurondera ivyo bisa mu gukoresha inyandiko. Nk’akarorero, inyandiko zimwe zimwe z’abantu batobato nka Multisig zishobora kworoha kubona kuruta inyandiko za SegWit V0. Uko umugwi twihishamwo uba munini, ni ko bigorana kutubona. Iyi ni imwe mu mpamvu zituma, ku masezerano meza ya CoinJoin, abaje mu nama bose bakoresha ubwoko bumwe nyabwo bw’inyandiko.


Muri rusangi, umusesanguzi arashobora kandi kwibanda ku bimenyetso vy’intoke vy’i Wallet. Ivyo ni inzira zijanye n’ikoreshwa zishobora kumenyekana kugira ngo zikoreshwe nk’ubuhinga bwo gukurikirana. Mu yandi majambo, nitwabona ukwirundanira kw’ibiranga nyene vyo mu mutima ku bikorwa vy’ubudandaji vyerekeye ikigo gikurikiranywe, turashobora kugerageza kumenya ivyo biranga nyene ku bindi bikorwa vy’ubudandaji.


Nk'akarorero, tuzoshobora kumenya ko uwukoresha akurikiranye yohereza ihinduka ryiwe ku ma aderesi ya P2TR (`bc1p...`). Iyo iyo nzira isubiwemwo, turashobora kuyikoresha nk’ubuhinga bwo gutahura ibintu (heuristic) mu gihe gisigaye c’isesengura ryacu. Turashobora kandi gukoresha ibindi bimenyetso vy'intoke, nk'urutonde rwa UTXOs, ikibanza c'ihinduka mu bisohoka, ikimenyetso ca RBF (Replace-by-fee), canke inomero ya verisiyo, umwanya wa `nSequence` n'umwanya wa `nLockTime`.


![BTC204](assets/rn/057.webp)


Nk’uko [@LaurentMT](https://twitter.com/LaurentMT) abivuga muri [Igitabu c’Ikirere #19](Ikiganiro c’Ikirere. Podcast yo mu rurimi rw’igifaransa), akamaro k’ibimenyetso vy’intoke vya Wallet mu gusesangura uruhererekane karagenda karagwira cane uko igihe kigenda kirarenga. Nkako, ukuntu ubwoko bw’inyandiko buriko buragwira be n’ukuntu ivyo bintu bishasha bigenda birakoreshwa na porogarama ya Wallet, biratuma habaho ubudasa. Mu bihe bimwebimwe, birashoboka mbere ko umuntu amenya porogarama nyayo ikoreshwa n’ico kigo gikurikirana. Ni ngombwa rero gutahura ko inyigisho y’ibirenge vya Wallet ari ngirakamaro cane cane ku bikorwa vy’ubudandaji biherutse gukorwa, aho gushingira ku vyo vyatanguye mu ntango z’imyaka ya 2010.


Mu guca irya n’ino, ikirenge gishobora kuba umugenzo uwo ari wo wose wihariye, ukorwa ubwawo na Wallet canke n’uwuwukoresha, dushobora gusanga ku bindi bikorwa kugira ngo bidufashe mu gusesangura kwacu.


### Injiza rusangi Ownership Ivyiyumviro (CIOH)


Igiharuro ca Common Input Ownership Heuristic (CIOH) ni igiharuro kivuga ko iyo igikorwa gifise ibiharuro vyinshi, vyose bishobora kuva ku kintu kimwe. Ku bw’ivyo, Ownership yabo irasanzwe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/058.webp)


Kugira ngo dukoreshe CIOH, tubanje kwihweza igikorwa gifise ibintu vyinshi vyinjizwa. Ivyo bishobora kuba 2 vy’injiza, canke 30 vy’injiza. Ico kiranga kimaze kumenyekana, turasuzuma nimba iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ihuye n’akarorero k’ugucuruza kazwi. Nk'akarorero, nimba hariho ibintu 5 vyinjizwa bifise umubare umwe n'ibintu 5 bisohoka bifise umubare umwe, tuzomenya ko ari imiterere ya CoinJoin. Ntituzoshobora gukoresha CIOH.


![BTC204](assets/rn/059.webp)


Ku rundi ruhande, iyo igikorwa co gucuruza kitajanye n’uburyo bwo gucuruza buzwi bw’ubufatanye, rero turashobora gusobanura ko ivyo vyose bishobora kuva mu kigo kimwe. Ivyo birashobora kuba ngirakamaro cane mu kwagura ikirundo gisanzwe kizwi canke mu kubandanya urutonde.


![BTC204](assets/rn/060.webp)


CIOH yavumbuwe n’indege yitwa Satoshi yitwa Nakamoto. Abivuga mu gice ca 10 c’Igitabu Cera:


"_[...] guhuza ni ikintu kitari bwigere gishoboka n'ibikorwa vy'injira vyinshi, ivyo bikaba vyerekana ko ibikorwa vyavyo vyari bifiswe na nyen'urufunguzo umwe. Ico kibazo ni uko iyo nyir'urufunguzo ahishuwe, ayo mahuza ashobora kwerekana ayandi mafaranga yari aya nyen'urufunguzo umwe._"


![BTC204](assets/rn/061.webp)


Biratangaje cane kubona ko Satoshi Nakamoto, mbere n’imbere y’uko Bitcoin itanguzwa ku mugaragaro, yari amaze kumenya ingorane zibiri nyamukuru z’ubuzima bwite ku bakoresha, ni ukuvuga CIOH na Address gusubira gukoresha. Mwene ukwo kubona imbere y’igihe ni ikintu gitangaje cane, kuko izo nzira zibiri ziguma, mbere n’ubu, ari zo ngirakamaro kuruta izindi mu gusesangura Blockchain.


Kugira ngo ndabahe akarorero, ng’iyi transaction kumbure dushobora gukoresha CIOH:


```plaintext
20618e63b6eed056263fa52a2282c8897ab2ee71604c7faccfe748e1a202d712
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/062.webp)


Inkomoko: [Mempool.ikibanza](20618e63b6eed056263fa52a2282c8897ab2ee71604c7faccfe748e1a202d712)


### Amakuru ya off-chain


Ego ni ko, isesengura ry’uruzitiro ntirigarukira gusa ku makuru yo ku ruzitiro. Amakuru yose ava mu gusesangura kwa kera canke aboneka kuri Internet na yo nyene arashobora gukoreshwa mu gutunganya isesengura.


Nk’akarorero, nitwabona ko amafaranga akurikiranywe atangazwa mu buryo butunganye avuye ku nzira imwe ya Bitcoin, maze tukamenya IP yayo Address, twoshobora kumenya ayandi mafaranga ava ku kigo kimwe, hamwe no kumenya igice c’akaranga k’uwutanga. Naho iyo ngeso idashoboka, kuko isaba gukoresha utugingo ngengabuzima twinshi, ishobora gukoreshwa n’amashirahamwe amwe amwe yizeye mu gusesangura Blockchain.


Uwo musesanguzi arafise kandi uburenganzira bwo kwizigira isesengura ry’imbere ryakozwe mu buryo bw’ubuhinga bufunguye, canke isesengura ryiwe bwite ry’imbere. Kumbure tuzoshobora kuronka igisohoka kigaragaza ikirundo c’amaderesi twamaze kumenya. Rimwe na rimwe, birashoboka kandi kwizigira ibisohoka vyerekana urubuga rwa Exchange, nk’uko amaderesi y’ayo masosiyete azwi muri rusangi.


Mu buryo nk’ubwo nyene, urashobora gukora isesengura mu gukuraho. Nk’akarorero, nimba igihe dusuzuma igikorwa gifise ibisohoka bibiri, kimwe muri vyo gifitaniye isano n’ikigwi ca Address gisanzwe kizwi, ariko gitandukanye n’ikintu turiko turakurikirana, rero turashobora gusobanura ko ikindi gisohoka gishobora kuba giserukira ihinduka.


Isesengura ry’imirongo kandi ririmwo igice ca OSINT (*Ubwenge bw’Isoko Yuguruye*) rusangi gatoyi, kirimwo ugushakashaka kuri internet. Ni co gituma duhanura ko umuntu adashobora gutangaza amaderesi ataco akora ku mbuga ngurukanabumenyi canke ku rubuga rwa interineti, yaba ari ay’uruyeri canke atari yo.


![BTC204](assets/rn/063.webp)


### Ivyitegererezo vy'igihe


Turavyiyumvira bike, ariko inyifato zimwe zimwe z’abantu ziramenyekana onchain. Kumbure ikintu gifise akamaro kuruta ibindi vyose mu gusuzuma ni ukuntu usinzira! Ego cane iyo uryamye, ntutangaza amakuru ya Bitcoin. Ariko muri rusangi uryama nk’isaha imwe. Ni co gituma ari umugenzo gukoresha isesengura ry'igihe mu isesengura rya Blockchain. Mu buryo bworoshe, iri ni ibarura ry’ibihe amafaranga y’ikigo kinaka atangazwa ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin. Dusuzumye ivyo bigereranyo vy’igihe, turashobora gukuramwo amakuru menshi cane.


Mbere na mbere, isesengura ry’igihe rimwe na rimwe rirashobora kugaragaza kamere y’ikintu gikurikiranywe. Nitwabona ko amafaranga atangazwa ata guhinduka mu masaha 24, ivyo rero bizogaragaza igikorwa c’ubutunzi kiri ku rugero rwo hejuru. Ikigo kiri inyuma y’ivyo bikorwa gishobora kuba ari ishirahamwe, rishobora kuba ari iryo kw’isi yose kandi kumbure rifise uburyo bwo gukora mu nzu.


Nk’akarorero, [Namenye iyo nzira mu mezi makeyi aheze] (https://witter.com/Loic_Pandul/status/1701127409712452072) igihe nariko ndasesangura [isoko ryari ryatanze mu makosa ama bitcoins 19 mu 2012). amafaranga](Mempool.ikibanza/tx/d5392d474b4c436e1c9d1f4ff4be5f9bb0eb2e26b61d2781751474b7e870fd). Isesengura ryoroshe ry’igihe ryatumye nshobora kwiyumvira ko twariko turakorana n’igikorwa c’ubuhinga, kandi rero kumbure n’ikintu kinini nk’urubuga rwa Exchange.


Nkako, haciye imisi mikeyi, vyavumbuwe ko ayo mahera ari aya PayPal, biciye ku rubuga rwa Paxos Exchange.


Ahubwo, nimba dushobora kubona ko igihe gica mu masaha 16, rero turashobora kugereranya ko turiko turakorana n’umuntu ku giti ciwe, canke kumbure ishirahamwe ryo mu karere bivanye n’ingero z’ibintu vyahinduwe.


Uretse kamere y’ikintu cihwejwe, urugero rw’igihe rurashobora kandi kutubwira hafi aho uwukoresha ari, bivuye ku bice vy’amasaha. Muri ubwo buryo, turashobora guhuza n’ibindi bikorwa, maze tugakoresha ibimenyetso vy’igihe vyavyo nk’inyongera y’ubuhinga bwo kumenya ibintu bishobora kwongerwa ku nseguro yacu.


Nk’akarorero, kuri Address ikoreshwa kenshi navuga, turashobora kubona ko amafaranga yinjira n’asohoka, yibanda ku kiringo c’amasaha 13.


```plaintext
bc1qqtmeu0eyvem9a85l3sghuhral8tk0ar7m4a0a0
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/064.webp)


Inkomoko: OXT.me


Ico kibanza gishobora kuba gihuye n’Uburayi, Afirika canke Uburasirazuba bwo Hagati. Turashobora rero kwiyumvira ko uwukoresha ivyo bicuruzwa aba muri ivyo bice.


Mu buryo butandukanye, isesengura ry’igihe ry’ubwo bwoko na ryo nyene ryatumye habaho iciyumviro c’uko Satoshi Nakamoto itariko irakora ivuye mu Buyapani, ariko ivuye muri Amerika: [*Ibihe vy’indege ya Satoshi Nakamoto*]


## Kubishira mu ngiro n’igitabu Block explorer .


<chapterId>6493cf2f-225c-405f-9375-c4304f1087ed</chapterId>


Muri iki gice ca nyuma, turaza gushiramwo ivyiyumviro twize gushika ubu mu ngiro. Ngiye kukwereka ingero z’ibikorwa vy’ukuri vya Bitcoin, kandi uzobwirizwa gukura amakuru ndiko ndagusaba.


Mu vyiza, kugira ngo umuntu akore ivyo vyiyumviro, vyoba vyiza akoresheje igikoresho c’umwuga co gusesangura uruhererekane. Ariko kuva abaremye Samourai Wallet bafashwe, igikoresho conyene co gusesangura ku buntu OXT.me ntikigihari. Tuzohitamwo rero Block explorer ya kera ku bw’ivyo bikorwa. Ndabagira inama yo gukoresha [Mempool.space](https://Mempool.space/) kubera ibiranga vyinshi n’urutonde rw’ibikoresho vyo gusesangura uruhererekane, ariko ushobora kandi guhitamwo uwundi mushakashatsi nka [Bitcoin Explorer](https://bitcoinexplorer.org/).


Kugira ntangire, nzobamenyesha imyimenyerezo. Koresha urupapuro rwawe rwa Block explorer kugira ngo uzizuze, hanyuma wandike inyishu zawe ku mpapuro. Hanyuma, mu mpera z’iki gice, nzobaha inyishu kugira ngo mushobore kugenzura no gukosora ivyo mwabonye.


*Imigenderanire yatowe muri ivyo bikorwa yatowe gusa kubera ibiranga mu buryo bumwe bumwe butari bwo. Iki gice kigenewe kwigisha no gutanga amakuru gusa. Ndashaka gusobanura neza ko ntashigikiye canke ngo ndemeshe gukoresha ivyo bikoresho mu ntumbero mbi. Intumbero ni ukukwigisha ingene wokwikingira gusesangura imirongo, atari ugusesangura kugira ngo ushire ahabona amakuru y’ibanga y’abandi.*


### Imyimenyerezo ya 1


Indangamuntu y'ugucuruza gusuzumwa:


```plaintext
3769d3b124e47ef4ffb5b52d11df64b0a3f0b82bb10fd6b98c0fd5111789bef7
```


Izina ry’ico kigereranyo c’iyi nzira y’ugucuruza ni irihe, kandi ni insobanuro izihe zishobora gutorwa mu gusuzuma gusa ikigereranyo caco, ni ukuvuga imiterere y’iyi nzira?


### Imyimenyerezo ya 2


Indangamuntu y'ubucuruzi buzosuzumwa:


```plaintext
baa228f6859ca63e6b8eea24ffad7e871713749d693ebd85343859173b8d5c20
```


Izina ry’ico kigereranyo c’iyi nzira y’ugucuruza ni irihe, kandi ni insobanuro izihe zishobora gutorwa mu gusuzuma gusa ikigereranyo caco, ni ukuvuga imiterere y’iyi nzira?


### Imyimenyerezo ya 3


Indangamuntu y'ugucuruza gusuzumwa:


```plaintext
3a9eb9ccc3517cc25d1860924c66109262a4b68f4ed2d847f079b084da0cd32b
```


None iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ni iyihe nzira?


Amaze kumenya akarorero kayo, akoresheje ubuhinga bwo mu mutima bw’ugucuruza, ni igiki gishobora guserukira iyo mpinduka?


### Imyimenyerezo ya 4


Indangamuntu y'ugucuruza gusuzumwa:


```plaintext
35f0b31c05503ebfdf7311df47f68a048e992e5cf4c97ec34aa2833cc0122a12
```


None iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ni iyihe nzira?


Amaze kumenya ivyerekanwa vyayo, akoresheje ubuhinga bwo mu mutima bw’ugucuruza, ni igiki Exchange ishobora guserukira?


### Imyimenyerezo ya 5


Reka twiyumvire ko Loïc yashize imwe mu nzira ziwe zo kwakira Bitcoin ku rubuga rwa Twitter:


![BTC204](assets/rn/065.webp)


```plaintext
bc1qja0hycrv7g9ww00jcqanhfpqmzx7luqalum3vu
```


Hashingiwe kuri ayo makuru no gukoresha **ubuhinga bwo gusubira gukoresha Address gusa**, ni ibihe bikorwa vya Bitcoin bishobora guhuzwa n’akaranga ka Loïc?


*Biragaragara ko ntari nyen'iyi reception Address vy'ukuri kandi sinayishize ku mbuga ngurukanabumenyi. Ni Address nafashe mu buryo bw'impfagusa muri Blockchain*


### Imyimenyerezo ya 6


Kubera umwimenyerezo wa 5, kubera ubuhinga bwo gusubira gukoresha Address, warashoboye kumenya amafaranga menshi ya Bitcoin Loïc asa n’uwurimwo. Mu bisanzwe, mu bikorwa vyamenyekanye, wari ukwiye kubona iki:


```plaintext
2d9575553c99578268ffba49a1b2adc3b85a29926728bd0280703a04d051eace
```


Iryo soko ni ryo rya mbere ryohereje amahera kuri Address ya Loïc. None mubona ama bitcoins Loïc yaronse biciye muri iyo transaction yava hehe?


### Imyimenyerezo ya 7


Kubera umwimenyerezo wa 5, kubera ubuhinga bwo gusubira gukoresha Address, warashoboye kumenya amafaranga menshi ya Bitcoin Loïc asa n’uwurimwo. None rero ushaka kumenya aho Loïc yava. Hashingiwe ku bikorwa vyabonetse, nukore isesengura ry’isaha kugira uronke isaha ishobora kuba ikoreshwa cane na Loïc. Uhereye kuri iyo saha, menya ahantu Loïc asa n’uwuba (igihugu, intara/akarere, igisagara...).


![BTC204](assets/rn/066.webp)


### Imyimenyerezo ya 8


Aha niho hari igikorwa ca Bitcoin co kwiga:


```plaintext
bb346dae645d09d32ed6eca1391d2ee97c57e11b4c31ae4325bcffdec40afd4f
```


Turavye iyo nzira yo gucuruza gusa, ni amakuru ayahe twoshobora gusobanura?


### Inyishu z'imyimenyerezo


***Imyimenyerezo ya 1:***


Icogereranyo c’ivyo bikorwa ni icogereranyo c’ukwishura gisanzwe. Twize gusa imiterere yayo, turashobora gusobanura ko igisohoka kimwe kigereranya ihinduka, ikindi gisohoka kigereranya ukwishyura nyakuri. Turazi rero ko uwukoresha yihwejwe kumbure atagifise imwe muri izo UTXO zibiri ziri mu vyo gusohora (izo kwishura), ariko akaba agifise iyindi UTXO (iyo y’ihinduka).


***Imyimenyerezo ya 2:***


Icogereranyo c’ivyo bikorwa ni ico gukoresha amahera mu migwi. Ico kigereranyo kumbure kigaragaza igikorwa c’ubutunzi kinini, nk’urubuga rwa Exchange. Turashobora gufata ingingo y’uko inyungu UTXO iva mw’ishirahamwe rifise ibikorwa vy’ubutunzi vy’agaciro kanini, kandi ko UTXO zisohoka zizosanzazwa. Bimwe bizoba ari ivy’abaguzi b’amashirahamwe bakuye ama bitcoins yabo mu bipapuro vy’amahera vy’ukwibika. Abandi boshobora kuja mu mashirahamwe bafatanya. Ubwa nyuma, nta gukeka ko hazoba ihinduka rizosubira ku sosiyete yatanze iyo mpapuro.


***Imyimenyerezo ya 3:***


Icogereranyo c’ivyo bikorwa ni ukwishura mu buryo bworoshe. Turashobora rero gukoresha ubuhinga bwo mu mutima ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kugira ngo tugerageze kumenya ihinduka.


Nanje ubwanje narabonye n’imiburiburi ubuhinga bubiri bwo mu mutima bushigikira iciyumviro kimwe:




- Gusubira gukoresha ubwoko bumwe bw’inyandiko;
- Igisohoka kinini kuruta ibindi vyose.


Ivyiyumviro bigaragara cane ni ivyo gusubira gukoresha ubwoko bumwe bw’inyandiko. Nkako, igisohoka `0` ni `P2SH`, kimenyekana ku kwakira kwaco Address gutangura na `3`:


```plaintext
3Lcdauq6eqCWwQ3UzgNb4cu9bs88sz3mKD
```


Mugihe igisohoka `1` ari `P2WPKH`, kimenyekana na Address yayo itangura na `bc1q`:


```plaintext
bc1qya6sw6sta0mfr698n9jpd3j3nrkltdtwvelywa
```


UTXO ikoreshwa nk'injiza muri iyi nzira nayo ikoresha inyandiko `P2WPKH`:


```plaintext
bc1qyfuytw8pcvg5vx37kkgwjspg73rpt56l5mx89k
```


Gutyo, turashobora kwiyumvira ko igisohoka `0` gihuye n'ukwishura kandi igisohoka `1` ni ihinduka ry'ibikorwa, ivyo vyoba bisobanura ko umukoresha w'inyungu yama afise igisohoka `1`.


Kugira ngo dushigikire canke tuhakane ico ciyumviro, turashobora kurondera izindi nzira zishobora kwemeza ivyiyumviro vyacu, canke zigabanura ubushobozi bw’uko iciyumviro cacu ari ukuri.


Nabonye n’imiburiburi uwundi murongo umwe w’ivy’ubuhinga. Ni umusaruro munini kuruta iyindi yose. Igisohoka `0` gipima `123.689 Sats`, mu gihe igisohoka `1` gipima `505.839 Sats`. Hari rero itandukaniro rikomeye hagati y’ivyo bivako bibiri. Igisubizo kinini cane heuristic kivuga ko igisubizo kinini cane gishobora kuba ari co gihinduka. Iryo heuristic rirushiriza gukomeza iciyumviro cacu ca mbere.


Bisa rero n'uko uwukoresha yatanze UTXO nk'inyungu agifise `1` output, isa n'iyirimwo ihinduka ry'ugucuruza.


***Imyimenyerezo ya 4:***


Icogereranyo c’ivyo bikorwa ni ukwishura mu buryo bworoshe. Turashobora rero gukoresha ubuhinga bwo mu mutima ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kugira ngo tugerageze kumenya ihinduka.


Nanje ubwanje narabonye n’imiburiburi ubuhinga bubiri bwo mu mutima bushigikira iciyumviro kimwe:




- Gusubira gukoresha ubwoko bumwe bw’inyandiko;
- Igisohoka c’iposita y’uruziga.


Ivyiyumviro bigaragara cane ni ivyo gusubira gukoresha ubwoko bumwe bw’inyandiko. Nkako, igisohoka `0` ni `P2SH`, kimenyekana ku kwakira kwaco Address gutangura na `3`:


```plaintext
3FSH5Mnq6S5FyQoKR9Yjakk3X4KCGxeaD4
```


Mugihe igisohoka `1` ari `P2WPKH`, kimenyekana na Address yayo itangura na `bc1q`:


```plaintext
bc1qvdywdcfsyavt4v8uxmmrdt6meu4vgeg439n7sg
```


UTXO ikoreshwa nk'injiza muri iyi nzira nayo ikoresha inyandiko `P2WPKH`:


```plaintext
bc1qku3f2y294h3ks5eusv63dslcua2xnlzxx0k6kp
```


Gutyo, turashobora kwiyumvira ko igisohoka `0` gihuye n'ukwishura kandi igisohoka `1` ni ihinduka ry'ibikorwa, ivyo vyoba bisobanura ko umukoresha w'inyungu yama afise igisohoka `1`.


Kugira ngo dushigikire canke tuhakane ico ciyumviro, turashobora kurondera izindi nzira zishobora kwemeza ivyiyumviro vyacu, canke zigabanura ubushobozi bw’uko iciyumviro cacu ari ukuri.


Nabonye n’imiburiburi uwundi murongo umwe w’ivy’ubuhinga. Ni igisohoka c’umubare w’uruziga. Igisohoka `0` gipima `70.000 Sats`, mu gihe igisohoka `1` gipima `22.962 Sats`. Turafise rero igisubizo gikikuje neza mu gice ca konti ca BTC. Ivyo bimenyetso vyerekana ko UTXO ifise amahera azunguruka ari yo yo kwishura, kandi ko mu gukuraho, uwundi aserukira ihinduka. Iryo heuristic rirushiriza gukomeza iciyumviro cacu ca mbere.


Ariko rero, muri aka karorero, uwundi murongo w’ubuhinga woshobora gutera umugere ivyiyumviro vyacu vya mbere. Nkako, igisohoka `0` ni kinini kuruta igisohoka `1`. Hashingiwe ku ciyumviro c'uko igisubizo kinini cane ari co gihinduka, twoshobora gufata ko igisubizo `0` ari co gihinduka. Ariko rero, iyo nkuru y’ugusubiza inyuma isa n’iyidashobora kwemerwa, kuko izindi nzira zibiri zisa n’izijijura cane kuruta nzira nini kuruta izindi zo gutanga umusaruro. Ku bw’ivyo, bisa n’ibibereye kuguma dufise iciyumviro cacu ca mbere naho ivyo bisa n’ibivuguruzanya.


Bisa rero n'uko uwukoresha yatanze UTXO nk'inyungu agifise `1` output, isa n'iyirimwo ihinduka ry'ugucuruza.


***Imyimenyerezo ya 5:***


Turashobora kubona ko amafaranga 8 ashobora gufatanywa n’akaranga ka Loïc. Muri ivyo, 4 birimwo kwakira amafaranga y’ibiceri:


```plaintext
2d9575553c99578268ffba49a1b2adc3b85a29926728bd0280703a04d051eace
8b70bd322e6118b8a002dbdb731d16b59c4a729c2379af376ae230cf8cdde0dd
d5864ea93e7a8db9d3fb113651d2131567e284e868021e114a67c3f5fb616ac4
bc4dcf2200c88ac1f976b8c9018ce70f9007e949435841fc5681fd33308dd762
```


Ibindi 4 vyerekeye ivyoherezwa vya Bitcoin:


```plaintext
8b52fe3c2cf8bef60828399d1c776c0e9e99e7aaeeff721fff70f4b68145d540
c12499e9a865b9e920012e39b4b9867ea821e44c047d022ebb5c9113f2910ed6
a6dbebebca119af3d05c0196b76f80fdbf78f20368ebef1b7fd3476d0814517d
3aeb7ce02c35eaecccc0a97a771d92c3e65e86bedff42a8185edd12ce89d89cc
```


***Imyimenyerezo ya 6:***


Turavye akarorero k’iyi nzira, biragaragara ko ari amafaranga akoreshwa hamwe. Nkako, iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ifise ikintu kimwe co kwinjiza n’ivyo gusohora 51, ivyo bikaba vyerekana ko igikorwa c’ubutunzi kiri ku rugero rwo hejuru. Turashobora rero kwiyumvira ko Loïc yakuye ama bitcoins ku rubuga rwa Exchange.


Hari ibintu vyinshi bikomeza iyo nyiyumvo. Ica mbere, ubwoko bw’inyandiko ikoreshwa mu gukingira injiza ya UTXO ni inyandiko ya P2SH 2/3 Multisig, yerekana urugero rwo hejuru rw’umutekano rusanzwe ku bikoresho vya Exchange:


```plaintext
OP_PUSHNUM_2
OP_PUSHBYTES_33 03eae02975918af86577e1d8a257773118fd6ceaf43f1a543a4a04a410e9af4a59
OP_PUSHBYTES_33 03ba37b6c04aaf7099edc389e22eeb5eae643ce0ab89ac5afa4fb934f575f24b4e
OP_PUSHBYTES_33 03d95ef2dc0749859929f3ed4aa5668c7a95baa47133d3abec25896411321d2d2d
OP_PUSHNUM_3
OP_CHECKMULTISIG
```


Ikindi, Address yize `3PUv9tQMSDCEPSMsYSopA5wDW86pwRFbNF` isubira gukoreshwa mu bikorwa bitandukanye birenga 220.000, ivyo bikaba akenshi biranga ama platforms ya Exchange, muri rusangi ataco yitwararika ku bijanye n’ibanga ryayo.


Ivyiyumviro vy’igihe vyakoreshejwe kuri iyi Address na vyo nyene vyerekana ugutangaza amakuru hafi ku musi ku musi mu kiringo c’amezi 3, n’amasaha yagutse arenga amasaha 24, bikaba vyerekana igikorwa gikomeza c’urubuga rwa Exchange.


Ubwa nyuma, ibitabu bikoreshwa n’ico kigo ni vyinshi cane. Address yaronse kandi yohereza 44 BTC mu bikorwa 222.262 hagati y’ukwezi kwa kigarama 2022 n’ukwezi kwa gatatu 2023. Ivyo bitabo vyinshi biremeza kandi uburyo igikorwa c’urubuga rwa Exchange gishobora kuba.


***Imyimenyerezo ya 7:***


Mu gusuzuma ibihe vy’ukwemeza amafaranga, ibihe vya UTC bikurikira birashobora kumenyekana:


```plaintext
05:43
20:51
18:12
17:16
04:28
23:38
07:45
21:55
```


Isesengura ry’izo nzira ryerekana ko UTC-7 na UTC-8 zihuye n’urutonde rw’ibikorwa vy’abantu biriho ubu (hagati ya 08:00 na 23:00) ku nzira nyinshi:


```plaintext
05:43 UTC > 22:43 UTC-7
20:51 UTC > 13:51 UTC-7
18:12 UTC > 11:12 UTC-7
17:16 UTC > 10:16 UTC-7
04:28 UTC > 21:28 UTC-7
23:38 UTC > 16:38 UTC-7
07:45 UTC > 00:45 UTC-7
21:55 UTC > 14:55 UTC-7
05:43 UTC > 21:43 UTC-8
20:51 UTC > 12:51 UTC-8
18:12 UTC > 10:12 UTC-8
17:16 UTC > 09:16 UTC-8
04:28 UTC > 20:28 UTC-8
23:38 UTC > 15:38 UTC-8
07:45 UTC > 23:45 UTC-8
21:55 UTC > 13:55 UTC-8
```


![BTC204](assets/rn/067.webp)


Isaha ya UTC-7 irakenewe cane cane mu ci, kuko irimwo intara n’uturere nka:




- Kaliforuniya (ifise ibisagara nka Los Angeles, San Fransisko na San Diego);
- Nevada (hamwe n’igisagara ca Las Vegas);
- Oregon (hamwe n’igisagara ca Porti);
- Washington (hamwe n’igisagara ca Seattle);
- Akarere ka Canada ka Kolombiya y’Ubwongereza (karimwo ibisagara nka Vancouver na Victoria).


Aya makuru yerekana ko Loïc ashobora kuba aba ku nkengera y’ikiyaga co mu burengero bwa Leta Zunze Ubumwe za Amerika canke Kanada.


***Imyimenyerezo ya 8:***


Isesengura ry’ivyo bikorwa ryerekana ivyinjizwa 5 n’isohoka rimwe, bikaba vyerekana ko hariho ugushira hamwe. Dukoresheje ubuhinga bwa CIOH, turashobora kwiyumvira ko ama UTXO yose yinjira ari ay’ikigo kimwe, kandi ko igisohoka UTXO na co nyene ari ic’ico kigo. Bisa n’uko uwukoresha yahisemwo gukoranya ama UTXO menshi yari afise, kugira ngo akore UTXO imwe mu vyo asohora, afise intumbero yo gukomeza ama UTXO yiwe. Ivyo bishobora kuba vyatumwe n’icipfuzo co kwungukira ku giciro gitoyi c’ugucuruza co muri ico gihe, kugira ngo bagabanye igiciro co muri kazoza.


___


*Kugira ngo ndiko ndandika iki gice ca 3 c'isesengura rya on chain, nakoresheje ibi bikurikira:*




- Urutonde rw'ingingo zine zifise umutwe uvuga ngo: [Gutahura ubuzima bwite bwa Bitcoin na OXT](https://medium.com/oxt-research/gutahura-ubuzima bwite-na-oxt igice-ca-1-4-8177a40a5923), zasohowe na Samou27;
- Raporo zitandukanye zivuye muri **ubushakashatsi bwa OXT**, hamwe n'igikoresho cabo co gusesangura Blockchain ku buntu (ntikigihari muri iki gihe gikurikira ugufatwa kw'abashinze Samourai Wallet);
- Mu buryo bwagutse, ubumenyi bwanje buva ku ma tweets atandukanye n'ibirimwo bivuye kuri [@LaurentMT](https://twitter.com/LaurentMT) na [@ErgoBTC](https://twitter.com/ErgoBTC);
- Ivyo [Space Kek #19] (abamenyeshamakuru b'ibiganiro. [@louneskmt](https://twitter.com/louneskmt), [@TheoPantamis](https://twitter.com/TheoPantamis), [@Sosthene___](https://twitter.com/Sosthene___) na [@LaurentMT](https://twitter.com/LaurentMT).


*Ndashima abanditsi bavyo, ababiteguye n'ababikora. Ndashimira kandi abakosora bakosoye neza ingingo iki gice ca 3 gishingiyeko, bakampa impanuro zabo z’abahinga:*




- [Gilles Cadignan](ku rubuga rwa Twitter);
- [Ludovic Lars](ibara ry'umugera.fr/)


# Kumenya ingendo nziza zo kurinda ubuzima bwite bwawe


<partId>9bd04b63-f1af-4e50-9061-6bc90009df68</partId>


## Address gusubira gukoresha


<chapterId>f3e97645-3df3-41bc-a4ed-d2c740113d96</chapterId>
