Tumaze kwiga ubuhinga bushobora gusenyura ibanga ryawe kuri Bitcoin, muri iki gice ca gatatu ubu turaza kuraba uburyo bwiza bwo gukurikiza kugira ngo wikingire. Intumbero y’iki gice si ugutohoza uburyo bwo gutuma ibanga rigenda neza, ikintu kizokwihwezwa mu nyuma, ahubwo ni ugutahura ingene umuntu yokorana neza na Bitcoin kugira ngo agumane ibanga itanga mu buryo busanzwe, ata gukoresha ubuhinga bwo kwongerako.


Biragaragara ko kugira ngo dutangure iki gice ca gatatu, tuzovuga ku bijanye no gusubira gukoresha Address. Ico kintu ni co gitera ubwoba cane ibanga ry’abakoresha. Nta gukeka ko iki kigabane ari co gihambaye kuruta ibindi vyose.


### Address yakira ni iki?


Bitcoin yakira Address ni urudodo canke ikimenyetso gikoreshwa mu kwakira amafaranga kuri Wallet.


Mu buryo bw'ubuhinga, Bitcoin yakira Address nti "yakira" ama bitcoins mu buryo nyabwo, ahubwo ikoreshwa mu gusobanura ivy'ama bitcoins ashobora gukoreshwamwo. Mu majambo nyayo, iyo urungikiwe amahera, igikorwa c’uwagurungikiye kiguremera UTXO nshasha nk’isohoka rivuye mu ma UTXO yakoresheje nk’ibintu vy’injiza. Kuri iki gisohoka, gishirako inyandiko isobanura ingene iyo UTXO ishobora gukoreshwa mu nyuma. Iyi nyandiko izwi nka "*InyandikoPubKey*" canke "*Inyandiko yo Gufunga*". Ukwakira kwawe Address, canke neza cane umuzigo wayo, uri muri iyo nyandiko. Mu majambo y’abanyabwenge, iki canditswe ahanini kivuga ngo:


> "*Kugira ngo ukoreshe iyi UTXO nshasha, utegerezwa gutanga umukono wa digitale ukoresheje urufunguzo rw'ibanga rujanye n'iyi Address.*"
![BTC204](assets/rn/068.webp)


Amaderesi ya Bitcoin aza mu bwoko butandukanye, bivanye n'uburyo bwo kwandika bukoreshwa. Ivyitegererezo vya mbere, bizwi nka **Iragi**, birimwo aderesi `P2PKH` (**Ishura-ku-Rufunguzo-Hash**) na `P2SH` (**Pay-to-Script-Hash**). Amaderesi ya P2PKH yama atangura na `1`, na P2SH na `3`. Naho izo nzira zikiri zitekanye, ubu ntizikoreshwa, kuko zituma umuntu atanga amahera menshi kandi zikaba zitanga ibanga ritoyi kuruta izo nzira nshasha.


Amaderesi ya SegWit V0 (`P2WPKH` na `P2WSH`) n'aya Taproot / SegWit V1 (`P2TR`) agereranya imiterere y'ubu. Aderesi za SegWit zitangura na `bc1q` na aderesi za Taproot, zashizweho mu 2021, zitangura na `bc1p`.


Nk’akarorero, ng’iyi Taproot y’ukwakira Address:


```text
bc1ps5gd2ys8kllz9alpmcwxqegn7kl3elrpnnlegwkm3xpq2h8da07spxwtf5
```


Uko ScriptPubKey yubatswe bizovana n'urugero uriko urakoresha:


| ScriptPubKey       | Script template                                         |
|--------------------|--------------------------------------------------------|
| P2PKH              | OP_DUP OP_HASH160 `<pubKeyHash>` OP_EQUALVERIFY OP_CHECKSIG |
| P2SH               | OP_HASH160 `<scriptHash>` OP_EQUAL                    |
| P2WPKH             | 0 `<pubKeyHash>`                                      |
| P2WSH              | 0 `<witnessScriptHash>`                               |
| P2SH - P2WPKH      | OP_HASH160 `<redeemScriptHash>` OP_EQUAL              |
| P2SH - P2WSH       | OP_HASH160 `<redeemScriptHash>` OP_EQUAL              |
| P2TR               | 1 `<pubKey>`                                          |


Ubwubatsi bw’amaderesi y’ukwakira na bwo buvana n’akarorero k’inyandiko yatowe:




- Ku ma aderesi `P2PKH` na `P2WPKH`, umuzigo w’inyungu, ni ukuvuga umushinge wa Address, ugereranya Hash y’urufunguzo rwa bose;
- Ku maderesi `P2SH` na `P2WSH`, umuzigo w’inyungu ugereranya Hash ya a;
- Naho ku bijanye n'amaderesi ya `P2TR`, umuzigo ni urufunguzo rwa bose rwahinduwe. Ibisohoka vya P2TR bihuza imice ya _Kwishura-ku-PubKey_ na _Kwishura-ku-Script_. Urufunguzo rwa bose rwahinduwe ni ingaruka yo kwongerako urufunguzo rwa bose rwo gukoresha amahera rwa kera rufise "tweak", ruva kuri Merkle Root y'urutonde rw'inyandiko zishobora kandi gukoreshwa mu gukoresha amahera y'ibiceri.


![BTC204](assets/rn/069.webp)


Amaderesi yerekanwa kuri porogaramu yawe ya Wallet na yo nyene arimwo HRP (*Igice Gisomwa n'Umuntu*), mu bisanzwe `bc` ku maderesi y'inyuma ya SegWit, itandukaniro `1`, n'inomero ya verisiyo `q` ku SegWit V0 na `p` ku Taproot/G1-3. Hariho kandi igitigiri c’ibintu bigenzurwa kugira ngo umuntu yizere ko Address ari nziza kandi ko ari nziza mu gihe co gutanga amakuru.


Ubwa nyuma, aderesi zishirwa mu buryo busanzwe:




- Base58suzuma amaderesi ya kera y'Iragi;
- Bech32 ku bijanye n’amaderesi ya SegWit;
- Bech32m ku bijanye n’amaderesi ya Taproot.


Aha niho hari urutonde rw'inyongezo ry'imiterere ya bech32 na bech32m (SegWit na Taproot) kuva ku rwego rwa 10:


| +  | 0 | 1 | 2 | 3 | 4 | 5 | 6 | 7 |
|----|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 0  | q | p | z | r | y | 9 | x | 8 |
| 8  | g | f | 2 | t | v | d | w | 0 |
| 16 | s | 3 | j | n | 5 | 4 | k | h |
| 24 | c | e | 6 | m | u | a | 7 | l |


### None Address ni iki?


Address gusubira gukoresha ni ugukoresha iyo Address nyene yakira kugira ngo ihagarike UTXO zitandukanye.


Nk’uko twabibonye mu gice ca mbere, UTXO yose irafise ScriptPubKey yayo, iyo na yo ikayifunga kandi itegerezwa guhazwa kugira ngo UTXO ikoreshwe nk’injiza mu bikorwa bishasha. Ni muri iyi ScriptPubKey aho amaderesi y'umuzigo w'inyungu ashirwamwo.


Iyo ScriptPubKeys zitandukanye zirimwo Address imwe, ivyo vyitwa Address gusubira gukoresha. Mu bikorwa, ivyo bisigura ko uwukoresha yasubiyemwo Address imwe nyene ku bayirungitse kugira ngo aronke amafaranga y’ibiceri biciye mu kwishura kenshi. Kandi ni uwo mugenzo nyene utera akaga ku buzima bwawe bw’ibanga.


### Ni kuki Address yosubira gukoresha ari ingorane?


Kubera ko Blockchain ari iya bose, biroroshe kubona aderesi zifunga UTXO n’ama bitcoins angahe. Iyo iyo Address nyene ikoreshejwe mu bikorwa vyinshi, birashoboka ko umuntu afata ingingo y’uko ama bitcoins yose ajanye n’iyo Address ari ay’umuntu umwe. Ivyo bitera ingorane ubuzima bwite bw’abakoresha mu gutuma amahuzu ashobora gushingwa hagati y’ibikorwa bitandukanye n’amahera y’ibiceri bishobora gukurikiranywa kuri Blockchain. Satoshi Nakamoto ubwiwe yaramaze kugaragaza iyo ngorane mu gitabu cera ca Bitcoin:


> *Nk'uruhome rw'umuriro rw'inyongera, urufunguzo rushasha rwoshobora gukoreshwa ku bijanye n'ugucuruza kwose kugira ngo rugume rudahuye n'uwundi muntu rusangi*
![BTC204](assets/rn/070.webp)


Inkomoko: S. Nakamoto, "Bitcoin: Uburyo bwo gutanga amafaranga y'ubuhinga bwa none", 2009.


Intumbero ya Satoshi muri iri rungane ryari iyo guhingura uruhome rw’umuriro rw’inyongera mu gihe hoba hariho isano hagati y’akaranga k’ukoresha n’urufunguzo rubiri kuri Bitcoin, kugira ngo igikorwa ciwe cose ntikihuzwe ku mugaragaro n’akaranga kiwe. Ubu, n'ukwiyongera kw'amashirahamwe y'isesengura rya Blockchain n'amabwirizwa ya KYC, gukoresha amaderesi yihariye ntibikiri "uruhome rw'umuriro rw'inyongera", ahubwo ni umugenzo w'ingenzi ku muntu wese yipfuza kuzigama ubuzima bwite bukeyi.


Iyo usubiye gukoresha Address, uba ugira isano hagati y'ibikorwa vyose bijanye n'iyo Address. Naho ivyo bidatera ingorane amahera yawe ataco uhinduye, nk’uko ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru y’ibanga (elliptic curve cryptography) butanga umutekano w’imfunguruzo zawe z’ibanga, biratuma vyoroha gukurikirana ibikorwa vyawe. Nkako, umuntu wese afise urudodo arashobora kwihweza ibikorwa n’imibare y’amaderesi, ivyo bikaba bishobora gutuma udashobora kumenyekana.


![BTC204](assets/rn/071.webp)


Kugira ngo tubone neza ico ciyumviro, reka dufate akarorero ka Bob, umukoresha akunda kugura ama bitcoins mu giciro gitoyi muri DCA kandi akama ayarungika kuri Address nyene. Inyuma y’imyaka ibiri, iyi Address irimwo amafaranga menshi cane yitwa bitcoins. Iyo Bob ikoresheje iyo Address kugira ngo yishure umudandaza wo mu karere, uwo mucuruzi azoshobora kubona amahera yose ajanye na yo maze akureho ubutunzi bwa Bob. Ivyo bishobora gutuma umuntu agira ingorane z’umutekano wiwe, nk’ukugerageza kwiba canke gufata amahera. Iyo Bob akoresha urupapuro rwa Address rudafise ikintu kugira ngo aronke ikintu cose agura mu bihe bitandukanye, yari guhishurira umudandaza wiwe amakuru make cane ataco amaze.


Mu gusesangura imirongo, hari ubwoko 2 bwo gusubira gukoresha Address:




- Gusubira gukoresha hanze;
- Gusubira gukoresha imbere mu gihe c’ugucuruza.


Ica mbere ni igihe Address isubiye gukoreshwa mu bikorwa vyinshi bitandukanye vya Bitcoin. Ivyo ni vyo twavuganye mbere: iyo heuristic ivuga ko ama UTXO yose yaciye muri iyi Address ari ay’ikigo kimwe.


Gusubira gukoresha Address yo mu mutima ntibishika iyo gusubira gukoresha bibaye mu bikorwa vyinshi, ariko iyo bibaye mu bikorwa bimwe. Nkako, iyo Address nyene ikoreshwa mu gufunga inyungu ikoreshwa nk’isohoka ry’ibikorwa, rero turashobora gufata ingingo y’uko iyo sohoka ikiri iy’uwo mukoresha umwe (ihinduka), kandi ko isohoka rya kabiri rigereranya ukwishyura nyakuri. Iyindi heuristic ituma bishoboka gukomeza urutonde rw’amahera ku bikorwa vyinshi.


![BTC204](assets/rn/072.webp)


Address gusubira gukoresha ni ikiza nyaco kuri Bitcoin. Dushingiye ku rubuga rwa OXT.me (ubu ntirushobora gushikwako), igitigiri cose c’abasubira gukoresha Address kuri Bitcoin cari hafi 52% mu 2022:


![BTC204](assets/rn/073.webp)


Ico kigero ni kinini cane, ariko kiva cane cane ku bikoresho vya Exchange aho kuva ku bakoresha ku giti cabo.


### Ni gute twokwirinda gusubira gukoresha Address?


Kwirinda gusubira gukoresha Address ni vyoroshe cane: **koresha gusa Address nshasha, idafise ikintu ku vyo wishura vyose bishasha kuri Wallet yawe**.


Kubera BIP32, ama wallets y’ubu ubu aragenwa kandi arategekanijwe. Ivyo bisigura ko uwukoresha ashobora generate umubare munini w'amaderesi avuye ku makuru amwe y'intango: seed. Mu kubika ayo makuru amwe, birashoboka ko umuntu asubizaho imfunguruzo zose z’ibanga ziri muri Wallet, ivyo bikaba bituma umuntu ashobora kuronka amahera akingiwe n’amaderesi ahuye.


![BTC204](assets/rn/074.webp)


Ni co gituma, iyo ukanda kuri buto ya "*kwakira*" muri porogarama yawe ya Wallet, Address yakira itakoreshwa irasabwa igihe cose. Amaze kwakira ama bitcoins kuri iyi Address, iyo porogarama ica itanga iciyumviro c’iyindi nshasha.


> *PS: Vuba aha, hariho porogarama za Wallet zatangaje ko zizohagarika gutanga amaderesi ataco avuga, zitinya ko ivyo vyobonwa n’ubutegetsi nk’uburyo bwo gukoresha amahera mu buryo butari bwo. Nimba porogarama yawe ari imwe muri izo, ndaguhanura cane ko woyisubirira ubwo nyene, kuko ivyo ntivyemerwa n’uwuyikoresha.*
Niba ukeneye ikimenyetso kidahinduka kugira ngo ubone amahera, nk’intererano, si vyiza gukoresha Bitcoin Address ya kera kubera ingorane zo gusubira kuyikoresha. Ahubwo, koresha Lightning Address, canke uhitemwo ikimenyetso c’ukwishura ku ruzitiro rudahinduka, nka BIP47 canke Ukwishura mu gacerere. Ivyo bipimo birasigurwa mu buryo burambuye mu gice ca 6 c’iri shure.


## Gushirako ikimenyetso no kugenzura UTXOs


<chapterId>fbdb07cd-c025-48f2-97b0-bd1bc21c68a8</chapterId>



Nk’uko twabibonye mu gice kivuga ku gusesangura imirongo, hariho ubuhinga bwinshi bwo gutahura ibintu n’imirongo bishobora gukoreshwa mu gukuraho amakuru yerekeye igikorwa. Nk’uwukoresha, birahambaye ko umenya ubu buhinga kugira ngo ushobore kubukingira neza.


Ivyo birimwo gucunga neza Wallet yawe mu kwizigama, ivyo bisigura kumenya inkomoko y’ama UTXO yawe, hamwe no guhitamwo neza ama UTXO uzokoresha igihe uriko urishura. Ubu burongozi bwiza bwa Wallet bwishingikiriza ku bintu bibiri bihambaye vy’amasakoshi meza ya Bitcoin: gushiramwo ibimenyetso no kugenzura Coin.


Muri iki gice, turaza kuraba ivyo bikoresho maze turabe ingene wobikoresha mu buryo bw'ubwenge, utaronse akazi kenshi, kugira ngo ukoreshe neza cane ubuzima bwite bwawe kuri Bitcoin.


### Gushirako ikimenyetso ni iki?


Gushirako ikimenyetso ni umugenzo wo gushirako ikimenyetso canke ikimenyetso ku UTXO yihariye muri Bitcoin Wallet. Ivyo bisobanuro bibikwa aho hantu na porogarama ya Wallet kandi ntivyigera birungikwa ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin. Gushirako amazina rero ni igikoresho co kurongora umuntu ku giti ciwe.


Nk'akarorero, nimba mfise UTXO iva kuri P2P naguze kuri Bisq na Charles, noshobora kuyindika "`Bisq Charles atari KYC`".


Gushirako ibimenyetso ni akamenyero keza gafasha kwibuka inkomoko canke aho UTXO igamije kuja, ivyo bikaba rero bituma umuntu ashobora gucunga neza amahera no gutuma ubuzima bwiwe bwite bugenda neza. Nkako, Bitcoin Wallet yawe nta gukeka ko icungera UTXO nyinshi. Nimba inkomoko y'izo UTXO zitandukanye, ushobora kudashaka gufatanya izo UTXO muri kazoza, ahandi ho woshobora guhishura Ownership yabo rusangi. Mu gushiramwo neza UTXO zawe zose, urashobora kwizigira udakeka ko uzokwibuka aho zavuye igihe uzoba ukeneye kuzikoresha, naho vyoba imyaka ikurikira.


### None ubugenzuzi bw’imfuruka ni iki?


Ikoreshwa ry’ibikorwa ry’ugushirako amazina rirushiriza gushimisha iyo rifatanijwe n’uburyo bwo kugenzura Coin kuri porogarama yawe ya Wallet.


Coin control ni ikintu kiboneka muri porogaramu nziza Bitcoin Wallet, kiguha ubushobozi bwo guhitamwo n’amaboko UTXOs zihariye zo gukoresha nk’inyungu kugira ngo urangize igikorwa. Nkako, kugira ngo uhaze amahera y’isohoka, ukeneye gukoresha amahera y’injiza UTXO mu gusubiza. Kubera imvo zitari nke, tuzozirabira mu nyuma, ushobora guhitamwo neza neza ama UTXO uzokoresha nk’ibintu vyo gukoresha kugira ngo uhaze amahera yatanzwe. Ivyo nyene ni vyo ubugenzuzi bwa Coin buguha uburenganzira bwo gukora. Kugira ngo nkuhe ikigereranyo, iki kintu gisa n’uguhitamwo Coin yihariye muri Wallet yawe igihe uriha baguette yawe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/075.webp)


Ikoreshwa rya porogarama ya Wallet ifise ubugenzuzi bwa Coin, hamwe n’ugushirako ikimenyetso ca UTXO, bituma abakoresha bashobora gutandukanya no guhitamwo neza UTXOs ku bikorwa vyabo.


### None UTXO zanyu muzishirako gute?


Nta buryo bumwe bwo gushirako amazina UTXOs. Ni wewe ushobora gusobanura uburyo bwo gushirako amazina yoroshe gutahura kuri Wallet yawe. Uko biri kwose, nuzirikane ko gushirako ikimenyetso ciza ari ugushirako ikimenyetso ushobora gutahura igihe ubikeneye. Nimba Bitcoin Wallet yawe igenewe canecane kuzigama, ivyo bimenyetso vyoshobora kutagufasha mu myaka mirongo izoza. Rero urabe neza ko zitomoye, zitomoye kandi zitomoye.


Ni ngombwa ko abakunzi bawe bashobora kumenya neza aho ayo mahera akomoka nimba umusi umwe bakeneye kuronka igitabu cawe ca Wallet. Ivyo bizobafasha kubera imvo z’ibanga no kubera imvo zijanye n’amategeko, iyo bakeneye gushingira intahe ubuyobozi aho ayo mahera yava.


Ikintu gihambaye cane co kumenya ku rupapuro ni inkomoko ya UTXO. Ushobora gusa kwerekana ingene Coin yaje kuba muri Wallet yawe. Mbega ni ingaruka y’ugugura ku rubuga rwa Exchange? Igiciro ca Invoice kivuye ku mukiriya? Igikoresho c’urunganwe Exchange? Canke vyoba bigereranya uguhinduka kw’amahera akoreshwa? Nk'akarorero, ushobora gusobanura:




- gukuraho Exchange.com`;
- kwishura abakiriya Dawidi`;
- kugura P2P Karoli`;
- `Hindura ugugura sofa`


![BTC204](assets/rn/076.webp)


Kugira ngo utunganye neza uburongozi bwawe bwa UTXO no kwubahiriza ingamba zawe zo gutandukanya amafaranga muri Wallet yawe, woshobora gutunganya ibimenyetso vyawe n’ikimenyetso c’inyongera kigaragaza ivyo gutandukanya. Nimba Wallet yawe irimwo ivyiciro bibiri vya UTXO ushaka cane kudavanga, woshobora gushiramwo ikimenyetso mu bimenyetso vyawe kugira ngo ushobore gutandukanya neza iyo migwi. Ivyo bimenyetso vyo gutandukanya bizovana n’ingingo zawe bwite, nk’ugutandukanya hagati y’ama UTXO ava mu nzira y’ugugura irimwo KYC, canke hagati y’amahera y’umwuga n’ay’umuntu ku giti ciwe. Dufashe ingero z’ibimenyetso twavuze haruguru, ivyo vyoshobora guhinduka:




- `KYC - Gukuraho Exchange.com`;
- `KYC - Ukwishura kw'abaguzi Dawidi`;
- `NTA KYC - Gura P2P Karoli`;
- `NTA KYC - Hindura ugugura sofa`


![BTC204](assets/rn/077.webp)


Ni vyiza kandi ko umuntu aguma ashirako ikimenyetso ku UTXO mu gihe c’amafaranga. Nk’akarorero, igihe ushize hamwe UTXO no-KYC, urabe neza ko UTXO ivuyemwo atari gusa `ugushiramwo`, ariko cane cane nk’`ugushiramwo no-KYC` kugira ngo ugume ufise inyandiko igaragara y’aho ivyo biceri vyavuye.


Ubwa nyuma, si ngombwa gushiramwo itariki ku kimenyetso. Porogaramu nyinshi za Wallet zirasanzwe zigaragaza itariki y'ugucuruza, kandi birashoboka kwama ubona aya makuru kuri Block explorer kubera txid yayo.


### Ni gute twohitamwo ama UTXO akwiriye?


Iyo ukora igikorwa, ubugenzuzi bwa Coin buragufasha guhitamwo vyihariye UTXOs zo gukoresha nk’ibintu vyinjizwa kugira ngo uhaze umusaruro w’ukwishyura. Hariho imice ibiri y’iryo hitamwo:




- Ubushobozi bw’uko uwuronka amahera yo guhuza igice c’akaranga kawe n’ama UTXO akoreshwa mu vyo kwinjiza;
- Ubushobozi bw’umugenzuzi wo hanze bwo gushinga amasano hagati y’ama UTXO yose akoreshwa nk’ibintu vy’injiza.


Kugira ngo dusobanure iciyumviro ca mbere, reka dufate akarorero nyako. Twibaze ko ugura umukate mu bitcoins ku mutetsi wawe. Ukoresha UTXO imwe canke nyinshi ufise nk’ibintu vy’injiza kugira ngo ushikire n’imiburiburi igiciro ca baguette mu bisohoka, hamwe n’amahera y’ugucuruza. Umutetsi wawe yoshobora rero gufatanya mu maso hawe, canke ikindi gice cose c’akaranga kawe azi, n’ibiceri bikoreshwa nk’ibintu vy’injiza. Kubera ko uzi ko iyo nzira iriho, woshobora guhitamwo UTXO yihariye aho guhitamwo iyindi igihe uriha.


![BTC204](assets/rn/078.webp)


Nk’akarorero, nimba imwe mu UTXO zawe iva ku rubuga rwa Exchange kandi ukaba ushaka ko umutetsi w’imikate atamenya ivyerekeye konti yawe kuri iyo rubuga, uzokwirinda gukoresha iyo UTXO kugira ngo wishyure. Niba ufise UTXO y’agaciro kanini yerekana amafaranga menshi cane, woshobora kandi guhitamwo kutayikoresha kugira ngo umutetsi ntamenye ubutunzi bwawe bwa BTC.


Guhitamwo UTXOs zo gukoresha kuri iyi ngingo ya mbere rero ni ingingo y’umuntu ku giti ciwe, ishingiye ku vyo wipfuza guhishura canke udashaka guhishura. Ivyo bimenyetso ushira ku ma UTXO yawe iyo uyakiriye bizokufasha guhitamwo ivyo, iyo umaze kubikoresha, bigaragaza gusa amakuru ushobora guhishurira uwuyakira.


Uretse amakuru ashobora guhishurirwa uwuyakira, uguhitamwo ivyo winjiza biragira ico bikoze ku vyo uhishurira abarorerezi bose ba Blockchain. Nkako, ukoresheje UTXO nyinshi nk’ibintu vyinjizwa mu gucuruza kwawe, uhishura ko ari ivy’ikigo kimwe, hakurikijwe ubuhinga bwa CIOH (_Common Input Ownership Heuristic_).


![BTC204](assets/rn/079.webp)


Igihe uhitamwo ama UTXO yawe rero, urakeneye kumenya ko igikorwa ugiye gutangaza kizotuma habaho ihuriro hagati y’ama UTXO yose akoreshwa. Iryo huriro rishobora kuba ingorane ku buzima bwawe bwite, cane cane iyo UTXOs zivuye mu bibanza bitandukanye.


![BTC204](assets/rn/080.webp)


Reka dufate akarorero k’iyi UTXO yanje idafise KYC iva muri Bisq; Nshaka kwirinda kubifatanya na UTXO iva, tuvuge, ku rubuga rwa Exchange rutegekanijwe ruzi akaranga kanje. Nkako, nivyashika nkoresheje izo UTXO 2 nk’ibintu vyinjizwa mu gikorwa kimwe, urubuga rutegekanijwe ruzoshobora guhuza akaranga kanje na UTXO naguze kuri Bisq, iyo mbere itari ifatanijwe n’akaranga kanje.


![BTC204](assets/rn/081.webp)


Ubwa nyuma, iyo uhisemwo UTXO zo gukoresha nk’inyungu mu gucuruza, ikintu gihambaye cane ni ukwirinda gukoresha UTXO nyinshi. Ivyinshi, iyo ushoboye, nuhitemwo Coin imwe nini bihagije kugira ngo uhaze ivyo uriha. Muri ubwo buryo, ukirinda rwose ingorane zijanye n’ugukoresha CIOH. Ariko rero, nimba ata UTXO imwe ihagije kugira ngo umuntu yishure kandi ukeneye gukoresha nyinshi, urabe neza ko ziva mu bibanza bisa n’ivyo kugira ngo ugabanye ingorane zo guhuza abantu udashaka. Kandi uzirikane ko uwuronka amakuru yoshobora gufatanya amakuru afise kuri wewe n’amateka y’ibiceri vyakoreshejwe mu gushiramwo ibintu.


### Gutahura uguhitamwo kwa UTXO


Mu bice vyabanje, twavuganye ku guhitamwo n’amaboko ama UTXO azokoreshwa mu gucuruza. Ariko none bigenda gute iyo porogarama ya Wallet ikoze ivyo guhitamwo ubwo nyene? Hari uburyo bwinshi bwo kumenya ibiceri vyo gukoresha, kandi guhitamwo UTXOs ni ikintu nyaco co gukora ubushakashatsi kuri Bitcoin. Intumbero ihambaye y’iyi nzira yikora kenshi ni ugugabanya amafaranga y’ugucuruza ku muntu akoresha.


Uburyo bwo guhitamwo UTXO nka FIFO (*Ubwa mbere Mu Mbere Gusohoka*) na LIFO (*Ubwa nyuma Mu Mbere Gusohoka*) ni bumwe mu buryo bworoshe, ariko kandi burakora neza cane. Na FIFO, UTXO za kera cane ziri muri Wallet ni zo zikoreshwa ubwa mbere. Ubwo buryo muri rusangi ntibukora neza mu kugabanya amafaranga y’ugucuruza no mu kuzigama ibanga, kiretse mu bihe aho hakoreshwa amasaha y’igihe kandi akeneye gusubirwamwo ubudasiba. Ku rundi ruhande, LIFO ishira imbere gukoresha ama UTXO aheruka cane. Ubwo buryo bwompi, naho bworoshe, akenshi buragaragara ko ata co bumaze.


Uburyo buteye imbere cane ni *Umutorera umuti w'Isakoshi*. Ivyo vyakoreshejwe kuri Bitcoin core Wallet gushika kuri verisiyo 0.17. Bigizwe no guhitamwo mu buryo busubiramwo kandi mu buryo butandukanye UTXOs muri Wallet, ukazishira mu bice bitobito, no kugumiza umuti ugabanya uburemere bw’ugucuruza uko bishoboka kwose, kugira ngo ugabanye igiciro ku wukoresha.


*Ishami-n'Imbohe* (BNB), akenshi yitwa "Murch algorithm" inyuma y'uwayihinguye, yasubiriye *Igisubizo c'Isakoshi* muri Bitcoin core kuva kuri verisiyo 0.17. Ubwo buryo buteye imbere cane bufise intumbero yo kurondera umugwi w'ama UTXO ahuye neza n'amahera akenewe kugira ngo umuntu ahaze ivyiza biva mu gucuruza. Intumbero ya BNB ni ugugabanya amafaranga y'ihinduka hamwe n'amahera, mu kugabanya ivyo bita ikigereranyo c'imyanda, kikaba gifata mu muzirikanyi amafaranga y'ubu nyene n'amafaranga yitezwe muri kazoza y'ivyo bikoresho vya Exchange. Ubu buryo buva ku ciyumviro c'intango c'*Ishami-n'Igihugu*, cavuzwe mu 1960 na Ailsa Land na Alison Harcourt, kandi butanga ugutunganya neza ama


Ubu buryo bwose bwo guhitamwo UTXO bwikora burashobora kuba bwiza mu kugabanya amahera y’ugucuruza, ariko kenshi ntibugira ico bukoze mu kuzigama ibanga ry’abakoresha. Nkako, izo algorithme zishobora gufatanya UTXO nyinshi mu vyo kwinjiza, gutyo zigahishura umutungo rusangi w’izo UTXO kubera CIOH. Biragaragara ko ubwo buryo butashobora kwitwararika ibimenyetso bishirwa ku ma UTXO, naho biri ukwo bikaba ari ngirakamaro mu guhitamwo neza ama UTXO yo guhishurira uwuronka amafaranga. Muri iki gihe, uburyo bumwe rudende bwo gutuma ibanga riguma ryiza igihe uhitamwo ibiceri ni ukubigira n’amaboko.


### Inyigisho ku gushirako ikimenyetso UTXO


Niba wifuza kumenya ingene woshirako amazina y'ama UTXO yawe, twakoze inyigisho yuzuye ku bijanye n'ubuhinga nyamukuru bwa Bitcoin Wallet hanze:


https://planb.network/tutorials/privacy/on-chain/utxo-labelling-d997f80f-8a96-45b5-8a4e-a3e1b7788c52

## KYC n'ikimenyetso c'urufunguzo


<chapterId>cec6b9d9-0eed-4f85-bc4e-1e9aa59ca605</chapterId>



KYC bisobanura "Menya umukiriya wawe". Ni uburyo bwo gutegeka bushirwa mu ngiro n’amashirahamwe amwe amwe akora mu rwego rwa Bitcoin. Intumbero y’iyi nzira ni ugusuzuma no kwandika akaranga k’abaguzi babo, n’intumbero yavuzwe yo kurwanya ugukoresha nabi amahera no gufasha iterabwoba.


Mu majambo y’ingirakamaro, KYC irimwo gukusanya amakuru atandukanye y’umuntu ku giti ciwe ku mukiriya, ashobora guhinduka bivanye n’ububasha, ariko muri rusangi harimwo indangamuntu, ifoto n’ikimenyamenya ca Address. Aya makuru araheza akagenzurwa maze akabikwa kugira ngo azokoreshwe muri kazoza.


Ubwo buryo bwacitse itegeko ku bikoresho vyose vy’ubuhinga bwa Exchange bitegekanijwe mu bihugu vyinshi vyo mu Burengero. Ivyo bisigura ko umuntu wese yipfuza Exchange amafaranga y’igihugu ku Bitcoin biciye kuri izo nzira ategerezwa kwubahiriza ibisabwa na KYC.


Ubwo buryo ntibutagira ingorane ku buzima bwite n’umutekano w’abakoresha. Muri iki gice, tuzosuzuma ivyo bibazo mu buryo burambuye kandi dusuzume ingaruka zidasanzwe za KYC n’imigenderanire yo kumenya umuntu ku buzima bwite bw’abakoresha Bitcoin.


### Gufasha gukurikirana onchain


Ico kibazo ca mbere gifitaniye isano na KYC ni uko itanga inzira y’agaciro yo kwinjira mu gusesangura Blockchain. Nk’uko twabibonye mu gice ca mbere, abasesangura barashobora gukoranya no gukurikirana ibikorwa kuri Blockchain bakoresheje uburyo bwo gukorana n’ubuhinga bwo kumenya ibintu. Bamaze kuroranirwa mu gukoranya igikorwa c’umukoresha onchain, ico bakeneye gukora n’ukurondera ahantu hamwe ho kwinjira mu bikorwa vyiwe vyose n’imfunguruzo kugira ngo bashobore guhungabanya ibanga ryiwe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/082.webp)


Iyo ukoze KYC, utanga ikibanza co kwinjiramwo c’agaciro kanini co gusesangura Blockchain, uko ufatanya amaderesi yawe yo kwakira akoreshwa igihe ukura amafaranga yawe y’ibiceri ku rubuga rwa Exchange n’akaranga kawe kuzuye, kagenzuwe. Mu vy’ukuri, ayo makuru amenyekana gusa n’ishirahamwe wayatanze, ariko nk’uko tuzobibona aha hepfo, ingorane yo gusohoka kw’amakuru ni nyayo. Ikindi kandi, kuba gusa ishirahamwe rifise ayo makuru birashobora gutera ingorane, naho boba batayasangiza abandi.


Rero, iyo udateye izindi ntambwe zo kugabanya ugukoranya ibikorwa vyawe kuri Blockchain, umuntu wese afise ubumenyi ku bijanye n’iyi nzira yo kwinjira muri KYC arashobora guhuza ibikorwa vyawe vyose kuri Bitcoin n’akaranga kawe. Uvuye ku mbonerahamwe y’iyo sosiyete, gukoresha kwawe Bitcoin biratakaza ibanga ryose.


![BTC204](assets/rn/083.webp)


Kugira ivyo tubigereranye n’ukugereranya, ni nk’aho umukozi wawe wo muri banki ya *Bank X* atari afise uburenganzira bwo kubona amafaranga yose ukoresha muri *Bank X* gusa, ariko kandi yari gushobora kwihweza amafaranga yose ukoresha muri *Bank Y* n’amafaranga yose ukoresha mu mafaranga.


Ibuka kuva mu gice ca mbere c’iri shure: Igishushanyo c’ibanga ca Bitcoin, nk’uko catekerejwe na Satoshi Nakamoto, gishingiye ku gutandukanya akaranga k’uwukoresha n’ababiri b’ingenzi ziwe. Naho iyo Layer y’ibanga itagihagije muri iki gihe, biracari vyiza ko umuntu agabanya ukuntu yononekaye uko bishoboka kwose.


### Gushikirwa n'ubugenzuzi bwa Leta


Ikibazo ca kabiri gikomeye kiri muri KYC ni uko ihishurira Leta ko wari ufise Bitcoin mu gihe kanaka. Iyo uguze bitcoins biciye ku mukinyi ategekanijwe, birashoboka ko Leta imenya ivy’ivyo bintu. Muri iki gihe, ivyo bishobora gusa n'ibidahambaye, ariko birahambaye kwibuka ko kazoza k'igihugu cawe mu vya politike n'ubutunzi katari mu maboko yawe.


Ica mbere, Leta irashobora kwihuta gufata ingingo y’ubutegetsi bw’agahomerabunwa. Amateka yuzuye ingero aho amategeko yahindutse bukwi na bukwi. Ubu, mu Buraya, aba Bitcoiners barashobora kwandika ingingo zivuga kuri Bitcoin, bagafata uruhara mu nama, bagacungera amasakoshi yabo mu kwizigama. Ariko none, ni nde yovuga ico ejo azoba? Iyo Bitcoin ihindutse umwansi wa bose mu kanya nk’ako gukubita, kuyifatanya na yo mu madosiye ya leta vyoshobora kuba ingorane.


Hanyuma, mu gihe habaye ingorane zikomeye z’ubutunzi, Leta yoshobora kwiyumvira gufata ama bitcoins afiswe n’abanyagihugu. Kumbure ejo, aba bitcoiners bazobonwa nk’abaronka inyungu mu bihe vy’amagorwa, kandi bazokorwako imisoro irenze urugero kubera inyungu zabo z’umutungo kamere mu gihe amafaranga y’ama fiat azoba ariko aragabanuka.


Ushobora kwibaza ko ivyo atari ikibazo, kuko ama bitcoins yawe aravanze, rero ntashobora gukurikirana. Ariko rero, gukurikirana si co kibazo kiri aha. Ikibazo nyaco ni uko Leta izi ko ufise Bitcoin. Aya makuru yonyene yoshobora kuba ahagije kugira ngo akugire icaha canke akugire ico ubazwa. Woshobora kugerageza kwivugira ko wakoresheje amahera yawe ya bitcoins, ariko ivyo vyobwirizwa kugaragara mu mpapuro zawe z’ikori, maze ugafatwa. Ushobora kandi kuvuga ko watakaje imfunguruzo zawe mu mpanuka y’ubwato, ariko uretse iyo nkuru y’agatwengo yo kuri Twitter, vy’ukuri wibaza ko ivyo vyoba bihagije kugira ngo urekure?


Ni ngombwa rero ko uzirikana ingorane za Leta kumenya ko ufise BTC, naho iyo ngorane yoba isa n’iyi kure gute uno musi.


Ikindi kibazo giterwa na KYC mu bijanye n’ukugenzura kwa Leta ni ugutanga raporo ku nguvu n’amashirahamwe ategekanijwe. Naho ntazi neza amategeko yo mu bindi bihugu, mu Bufaransa, *Prestataires de Services sur Actifs Numériques* (PSAN) zitegerezwa kumenyesha abajejwe kugenzura ivy’amahera iyo amahera yose abona ko ari ay’amakenga.


Mu Bufaransa mu mwaka w’2023, ibikorwa 1.449 biteye amakenga vyatangajwe n’aba PSAN. Kugeza ubu, vyinshi muri ivyo bikorwa bifitaniye isano n’ubugizi bwa nabi. Ariko kandi, abategetsi bariko barasaba amashirahamwe agengwa gutanga raporo ku bikorwa vyose biteye amakenga vy’ubuhinga bwa Bitcoin bishingiye gusa ku mibumbe yavyo. Iyo ukoze igikorwa co gukorana n’abandi, canke mbere igikorwa gusa gifise uburyo budasanzwe gatoyi, kandi ico gikorwa kikaba kitari kure y’ugukura ama Bitcoins yawe kuri izo nzira, woshobora kwisanga umenyeshejwe abategetsi. Naho ata bikorwa bibi vyakozwe kandi uburenganzira bwawe bukaba bukoreshwa mu buryo bubereye, mwene ukwo gutanga raporo kwoshobora gutuma habaho ugusuzuma n’ugucungera, ivyo bikaba ari ingorane wari kwirinda iyo utagira KYC.


### Ivyago vyo gusohoka kw'amakuru y'ibanga


Ikindi kibazo kiri muri KYC ni uko isaba ko amakuru yawe yose abikwa kuri servers z’ishirahamwe ry’abikorera ku giti cabo.


Ivyabaye vuba vyatwibukije ko ata n’umwe adashobora gushikirwa n’ingorane z’amahera canke z’ubuhinga bwa none. Muri 2022, abakiriya ba Celsius barashikiwe n'ingaruka. Inyuma y’aho iyo sosiyete ipfuye, amazina y’abayifitiye umwenda n’ingero y’itunga ryabo vyamenyeshejwe n’inkiko za Amerika mu gihe c’urubanza rw’ubutegetsi.


Haciye imyaka irenga ibiri gusa, yari igisagara gihambaye mu bijanye n’umutekano wo kuri internet w’amahera y’ibanga (cryptocurrency) cabonye amakuru y’ibanga y’abaguzi bayo yibwa. Naho ivyo bintu vyabaye bitajanye n’ugugura amafaranga y’ama bitcoins, mwene iyo ngorane iracariho no ku bikoresho vya Exchange. Hariho rero ingorane zitomoye zijanye n’amakuru y’umuntu ku giti ciwe.


Ni ukuri ko amakuru menshi y’ibanga dusanzwe tuyashira mu masosiyete yigenga. Ariko rero, ingorane iri aha ni zibiri, kuko ayo makuru atakumenya gusa, ariko kandi afitaniye isano n’ibikorwa biri kuri Bitcoin. Nkako, iyo umunyaruyeri aronse uburenganzira bwo gushika ku makuru y’abaguzi bo ku rubuga rwa Exchange, arashobora kwiyumvira ko abo baguzi bafise amafaranga yitwa Bitcoins. Ivyo bitera ingorane zirushirizwa n’uko Bitcoin, cokimwe n’ibindi bintu vyose vy’agaciro, ikwegera abasuma.


Mu gihe amakuru yoba yasohotse, mu vyiza woshobora kuba ari wo ugerageza guhenda abantu. Mu gihe kibi kuruta ibindi vyose, woshobora kwisanga uri hagati y’ibintu bishobora gutera ubwoba inzu yawe ku mubiri.


Uretse ingorane zidasanzwe zijanye n’inyandiko za Bitcoin, hariho kandi ingorane zijanye n’ugutanga inyandiko z’irangamuntu. Nkako, iyo amakuru asohotse, birashoboka ko umuntu yibwa akaranga. Rero ivyo bitera ntibigarukira gusa ku kurinda ibanga ry’amafaranga, ariko kandi birareba umutekano w’umuntu ku giti ciwe.


### Ivyiyumviro bimwebimwe vyerekeye KYC


Ni vyiza gusenyura bimwe mu vyiyumviro vy’imbere y’igihe ku bijanye na KYC dukunda guhura navyo kuri Twitter canke mu guhanahana amakuru hagati y’abakoresha amafaranga y’ama bitcoin.


Mbere na mbere, ntaco bimaze kwiyumvira ko kurinda ubuzima bwite bwawe ku Bitcoins uronka biciye ku KYC ata co bimaze. Ibikoresho n’uburyo bwo gucungera ubuzima bwite biri kuri Bitcoin biratandukanye kandi birafise intumbero zitandukanye. Gukoresha amafaranga y’ubudandaji ya CoinJoin ku ma Bitcoins yaronswe biciye ku KYC, nk’akarorero, si iciyumviro kibi. Ego ni ko, urakeneye kwiyubara ku bijanye n’amaporogarama ya Exchange ategekanijwe kugira ngo wirinde ko konti yawe ihagarara canke ngo ibuzwe, ariko mu bijanye n’ubuhinga bukomeye, ivyo bikorwa ntibihuye. CoinJoin irafise ingaruka zo guca amateka ya Coin, gutyo bikagufasha guhagarika ingorane zimwe zimwe zo gusesangura uruzitiro zijanye n’ivyo KYC ikora. Naho bidakuraho ingorane zose, biraserukira inyungu ikomeye.


![BTC204](assets/rn/084.webp)


Ibanga kuri Bitcoin ntirikwiye kubonwa mu buryo bw'ibice bibiri, nk'itandukaniro hagati y'ibice vy'amahera "bitazwi" n'ibindi bitazwi. Kugira Bitcoins zironswa biciye ku KYC ntibisigura ko vyose vyatakaye; ahubwo gukoresha ibikoresho vyo gucungera ibanga birashobora mbere gutuma umuntu agira akamaro kuruta.


Ku rundi ruhande, kuronka Bitcoin biciye ku buryo butajanye n’ubuhinga bwa KYC ntibiguha ibanga ritagira agasembwa, eka mbere ntibigusonerwa gufata izindi ngingo zo kwikingira. Iyo ufise Bitcoin itari iya KYC ariko ugasubira gukoresha amaderesi y’ukwakira incuro nyinshi, amafaranga yawe yoshobora gukurikirana no gukoranirizwa hamwe. Ihuriro ritoyi n’isi iri hanze ya Bitcoin ryoshobora gutuma Layer yonyene y’ibanga ufise ihungabana. Ni ngombwa rero ko umuntu abona ibikoresho vyose n’uburyo bwo kwongereza ubuzima bwite biri kuri Bitcoin nk’ivyo kwuzuzanya. Ubuhinga bwose buratorera umuti ingorane yihariye kandi burashobora kwongerako Layer y’uburinzi. Rero kugira Bitcoin itari KYC ntibisigura ko udakeneye gufata ibindi bintu vyo kwirinda.


### Mbega KYC yoshobora gukurwaho?


Rimwe na rimwe ndabazwa nimba bishoboka "gusubira inyuma" umaze gukora KYC, kandi nk'uko mushobora kubibona mu ngingo zibanza, inyishu irafise utunenge. Uburyo bworoshe bwo kwirinda ingorane zijanye n’ivyo KYC ikora ni ukutayikoresha igihe uronka ama bitcoins. Tuzorabira kuri iyo nkuru mu buryo burambuye mu kigabane gikurikira. Ariko rero, nimba KYC yaramaze gukorwa kandi bitcoins zikaba zaguzwe, hari uburyo bwo kugabanya ingorane zirimwo?


Ku bijanye n’ingorane zo gukurikirana amafaranga yawe, gukoresha CoinJoin ni umuti. Tuzorabira ubu buryo mu buryo burambuye mu nyuma mu nyigisho, ariko ukwiye kumenya ko CoinJoin ishobora kugufasha guca amateka ya Coin no kuyibuza gukurikirana kahise-ubu n’ubu-kahise. Mbere no ku BTC zironswa biciye ku rubuga rutegekanijwe, ubu buhinga burashobora kubuza ko zishobora gukurikirana.


Ariko rero, CoinJoin ntizimanganya ingorane ya kabiri ijana na KYC: ukuntu Leta ishobora kumenyeshwa ko ufise amafaranga y’ibiceri. Nkako, naho ibiceri vyawe vyoba bitagishobora gukurikirana, Leta, bivanye n’ububasha, ishobora kuronka uburenganzira bwo kuronka amatangazo yawe yo kwimurira ivy’amahera y’amahera. Kubera ko iyo ngorane atari iyo mu vy’ubuhinga, ariko iyo ari iyo mu butegetsi, nta miti yihariye ya Bitcoin yo kuyikuraho, uretse kutavyishira mu nzira ya KYC mu ntango. Uburyo bumwe rudende bushingiye ku mategeko bwo kugabanya iyo ngorane ni ukugurisha ku mbuga zitegekanijwe Bitcoins zawe waronse biciye ku mbuga zitegekanijwe, hanyuma ukazisubira kuzigura biciye ku buryo butagira KYC. Mu kugurisha no kumenyesha ko wimuriwe, abategetsi bakwiye kubona ko utagifise.


Naho ku bijanye n’akaga ko gusohoka kw’amakuru yawe bwite n’inyandiko z’akaranga, ivyo ni akaga kari hanze ya Bitcoin, kandi nta muti w’ubuhinga wo kuvyirinda. Amakuru yawe amaze guhishurirwa, biragoye gusubiramwo igikorwa. Ushobora kugerageza gufunga konti yawe kuri iyo nzira, ariko ivyo ntivyemeza ko amakuru yawe ya KYC azokurwaho, cane cane iyo ugusuzuma akaranga kawe gushikirijwe abandi. Gusuzuma ko amakuru yawe yasimbuwe burundu ntibishoboka. Nta muti rero wo gukingira burundu iyo ngorane no kumenya ko itagihari.


### Itandukaniro hagati ya KYC n'ikimenyetso nyamukuru


Rimwe na rimwe, bamwe mu bakoresha bitcoiners bakunda kwagura ijambo "KYC" ku BTC Exchange iyo ari yo yose irimwo uguhererekanya amahera canke kwishura ku ikarita y'inguzanyo, kuko ubwo buryo bushobora kandi guhishura inkomoko y'ukwishura, nk'uko KYC yobigira. Ariko rero, KYC ntikwiye gutera urujijo n’ikimenyetso c’ingenzi. Ku bijanye n’ivyo jewe ubwanje, ntegerezwa kwemera ko ukuntu mbona iyo nkuru vyahindutse uko igihe cagenda kirarenga.


KYC yerekeza canecane ku buryo bwo gutegeka bushirwa mu ngiro n’amashirahamwe amwe amwe kugira ngo asuzume kandi yandike akaranga k’abaguzi babo. Ni ikintu c’ibice bibiri: iyo uronka ama bitcoins yawe, canke ukora KYC, canke ntubikore. Ariko rero, ikimenyetso c’urufunguzo, kijanye n’ihuriro hagati y’uruhande rw’akaranga k’ukoresha n’igikorwa c’uruzitiro, si nk’ivy’ibiri, ahubwo kigereranya igikorwa gikomeza. Nkako, mu bijanye no kuronka canke kwimurira Bitcoin, ukwo kumenya kwama gushoboka ku rugero rutandukanye.


Nk’akarorero, iyo uguze ama bitcoins ku rubuga rutegekanijwe mu Busuwisi, KYC ntibisabwa. Ariko rero, imfunguruzo zawe zirashobora kumenyekana, kuko ivyo waguze biciye ku konti yawe yo muri banki. Aho niho ingorane zibiri za mbere zijanye n’ubuhinga bwa KYC - kworohereza abantu gukurikirana onchain no gushikirwa n’ubugenzuzi bwa Leta - na zo nyene zishobora kwigaragaza muri Exchange itagira KYC. Iyo ishirahamwe ry’Ubusuwisi rimenyesheje abategetsi bo mu gihugu cawe amahera ateye amakenga, barashobora gusa gusuzuma konti ya banki yakoreshejwe mu kugura kugira ngo bamenye uwo uri we. Rero, kugura ata KYC ku mbuga zitegekanijwe ni vyiza cane ku rugero rw’ingorane zo kumenya ivy’ingenzi.


![BTC204](assets/rn/085.webp)


Ariko rero, kwirinda ama platforms ategekanijwe no guhitamwo uburyo bwo kuronka P2P ntibikuraho burundu ingorane zo kumenya urufunguruzo, ahubwo biragabanya gusa. Reka dufate akarorero k’ugugura kuri Bisq canke ku yindi nzira ya P2P. Kugira ngo wishyure uwo mugenzi wawe, birashoboka ko uzokoresha konti yawe yo muri banki. Iyo abategetsi babajije uwo mwagurishije bagasaba izina ryawe, turasubira ku bibazo 1 na 2. Naho ivyo bibazo biri hasi cane y’igihe ugura ku rubuga rudafise KYC, mbere bikaba biri hasi y’igihe ugura ufise KYC, biracariho ku rugero rutoyi.


![BTC204](assets/rn/086.webp)


Ubwa nyuma, naho woba uronka ama bitcoins yawe biciye ku Exchange y’umubiri ku mafaranga, ntuba utazwi rwose. Uwo mwaganiriye yarabonye mu maso hawe, ivyo bikaba ari kimwe mu bigize akaranga kawe. Naho ari bike cane muri aka karorero, haracariho ubushobozi bwo kumenya urufunguruzo.


![BTC204](assets/rn/087.webp)


Mu gusozera, iyo bitcoins zihinduwe n’ibindi bintu, haba ugugura mu mafaranga ya Leta canke ugurisha ku kintu nyaco, hama hariho uburyo bumwe bwo kumenya urufunguruzo. Bivanye n’uburyo bwa Exchange bwatowe, iyo nzira yo kumenya umuntu ishobora gutandukanywa mu buryo bukomeye. Ni ngombwa ko tutavanga iyo nzira y’ukumenyekana na KYC, ari yo nzira y’amategeko isobanuwe neza. Ariko rero, hariho isano hagati ya KYC n’urutonde rw’ibimenyetso, kuko KYC iri ku mpera y’urutonde rwo hejuru, kuko ifasha mu buryo butunganye kumenya imfunguruzo z’abakoresha n’ubutegetsi.


## Uburyo bwo kugurisha no kuronka


<chapterId>756598af-95aa-4c77-ac48-243c7ad89530</chapterId>



Uhejeje gusoma igice c’imbere, ushobora kuba uriko uribaza ingene woshobora kugura canke kugurisha Bitcoin utaciye mu buryo bwo kugenzura akaranga, kugira ngo wirinde ingorane zijanye n’ugukoresha KYC. Hari uburyo bwinshi bwo gucuruza Bitcoin.


### P2P amafaranga yo guhindura


Nk’uko twabibonye, ​​uburyo bwiza cane mu bijanye n’ibanga buguma ari P2P (umuntu ku muntu) Exchange n’amahera yo gutanga. Ubwo buryo buratuma ugabanya ibimenyetso bisigaye inyuma, kandi bikagabanya cane ubushobozi bwo kumenya urufunguruzo, waba uriko uragura canke uriko uragurisha.


![BTC204](assets/rn/088.webp)


Naho ari ukwo, hariho ingorane zishobora gutuma umuntu agira umutekano. Icoba ari ikibazo nyamukuru kiri mu kuba, mu gihe ca Exchange, uwo mugenzi azomenya ko ufise amahera menshi, yaba mu mafaranga canke mu bitcoins. Aya makuru arashobora gukwegera abantu b’abanyaruyeri. Nkako, muri rusangi ni vyiza kuba umuntu yiyubara ku bijanye n’ivyo ufise mu Bitcoin. Iyo mpanuro yoshobora no gukoreshwa ku bijanye n’amahera. Ariko rero, iyo muhanahana umuntu ku giti ciwe, nta nkeka ko muhishura ko mufise ama bitcoins, kandi ivyo bishobora gukwegera abantu batavyipfuza.


![BTC204](assets/rn/089.webp)


Kugira ngo ivyo bibeho, ndaguhanura ko wokunda gukoresha amahera n’abantu wizigira, nk’abo mu muryango canke abagenzi somambike. Canke, woshobora kandi kwiyumvira gucuruza mu [makoraniro ya Bitcoin yo mu karere](https://btcmap.org/communities/map), umaze kujayo incuro nkeyi. Ivyo bizotuma umenya neza abandi bari muri iyo nama kandi ntube wenyene igihe uriko urahanahana amakuru ku mubiri. Ariko rero, birahambaye kumenya ko amafaranga P2P ahindura amafaranga afise ingorane ku mutekano wawe bwite zitabaho iyo ugura biciye ku rubuga rutegekanijwe no kuri konti yawe ya banki.


Ikindi, bivanye n’aho uba, gutwara no kubika amahera menshi birashobora gutera ingorane, yaba ari Bitcoin canke amahera y’agaciro.


Guhindura amahera birashobora kandi gutera ingorane mu vy’amategeko iyo abapolisi canke abandi bagenzura. Naho mu bihugu vyinshi ata mategeko agenga amahera ushobora gutwara, amahera arenze urugero arashobora gutuma umuntu akekeranya. Rero, urabe maso canecane nimba ubwirizwa gukora ingendo ndende, kandi wirinde gukora amahera menshi cane icarimwe, kugira ngo ntubwirizwe kwishingira intahe ko ufise amahera menshi.


Ubwa nyuma, ikindi kibazo co kugura P2P ni uko igiciro gikunda kuba kinini kuruta ku bibanza bitegekanijwe. Abagurisha kenshi basaba igiciro kuva kuri 1% gushika rimwe na rimwe kirenze 10%. Hari imvo zitari nke zituma haba iyo ntandukaniro y’igiciro. Ica mbere, ivyo ni umugenzo usanzwe mu bagurisha P2P waciye ushinga imizi uko igihe kigenda kirarenga. Ica kabiri, abagurisha barafise amahera ajanye n’ugucuruza kugira ngo barungikire ayo mahera uwuguze. Hari kandi n’ingorane nyinshi z’ubusuma mu kugurisha P2P ugereranyije n’ugucuruza ku mbuga ngurukanabumenyi, ivyo bikaba bituma umuntu atanga indishi ku ngorane zafashwe. Ubwa nyuma, igiciro c’inyongera gishobora kuba gifitaniye isano n’ivyo abantu basaba be n’uko Exchange imeze mu bijanye n’ibanga. Nk’umuguzi, inyungu mu ibanga irafise igiciro kigaragara mu giciro gishirwako n’ugurisha. Bamwe mu ba bitcoiners na bo nyene bemera ko igiciro co gushiramwo ikimenyetso ca BTC yaguzwe kuri P2P kigaragaza igiciro cayo nyaco, kandi bavuga ko ibiciro bigabanutse ku mbuga zitegekanijwe ari ingaruka y’ugusenyura ibanga ry’amakuru yawe bwite.


![BTC204](assets/rn/090.webp)


### P2P ihinduranya biciye ku rubuga rwo gushaka abagenzi


Iyindi nzira idatera ingorane nyinshi mu bijanye n’umutekano w’umuntu ni uguhindura amafaranga P2P ku rubuga gusa, biciye ku buryo bwo kwishura bukoresheje ubuhinga bwa none nka PayPal, gutanga amafaranga muri banki canke Revolut.


![BTC204](assets/rn/091.webp)


Ubwo buryo buratuma umuntu yirinda ingorane nyinshi zijanye n’ugukoresha amahera. Ariko rero, ingorane yo gutakaza amahera y’uwundi muntu ku rubuga rwa Exchange ni nyinshi cane. Nkako, muri Exchange y’umubiri, iyo uhaye amahera uwugurisha atagurungikiye ama bitcoins mu gusubiza, urashobora guca umuhamagara ngo akureho, kuko ahagaze imbere yawe. Ku rundi ruhande, kuri Internet, kenshi ntibishoboka gukurikirana umuntu yakwivye.


![BTC204](assets/rn/092.webp)


Kugira ngo ivyo bigabanywe, birashoboka gukoresha ama platforms yihariye yo guhinduranya P2P. Izo mbuga zikoresha uburyo bwo gutorera umuti amakimbirane kugira ngo zikingire abakoresha bababajwe. Mu bisanzwe, batanga uburyo bwo gushiramwo amafaranga, aho amafaranga y’ama bitcoins aguma gushika aho amahera y’amahera y’amahera yemejwe n’uwugurisha.


![BTC204](assets/rn/093.webp)


Ku bijanye n’umutekano w’umuntu, ubu buryo bwo kugura buratekanye cane kuruta amahera y’umubiri Exchange. Ariko rero, nk’uko twabibonye haruguru, uguhinduranya P2P kuri Internet bisiga ibimenyetso vyinshi kuruta Exchange y’umubiri, ivyo bikaba bishobora kwonona ubuzima bwite kuri Bitcoin. Mu gukoresha uburyo bwo kwishura kuri internet nk’ubwa banki, urashira ahabona amakuru menshi yoshobora kworohereza umuntu kumenya urufunguzo.


![BTC204](assets/rn/094.webp)


Na none, sinzosaba gukora ubudandaji bwinshi cane mu gucuruza kumwe kuri izo mbuga. Mu gucapura amafaranga yawe, urakwiragiza ingorane zo kwibwa n’abandi.


Na none, ikindi kibazo co kugura P2P ni uko igiciro gikunda kuba kinini kuruta ico umuntu abona ku mbuga zitegekanijwe. Abagurisha kenshi basaba igiciro kuva kuri 1% gushika rimwe na rimwe kirenze 10%. Hari imvo zitari nke zituma haba iyo ntandukaniro y’igiciro. Ica mbere, ivyo ni umugenzo usanzwe mu bagurisha P2P waciye ushinga imizi uko igihe kigenda kirarenga. Ica kabiri, abagurisha barafise amahera ajanye n’ugucuruza kugira ngo barungikire ayo mahera uwuguze. Hari kandi n’ingorane nyinshi z’ubusuma mu kugurisha P2P ugereranyije n’ugucuruza ku mbuga, ivyo bikaba bituma umuntu atanga indishi ku ngorane zafashwe. Ubwa nyuma, igiciro c’inyongera gishobora kuba gifitaniye isano n’ivyo abantu basaba be n’uko Exchange imeze mu bijanye n’ibanga. Nk’umuguzi, inyungu mu ibanga irafise igiciro kigaragara mu giciro gishirwako n’ugurisha. Bamwe mu ba bitcoiners na bo nyene bemera ko igiciro co gushiramwo ikimenyetso ca BTC yaguzwe kuri P2P kigaragaza igiciro cayo nyaco, kandi bavuga ko ibiciro bigabanutse ku mbuga zitegekanijwe ari ingaruka y’ugusenyura ibanga ry’amakuru yawe bwite.


![BTC204](assets/rn/095.webp)


Ku bijanye n’imiti, jewe ubwanje nama nkoresha [Bisq](https://bisq.network/) kandi ndayinezerewe cane. Uburyo bwabo burageragezwa kandi busa n’ubwo kwizigirwa. Ariko Bisq iboneka kuri PC gusa kandi Interface yayo ishobora kuba igoye cane ku batangura. Ikindi kibazo ni uko Bisq ikora gusa n’amafaranga y’uruzitiro, ivyo bishobora gutwara amahera menshi mu bihe vy’amahera menshi y’amafaranga y’amafaranga Bitcoin.


-> Raba inyigisho yacu ya Bisq.


https://planb.network/tutorials/exchange/peer-to-peer/bisq-fe244bfa-dcc4-4522-8ec7-92223373ed04

Kugira ngo ubone uburyo bworoshe, urashobora kugerageza [Peach](https://peachbitcoin.com/), porogarama yo kuri telefone ngendanwa ihuza abaguzi n’abagurisha n’uburyo bwo gutorera umuti amatati bushizwemwo. Ivyo bikorwa birashoboka cane kuruta ivya Bisq.


-> Raba inyigisho yacu ya Peach.


https://planb.network/tutorials/exchange/peer-to-peer/peach-c6143241-d900-4047-9b73-1caba5e1f874

Iyindi nzira yo kuri internet ni [HodlHodl](https://hodlhodl.com/), urubuga rwashinzwe neza rutanga amahera meza, naho jewe ubwanje ntari naragerageje.


-> Raba inyigisho yacu ya HodlHodl.


https://planb.network/tutorials/exchange/peer-to-peer/hodlhodl-d7344cd5-6b18-40f5-8e78-2574a93a3879

Ku bijanye n’ibisubizo bishingiye kuri Lightning Network, gerageza [RoboSats] na [LNP2PBot]. RoboSats ushobora kuyironka biciye ku rubuga kandi yoroshe gukoresha. LNP2PBot ni ikintu kidasanzwe, kuko ikora biciye ku nzira ya Exchange ku rubuga rwo gutanga ubutumwa rwa Telegram.


-> Raba inyigisho yacu ya RoboSats.


-> Raba inyigisho yacu ya LNP2PBot.


https://planb.network/tutorials/exchange/peer-to-peer/robosats-b60e4f7c-533a-4295-9f6d-5368152e8c06

https://planb.network/tutorials/exchange/peer-to-peer/lnp2pbot-v2-e6bcb210-610b-487d-970c-7cce85273e3c

![BTC204](assets/rn/096.webp)


### Imbuga zitunganijwe ata KYC


Bivanye n’igihugu ubamwo, ushobora kuronka uburenganzira bwo gukoresha ama platforms ategekanijwe adasaba uburyo bwa KYC kugira ngo ugure canke ugurishe ama bitcoins. Nk’akarorero, mu Busuwisi, mbere woshobora gukoresha [Relai](https://relai.app/) na [MtPelerin](https://www.mtpelerin.com/), ubu zitanga ibikorwa vyazo hakurikijwe amabwirizwa ya KYC.


-> Raba inyigisho yacu kuri Relai.


https://planb.network/tutorials/exchange/centralized/relai-v2-30a9671d-e407-459d-9203-4c3eae15b30e

Nk’uko twabibonye mu kigabane c’imbere, ubwo bwoko bw’urubuga buragukiza ingorane zijanye n’uburyo bwa KYC, ariko buratanga urugero rwo hejuru rw’ingorane zo kumenya ivy’ingenzi. Ku bijanye n’ibanga rya Bitcoin rero, izo nzira zitanga uburinzi bwiza kuruta uburyo bwo kugura hakoreshejwe KYC, ariko ziguma zidakwegera cane nk’uguhinduranya P2P.


Ariko rero, ku bijanye n’umutekano w’umuntu ku giti ciwe, gukoresha izo nzira ni ikintu giteye akaga gato cane kuruta gukoresha ubuhinga bwa P2P. Akenshi kandi ziroroshe gukoresha kuruta ama platforms ya P2P.


### Ama ATM


Iyindi nzira yo kugura canke kugurisha amafaranga y’ama bitcoins ata KYC ni ama ATM y’amafaranga y’ama cryptocurrency. Ku bwanje, sinigeze ngira akaryo ko kugerageza uwo muti, kuko mu gihugu canje nta n’umwe uriho. Ariko ubu buryo burashobora gushimisha cane, bivanye n’aho uba.


![BTC204](assets/rn/097.webp)


Ikibazo c’ama ATM ni uko abujijwe mu bihugu bimwe bimwe, canke akagenzurwa cane mu bindi. Iyo ATM isaba uburyo bwo kugenzura akaranga, rero irashikirwa n’ingorane nk’izo ziri mu bibanza bigenzurwa na KYC. Ku rundi ruhande, iyo ATM yemerera gukoresha amafaranga ata kugenzura akaranga k’amahera makeyi, rero gukoresha kwayo birashobora gutanga urugero rw’ibanga rugereranywa n’urw’amahera P2P Exchange, mu gihe umuntu yirinda ingorane nyinshi zijanye n’ubwo bwoko bwa Exchange.


Intambamyi nyamukuru y’ama ATM ni amahera akenshi atanga cane Exchange, kuva ku bice bike kw’ijana gushika rimwe na rimwe ku bice 15 kw’ijana vy’amahera ahindurwa.


### Ikarata y'ingabire


Mu gusozera, nashaka kandi kubamenyesha umuti ukora neza ku bashaka gukoresha amafaranga yabo ya bitcoins ku musi ku musi kugira ngo bagure aho kuyagurisha ku mafaranga ya fiat.


Uburyo bwiza bwo gukoresha BTC ni, birumvikana, gukoresha Bitcoin canke Lightning Network ataco uhinduye kugira ngo ugure ikintu canke igikorwa. Ariko rero, mu bihugu vyinshi, igitigiri c’abadandaza bemera Bitcoin kiracari gito. Iyindi nzira ngirakamaro ni ugukoresha amakarata y’ingabirano.


Ivyuma vyinshi bidasaba uburyo bwa KYC biratanga ubushobozi bwo guhindura amafaranga y’ama bitcoins ku makarita y’ingabirano ashobora gukoreshwa ku maduka akomeye. Ivyo birimwo [CoinsBee](Ishirahamwe Bitcoin](Ishirahamwe ry’Ibiceri) na [Bitrefill](Ishirahamwe ry’Ibiceri.com/). Izo nzira zituma vyoroha cane gukoresha amafaranga yawe ya bitcoins ku musi ku musi, bikaguha uburenganzira bwo kuronka ibintu vyinshi n’ibikorwa vyinshi ataco ukeneye kubihindura mu mafaranga y’amahera.


https://planb.network/tutorials/exchange/centralized/bitrefill-8c588412-1bfc-465b-9bca-e647a647fbc1

![BTC204](assets/rn/098.webp)


### Ubundi buryo bwo kuronka


Ubundi buryo bwo kuronka bitcoins mu gihe urinda ubuzima bwite bwawe harimwo, birashoboka, Mining. Kugira ngo utangure Mining Sats, ntukeneye kumenyesha akaranga kawe; gusa urondere Proof of Work ibereye maze uyirungike ku rubuga. Iyo uhisemwo pool Mining, pools zimwe zimwe zisaba uburyo bumwe bumwe bwo kumenya umuntu, nk’ikimenyetso ca KYC, mu gihe izindi zitabisaba.


Ubundi buryo ni ugukora muri Exchange ku bitcoins. Ubwo buryo bwo kuronka umuntu burashobora gushimisha, mugabo urugero rwo kumenya umuntu rusabwa ruratandukanye cane bivanye n’ingene ivyo bintu vyifashe.


*Kugira ngo ndiko ndandika iki gice, nakoresheje inyigisho ya BTC205 yatanzwe na* [@pivi___](https://x.com/pivi___) *ku rupapuro rwa Plan ₿ Network (ruboneka mu gifaransa gusa muri iki gihe)*


## Gushiramwo, uburongozi bwa UTXO na CIOH


<chapterId>d0486c8f-332d-402b-ae2e-949416752b9c</chapterId>



Kimwe mu bintu bigoye cane mu gutwara igikoresho co kwibungabunga Wallet ni ugukomeza. Woba ukwiye gukomeza? Iciyumviro ni ikihe? Ni ubunini ubuhe bwa UTXO bukwiye kwubahirizwa? Ni ibihe bintu bishobora gusenyuka mu bijanye n’ibanga? Ivyo ni vyo tuzorabira muri iki gice.


### None ugushikama ni iki?


Bitcoin ikora nk’isoko ry’icuma, abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro bagatanga ivyiyumviro ku bijanye n’ugucuruza bitanga amahera makeyi. Ariko rero, igice cose gifise uburemere burenze, ivyo bikaba bigabanya umubare w’ibikorwa bishobora gushirwamwo. Nk’uko igice kimwe gisohoka mu mwanya w’iminota 10 yose, umwanya uri muri buri gice ni ubutunzi buke.


Abacukuzi b’amabuye y’agaciro, ibikorwa vyabo generate bitwara amahera menshi mu bijanye n’amashanyarazi, ibintu bihoraho n’ugutunganywa, mu bisanzwe barondera kuronka inyungu nyinshi. Bakunda rero gukunda amafaranga generate atanga amahera menshi kuruta ayandi yose ugereranije n’uburemere bwayo.


Si amafaranga yose ya Bitcoin afise uburemere bumwe. Abafise ivyo bashiramwo n’ivyo basohora vyinshi bazopima cane. Nk'akarorero, reka twiyumvire ibikorwa 2:




- Ibikorwa A birimwo input 1 n’isohoka 1. Itanga amafaranga 1.994 Sats kandi ifise uburemere bwa 141 vB;
- Ibikorwa B, ibikorwa bikomeye cane bifise ivyinjizwa 2 n’ibisohoka 2, bitanga 2.640 Sats mu mahera ku buremere bwa 220 vB.


![BTC204](assets/rn/099.webp)


Muri aka karorero, naho igikorwa B gitanga amahera yose hamwe menshi, abacukuzi bazohitamwo igikorwa A, kuko gitanga igipimo ciza hagati y’amahera n’uburemere. Ehe ibara ry'ibikorwa vyose, rigaragazwa muri Sats ku byte y'ukuri (sat/vB):


```text
TXA: 1994 / 141 = 14 sats/vB
TXB: 2640 / 220 = 12 sats / vB
```


Ivyo bisigura ko ku giciro cose c’uburemere, igikorwa A gitanga amahera menshi kuruta igikorwa B, naho igikorwa B gitanga amahera menshi mu buryo bushitse.


![BTC204](assets/rn/100.webp)


Ni co gituma vyama bishimishije cane ko uwukoresha akoresha ibintu bikeyi bishoboka mu bikorwa vyiwe. Ariko rero, urakeneye gukoresha amahera ahagije kugira ngo ushobore guhazwa n’amahera y’umusaruro. Igihe ucungera Wallet yawe, ukeneye kugira UTXO nini zihagije.


Ingingo ngenderwako y’ugushiramwo ni ugukoresha neza ibihe amafaranga ari make kuri Bitcoin kugira ngo ihurize hamwe UTXO zayo ntoyi zibe imwe nini. Uko niko, iyo amafaranga azoduga kuri Bitcoin, uzoshobora gukora amafaranga makeyi cane, rero ukoreshe amafaranga make ku mafaranga mu buryo bushitse. Intumbero rero ni ugutegura imbere y’igihe ibikorwa vy’ingorane bizokorwa mu bihe vy’amahera menshi.


![BTC204](assets/rn/101.webp)


Uretse kuzigama amafaranga y'ibikorwa, gushiramwo UTXOs birafasha gukingira "Dust". Dust" yerekeza ku UTXOs agaciro kayo muri Sats kari hasi cane ku buryo bidahagije kugira ngo umuntu ashobore kwishura amafaranga y'ugucuruza asabwa kugira ngo akoreshe. Ivyo bituma ayo ma UTXO adashobora gukoreshwa mu vy'ubutunzi igihe cose amafaranga y'ugucuruza aguma ari menshi. amafaranga aguma akoreshwa.


### Ni ubuhe bunini bukeyi bw’ama UTXO yawe?


Rimwe na rimwe ndabazwa agaciro gatoyi cane k’i UTXO. Ikibabaje, nta n’inyishu ihari, kuko bivana n’ivyo ukunda be n’ingene isoko ry’amahera rimeze. Ariko rero, ng'iyi formule ishobora kugufasha kumenya urugero rubereye ivyo ukeneye:


$$
\frac {P \times F}T = M
$$


Hehe:




- p$ ni uburemere bw’ibikorwa;
- $F$ igereranya igipimo c’amahera menshi cane mu satoshis ku vbyte (Sats/vB) ukingira;
- t$ ni ijana kw’ijana ry’amahera y’ugucuruza wifuza kwishura ugereranije n’agaciro kose k’igitabu ca UTXO;
- m$ ni umubare mutoyi mu satoshis kuri UTXO yose.


Reka twiyumvire ko utegura kwishura amafaranga y’ugucuruza kwa SegWit gusanzwe gufise input 1 n’isohoka 2, bipima 141 vB. Niba uriko urakingira amafaranga ashika kuri 800 Sats/vB, kandi wifuza gukoresha amafaranga ashika kuri 12% y’agaciro ka UTXO mu mafaranga menshi, rero igiharuro coba ari:


$$
\frac{141 \times 800}{0.12} = 940\ 000
$$


Muri aka karorero, vyoba vyiza rero ugumye agaciro gatoyi k'ama Sats 940.000 ku ma UTXO muri Wallet yawe.


### Gushiramwo hamwe na CIOH


Imwe mu nzira zikoreshwa cane mu gusesangura Blockchain ni CIOH (*Common Input Ownership Heuristic*), ifata ko ibintu vyose vyinjizwa mu gucuruza Bitcoin ari ivy’ikigo kimwe. Ingingo ngenderwako y’ugushiramwo ni ugukoresha ama UTXO menshi nk’ivyo kwinjiza no kurema UTXO imwe nk’ivyo gusohoka. Gushiramwo rero bituma ICOH ishobora gukoreshwa.


![BTC204](assets/rn/102.webp)


Mu bikorwa, ivyo bisigura ko uwubibona wo hanze ashobora gufata ingingo y’uko UTXO zose zihuriweko zishobora kuba ari iz’umuntu umwe, kandi ko umusaruro udasanzwe uvamwo na wo nyene ari uwiwe. Ivyo bishobora gutuma ibanga ryawe rihungabana mu gufatanya amateka atandukanye y’ibikorwa. Nk’akarorero, reka tuvuge ko nkoranya UTXO 3 zaronswe biciye kuri P2P n’imwe UTXO yaronswe biciye ku rubuga rusaba KYC:


![BTC204](assets/rn/103.webp)


Mu kubigira, ikigo cose gifise uburenganzira bwo kuronka amakuru y’urubuga rwa Exchange, bishoboka ko harimwo n’ibigo vya Leta, kizoshobora kumenya ko mfise ayandi mahera ya BTC. Mbere, izo UTXO ntizari zifitaniye isano n’akaranga kanje ata guca ku ruhande; ubu rero ni ko biri. Ikindi, bihishurira amasoko yose ko mfise umubare kanaka w’ama bitcoins.


Ku bijanye no gucunga amashirahamwe y’ubudandaji, ivy’ubutunzi, bituma habaho uguhuza amashirahamwe kugira ngo hagabanuke ibiciro, birahushanye n’imigenzo myiza y’ubuzima bwite, ivyo bikaba vyosaba ko amashirahamwe y’ubudandaji atazokwigera ahurizwa hamwe. Guhitamwo hagati y’ubutunzi n’ibanga rero bivana n’ivyo uwukoresha wese ashira imbere.


Niba ushobora kwirinda gukomera mu gihe uguma ufise UTXO nyinshi, ivyo ni vyiza. Kugira ngo ubikore, nutunganye neza uburyo ukoresha mu kuronka. Niwagura bitcoins zawe muri DCA, gerageza gutandukanya ivyo ugura rimwe gusa uko bishoboka kwose kugira ngo ukomeze agaciro ku UTXO nke. Bizoroha gucungera ugugura rimwe gusa kw’amayero 1.000 buri mezi 2, aho kugura amayero 120 buri ndwi. Ivyo bigabanya umubare w’ama UTXO avutse kandi bikorohereza uburongozi bwa Wallet yawe mu gihe uzigama ibanga ryawe.


Niwaba ubona ko ubwirizwa gushiramwo ama bitcoins yawe, banza ushire imbere gushiramwo ama UTXOs ava ku nzira imwe. Nk’akarorero, gufatanya ama UTXO 10 avuye ku rubuga rumwe bizokugirako ingaruka ku ibanga ryawe bike kuruta gufatanya ama UTXO 5 avuye ku rubuga A n’ama UTXO 5 avuye ku rubuga B. Nimba gufatanya amasoko atandukanye bidashoboka, gerageza kuyatandukanya hakurikijwe ibiranga. Nk’akarorero, ushire hamwe ama UTXO yaronswe biciye kuri KYC mu gucuruza kumwe, n’ayo yaronswe biciye kuri P2P mu yindi.


Uko biri kwose, ntimwibagire ko ugushira hamwe kwose ata kabuza gutuma umuntu atakaza ibanga. Rero, nusuzume witonze ukuntu iyo operation ikenewe be n’ingaruka bishobora kugira ku buzima bwawe bwite, uzirikana CIOH.


## Ibindi bikorwa vyiza


<chapterId>b5216965-7d13-4ea1-9b7c-e292966a487b</chapterId>



Reka turabe ubundi buryo bwiza bwo gutuma ubuzima bwite bwawe bugenda neza kuri Bitcoin.


### Ipfundo ryose


Kugira ama bitcoins yawe mu kwizigama ni vyiza cane, ariko gukoresha Full node yawe bwite ni vyiza kuruta! Ehe igituma kugira node yawe bwite ari ngirakamaro kugira ngo ukoreshe neza Bitcoin:




- **Uguhangana n'ugucengera**: Ivyo ukora nta n'umwe ashobora kubibuza;
- **Ukwigenga ku bandi bantu**: Ntugishingiye ku gikorwa ico ari co cose co hanze co kugenzura amakuru ya Blockchain;
- **Ukwifatanya n'abandi**: Ushobora gusobanura amategeko yawe yo kwemeza kandi ukagira uruhara mu buryo butaziguye mu guhurizako;
- **Intambwe y'urubuga**: Mu gukoresha urudodo, ufasha gukomeza no gukwiragiza urubuga rwa Bitcoin;
- **Uburezi bw'ubuhinga**: Gucungera Full node ni uburyo bwiza bwo gukomeza ubumenyi bwawe bw'ubuhinga bwa Bitcoin.


Uretse izo nyungu, gukoresha Full node na vyo nyene biratuma urushiriza kugira ibanga igihe utangaza amafaranga yawe. Iyo utanga amafaranga, abanza kuremwa no gusinywa biciye ku Wallet yawe. Kugira ngo imenyekane ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin, itegerezwa kumenyekana n’imiburiburi n’urudodo rumwe. Mu gukoresha urudodo rwawe bwite, urafise ububasha butaziguye kuri iyo nzira yo gukwiragiza, gutyo ugakomeza ibanga ryawe kandi ugagabanya ingorane zo gusohoka kw’amakuru.


![BTC204](assets/rn/104.webp)


Nimba udafise node yawe bwite ya Bitcoin, uzobwirizwa gukoresha iyindi, nk’iyo itangwa n’uwuguha porogarama ya Wallet. Uretse gutangaza amafaranga, Wallet yawe isaba kuronka amakuru atandukanye nk’amafaranga ategerejwe, amafaranga asigaye ajanye n’amaderesi yawe be n’umubare w’ivyemezo vy’amafaranga yawe. Kugira ngo ubone aya makuru yose, ukeneye kubaza urudodo.


![BTC204](assets/rn/105.webp)


Icoba ari ikibazo nyamukuru iyo udakoresha uruzitiro rwawe bwite rwa Bitcoin ni uko uwukoresha uruzitiro rw’uwundi muntu yoshobora kwihweza ibikorwa vyawe kuri Blockchain, canke mbere agasangira aya makuru n’ibindi bigo. Kugira ngo ugabanye ivyo bibazo, umuti wo hagati ni ugukoresha porogarama ya Wallet ipfuka amahuriro yawe biciye kuri Tor. Ivyo birashobora kugabanya ukuntu amakuru yawe agaragara. Ariko rero, umuti mwiza ni ukugira node yawe bwite ya Bitcoin maze ukayikoresha mu gutangaza amafaranga yawe. Ego ni ko, uzokenera kandi kwiyubara kugira ngo ntusohoke amakuru yose biciye ku nzira yawe, ariko iyo ni ikindi kintu tuzorabira mu bice bizokurikira.


Uretse akamaro kagaragara ku buzima bwite bwawe, kugira Full node yawe bwite na vyo nyene birakwizeza ukuri kw’amakuru ari kuri Blockchain, bikakurinda gucengera kandi bikaguha uburenganzira bwo kugira uruhara n’umwete mu butegetsi bwa Bitcoin. Mu gukoresha node yawe bwite, utanga uburemere bwawe bw’ubutunzi ku ruhererekane uhisemwo, ivyo bikaba bihambaye mu gihe c’amatati mu kibano, nk’igihe c’intambara ya Blocksize kuva mu 2015 gushika mu 2017 nk’akarorero. Mu gihe ca Fork, gukoresha urudodo rw’uwundi muntu vyoshobora kugushikana ku gushigikira urudodo udashaka gukunda, nk’uko umukoresha w’urudodo ari we aguhitamwo.


Nk’uko mubibona, kubera inyungu z’ibanga n’ubusegaba bw’umuntu ku giti ciwe, ni ngombwa ko wiruka kandi ukoresha Full node yawe bwite!


### Guhenda isesengura ry'ubuhinga


Mu buryo bwagutse, birahambaye gutahura heuristics twavuze mu gice ca mbere, kugira ngo tushobore kuzirinda canke kuzihenda. Kwemera urutonde rw’ingeso nziza cane birashobora kuba ngirakamaro, naho nyene bitari ngombwa. Batanga uburinzi bwongereweko Layer bushobora kuba buhambaye mu kubungabunga ibanga igihe ukoresha Bitcoin.


Impanuro ya mbere notanga ni iyo kwivanga n’abantu benshi cane. Ku Bitcoin, ivyo bisigura gukoresha ibigereranyo vy’inyandiko vyemewe cane. Nk’akarorero, inyandiko za P2WSH, zikoreshwa kenshi ku miterere ya SegWit V0 Multisig, ntizisanzwe cane. Ntibakwemerera kwihisha mu gice kinini c’abantu batazwi. Ivyo ni vyo bigenda no ku bikoresho vya kera nka P2PKH canke P2SH. Naho ziboneka cane mu gice ca UTXO, zikoreshwa cane mu bikorwa bishasha.


Muri rusangi, ni vyiza guhitamwo urugero rw’inyandiko rwa vuba cane, igihe cose rwashizweho bihagije. Rero, iyo mu 2022, noba naragira inama yo kudakoresha P2TR (Taproot) kubera ukuntu ikoreshwa cane, mu 2024, noba naragira inama yo guhitamwo ubwo bwoko bw’inyandiko aho, canke iyo bidashoboka, ku nyandiko ya SegWit V0, nk’uko umubare w’ibikorwa bikoreshwa cane GW userukira GW is-2.


![BTC204](assets/rn/106.webp)


Inkomoko: [ibiharuro.com](ibiharuro.com/d/000000054/UTXO-gushiraho-ugusubira gucapura-ku-bwoko-bw'isohoka)


Iyindi mpanuro yo kuzigama ibanga ryawe ni ukugerageza guca mu nzira y’ubuhinga bwo gukorana n’abandi. Nk’akarorero, igihe uriha, urashobora kugerageza kwirinda kurema igisohoka gifise umubare uzunguruka, kuko ivyo vyoshobora kwerekana ko ikindi gisohoka giserukira ihinduka. Niba ukeneye kohereza umugenzi 100 k Sats, wiyumvire ko yohereza amahera menshi gatoyi kugira ngo uhunga iyo heuristic. Na wewe nyene, gerageza kudahingura ibiva mu mpinduka iyo ari yo yose irengeye urugero mu bijanye n’ukwishyura kwakozwe, kuko ivyo vyoshobora kandi kwerekana ico mu biva mu bisohoka giserukira ihinduka.


![BTC204](assets/rn/107.webp)


Ubwa nyuma, nimba ukora ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji vya Bitcoin ku buryo budasanzwe, urabe neza ko udahora uyatangaza mu bihe bimwe. Mu gukwiragiza amakuru y’ivyo ukora mu musi wose no mu ndwi yose, urinda guha abarorerezi bo hanze akaryo ko kumenya urutonde rw’igihe rushingiye ku gihe rwoshobora gukomeza isesengura ryabo.


Uretse ivyo bikorwa vyiza vyose vyo gukurikiza ku musi ku musi, hari mbere n’uburyo bwiza bwo guca burundu uburyo bwo gukurikirana ama bitcoins yawe. Ivyo birimwo, birumvikana, amafaranga y’ubudandaji bwa CoinJoin, ivyo tuzobiraba mu buryo bwimbitse mu gice gikurikira.


# Gutahura ibikorwa vya CoinJoin


<partId>6d0bbf16-3714-4db1-9897-2d45019f6bdc</partId>


## None igikorwa ca CoinJoin ni iki?


<chapterId>0862bc6b-1c48-4aa4-b76d-4f547b469008</chapterId>



Tumaze kwiga ivy’ishimikiro vyo kurinda ubuzima bwite, ubu tugiye kuraba ubuhinga buteye imbere cane bugamije kurwanira n’umwete ibanga ryawe, cane cane mu gutandukanya amateka yawe ya Bitcoin. Mu gice gikurikira, tuzoba turiko turaraba ubuhinga buke buke, ariko mbere, ndashaka kubabwira ivya CoinJoin.


CoinJoin akenshi ifatwa nk’uburyo bwiza bwo kurinda ubuzima bwite bw’abakoresha Bitcoin. Ariko none, ugucuruza CoinJoin ni iki nyabuna? Reka tubimenye.


### Ingingo ngenderwako z’ishimikiro zo muri CoinJoin


CoinJoin ni ubuhinga bwo guca Bitcoin gukurikirana kuri Blockchain. Ishingiye ku gucuruza kw’ubufatanye gufise imiterere yihariye y’izina rimwe: ugucuruza kwa CoinJoin.


Nk’uko twabibonye mu bice vya mbere vy’iri shure, amafaranga y’ubudandaji ya Bitcoin arazwi n’abakoresha bose biciye ku nzira yabo. Biroroshe rero kugenzura uruhererekane rw’imikono y’ubuhinga bwa none y’igikoresho cose citwa Coin no kwihweza kahise kaco. Ivyo bisigura ko abakoresha bose bashobora kugerageza gusuzuma amafaranga y’abandi bakoresha. Ivyo bituma ukutamenyekana ku rugero rw’ugucuruza bidashoboka. Ariko rero, ukutamenyekana kurazigama ku rugero rw’ukumenyekana kw’umuntu ku giti ciwe. Mu buryo butandukanye n’uburyo busanzwe bwo gukoresha banki, aho konti yose ihuzwa n’akaranga k’umuntu, kuri Bitcoin, amahera afatanywa n’ibifungurwa bibiri vy’urufunguzo (canke inyandiko), bikaba biha abakoresha uburyo bw’izina ry’uruyeri inyuma y’ibimenyetso vy’urufunguzo.


![BTC204](assets/rn/108.webp)


Ibanga rya Bitcoin rirahungabana iyo abarorerezi bo hanze bashobora gufatanya UTXO zihariye n’abakoresha bamenyekanye. Iryo shirahamwe rimaze gushingwa, birashoboka gukurikirana amafaranga yabo no gusuzuma amateka yabo ya Bitcoin. CoinJoin ni ubuhinga nyabwo bwateguwe kugira ngo buce ubushobozi bwo gukurikirana UTXOs, kugira ngo abakoresha Bitcoin bashobore guhabwa Layer y’ibanga ku rugero rw’ibikorwa.


Coinjoins zikomeza ibanga ry’abakoresha Bitcoin mu gutuma isesengura ry’uruzitiro rirushiriza kugora abarorerezi bo hanze. Uburyo bwavyo butuma ibiceri vyinshi biva ku bakoresha batandukanye bishobora guhurizwa hamwe bikagira igikorwa kimwe, bikaba bituma imirongo itaboneka neza kandi bikaba bigoye kumenya amasano ari hagati y’amaderesi y’injiza n’ay’isohoka.


Ni ngombwa gutahura ko intumbero y'ugucuruza CoinJoin ari uguca amateka ya Coin. Ubu buhinga ntibutanga ubutamenyekana ubudasiba canke ngo bubuze gukurikirana Bitcoin, bitandukanye n’ivyo woshobora kwiyumvira. CoinJoin igamije gusa guca amateka ku ntumbero aho igikorwa ca CoinJoin gikorerwa. Ariko rero, imbere n’inyuma y’ico gikorwa, Coin iguma ifise ingorane nk’izo nyene ku bijanye n’ibanga.


![BTC204](assets/rn/109.webp)


### None ama coinjoins akora gute?


Ingingo ya CoinJoin ishingiye ku buryo bwo gukorana: abakoresha benshi bipfuza guvanga amafaranga yabo ya bitcoins bashiramwo amahera asa n’ayo bashiramwo mu gikorwa kimwe. Ivyo bihembo bica bisubira gukwiragizwa mu bisohoka bifise agaciro kangana n’uwubikoresha wese.


![BTC204](assets/rn/110.webp)


Ku mpera y’ugucuruza, biraca bidashoboka gufatanya igisohoka kinaka n’ukoresha azwi nk’inyungu. Nta sano ry’ukuri riri hagati y’ivyo winjiza n’ivyo usohoka, ivyo bikaba bica isano hagati y’abakoresha n’ama UTXO yabo, hamwe n’amateka ya buri UTXO.


![BTC204](assets/rn/111.webp)


Reka dufate akarorero ka Alice. Ashaka kohereza mushikawe Eva amafaranga agera ku bihumbi 100 vy’ama Sats ku musi wiwe w’amavuko. Ariko rero, Alice ntishaka ko Eva ashobora gukurikirana amateka yiwe y’ugucuruza, kuko ntashaka gutangaza ingene afise amafaranga y’ama bitcoins canke ingene yayaronse. Kugira ngo ivyo bishoboke, Alice ifata ingingo yo guca amateka yiwe ya UTXO n’ugucuruza CoinJoin. Arategura na Bob, Charles, David na Frank kugira ngo bakore igikorwa co gukorana:




- Alice, Bob, Charles, David na Frank umwe wese akora UTXO y’ama Sats 105.000 (n’ama Sats 5.000 y’amahera y’ama Mining) nk’ivyo gushiramwo mu gucuruza:


![BTC204](assets/rn/112.webp)




- Mu gusubiza gukoresha ivyo bikoresho, kimwe cose gitanga Address y’ubusa kugira ngo kireme ibisohoka bitanu bisa n’ivyo 100.000 Sats kimwe cose. Imwe yose igarura igisohoka kimwe:


![BTC204](assets/rn/113.webp)




- Alice yisanga afise UTXO y’ama Sats 100.000 amateka yayo avunganye. Akoresha iyo UTXO mu bikorwa bishasha kugira ngo yoherereze Eva ayo mahera ku musi wiwe w’amavuko:


![BTC204](assets/rn/114.webp)




- Eva niyagerageza gusuzuma iyo nzira kugira ngo akuremwo amakuru, azohura n’inzira ya CoinJoin irimwo Alice, Bob, Charles, David na Frank. Kubera ko Eva adashobora gutandukanya input ari iya nde kubera ukuntu amafaranga amwe, ntashobora gukurikirana amateka ya Alice ya UTXO, canke ngo amenye ingene mushikiwe afise ama bitcoins canke ingene yayaronse:


![BTC204](assets/rn/115.webp)


Muri ivyo, Alice yakoresheje ubuhinga bwa CoinJoin kugira ngo yongere ibanga ku bijanye n’isesengura ry’inyuma. Mu vy'ukuri, Alice iriko irikingira isesengura rishoboka rya Eva, yotangura n'ugucuruza kwihariye maze agakora asubira inyuma biciye mu mateka ya UTXO. Ukwo kurinda gusesangura kuva ubu gushika muri kahise kuzwi kw’izina rya backward anonset. Ico ciyumviro tuzokiraba mu buryo burambuye mu bice vya nyuma vy’iki gice.


Ariko kandi, CoinJoin iratanga kandi ubushobozi bwo gukomeza ibanga mu gihe c’isesengura kuva kera gushika ubu, rizwi kw’izina rya forward anonset. Reka dusubire ku karorero kacu aho Alice yarungikiye Eva 98.000 Sats ku musi wiwe w’amavuko, ariko inshingano zikaba zahindutse. None reka twiyumvire ko ari Eva ahagaritse umutima ku bijanye n’ubuzima bwiwe bwite. Nkako, Alice yoshobora kugeragezwa no gukurikirana Coin yarungitse Eva kugira ngo ayikuremwo amakuru. Eva yari gushobora gukoranya neza iyi UTXO aherutse kuronka n’izindi UTXO ziwe zose, ivyo bishobora guhishurira Alice umubare w’ama bitcoins afise muri Wallet yiwe. Kugira ngo ivyo ntibibeho, Eva arashobora kandi guca amateka y’iyi Coin aherutse kuronka:




- Eva, Grace, Mallory, Oscar na Victor umwe wese yashizemwo amafaranga 658 y’amafaranga 98.000 nk’inyungu mu gucuruza amafaranga 656:


![BTC204](assets/rn/116.webp)




- Mu gusubiza gukoresha ivyo bikoresho, umukoresha wese atanga Address y'ubusa izokoreshwa mu guhingura ibisohoka 5 vy'ibikoresho 97.500 bingana neza na Sats. Buri mukoresha aronka igisubizo kimwe:


![BTC204](assets/rn/117.webp)




- Eva ubu afise UTXO y’ama Sats 97.500 amateka yayo yacitse. Arashobora kuyikoresha ata bwoba kugira ngo akore ibikorwa vyo mu gihe kizoza. Nkako, Alice niyagerageza gukurikirana ama bitcoins yarungikiye Eva, azohura n’ugucuruza kwa CoinJoin. Ntazoshobora kumenya UTXO isohoka ari iya Eva. Isesengura rihinduka ridashoboka:


![BTC204](assets/rn/118.webp)


Mu karorero ka mbere, twabonye ingene CoinJoin ishobora kurinda ubuzima bwite bw’icumba mu bijanye n’ivya kera, mu karorero ka kabiri, ingene ishobora kandi gukingira amateka y’icumba mu bijanye n’akazoza kaco. Ni co gituma navuze ko CoinJoin ikwiye gufatwa nk’ikintu kiba rimwe gusa gicapura amateka ya UTXO mu nzira zompi:


![BTC204](assets/rn/119.webp)


### Igikoresho co guvanga, CoinJoin, igikoresho co guvanga... Ni igiki gitandukanye?


Coinjoins rimwe na rimwe zidondorwa nk'"abavanga", ijambo bamwe mu ba bitcoiners banka, batinya ko ryoshobora gutera urujijo n'abavanga abacungera. Ariko rero, nizera ko iyo nzira y’ugutahura ata shingiro ifise, kuko, mu bijanye n’imibare, CoinJoin irimwo neza na neza iciyumviro co kuvanga.


Mu bijanye n’imibare rusangi, ukuvanga ni umutungo w’urutonde rw’inguvu aho, inyuma y’igihe kinaka, ibice vyose vy’ikibanza c’intango bishobora mu vyiyumviro kuvanga n’ikindi gice ico ari co cose. Guvanga bisigura ko ikibanza c’igice canke uko urutonde ruri bihinduka mu buryo bw’uko ugukwiragira kwaco muri kazoza kutajanye n’ugukwiragira kwarwo kwa mbere, gutyo bigashika ku rwego aho ibiranga urutonde rw’intango bigabanywa mu buryo bumwe mu kibanza cose c’urutonde. Ivyo ni vyo nyene bishika muri CoinJoin ifise ama bitcoins. Rero, mu vyiyumviro vyanje, CoinJoin ni uburyo bwo kuvanga Coin vy’ukuri.


![BTC204](assets/rn/120.webp)


Ku rundi ruhande, birahambaye gutandukanya CoinJoin n’aba shufflers. Shuffler ni service aho abakoresha bohereje ama bitcoins yabo kugira ngo ahindurwe. Izo serivisi zari zizwi cane mu myaka ya 2010, ariko ikoreshwa ryazo ryaragabanutse kubera ingorane zibiri zikomeye ugereranyije na CoinJoin:




- Bisaba abakoresha kureka kubika amahera yabo mu gihe c’uguvanga, ivyo bikaba bituma bashikirwa n’ingorane zo kwibwa;
- Nta cizere ko iyo mixer itazokwandika amakuru y’ibikorwa, canke mbere ngo igurishe ayo makuru ku masosiyete akora isesengura ry’uruhererekane.


![BTC204](assets/rn/121.webp)


Abakoresha muri iki gihe rero barakunda CoinJoin, kuko ibafasha kuguma bafise ububasha bwose ku mahera yabo mu gihe cose bariko barakora. Abaje muri CoinJoin nta ngorane bafise yo kwibwa amafaranga yabo n’abandi ba UTXO bari muri iyo nzira. Reka turabe ingene ivyo vyose bishoboka mu kigabane gikurikira.


## Zerolink n'amafaranga y'i Chaumian


<chapterId>326c9654-b359-4906-b23d-d6518dd5dc3e</chapterId>



Ubuzima bwite butangwa na CoinJoin buronswa n’ubunini bw’umugwi igice cacu kinyegejwemwo. Ivyo bisigura kurondera abantu benshi bashoboka. Birashoboka cane gukora CoinJoin n’amaboko, n’abakoresha twisanze, ariko iyi ni inzira igoye, kandi ntizogutsinda anonsets nini.


Ni co gituma abahuzabikorwa ba CoinJoin bateye imbere kuri Bitcoin. Uruhara rwabo ni ugutuma abakoresha batandukanye bahuriza hamwe no gutanga amakuru akenewe kugira ngo baheza gukorana n’abandi.


![BTC204](assets/rn/122.webp)


Ariko twomenya gute ko umuhuzabikorwa atigera agira ibiganza vyiwe ku bitcoins z’abakoresha, kandi naho ari we muntu yubaka igikorwa ca CoinJoin, twomenya gute ko adashobora guhuza ivyo abakoresha binjiza n’ivyo basohora, ivyo bishobora kuba ari ugusohoka kw’ibanga?


### Imikono y'impumyi ya Chaum


Ivyuma vya CoinJoin vyo muri iki gihe bikoresha imikono y’impumyi ya David Chaum kugira ngo ntihagire amakuru asohoka. Reka twihweze ningoga ingene izo nkuru z’impumyi zikora.


Imikono ya Chaum y’impumyi ni uburyo bw’umukono w’ivyuma aho uwutanga umukono atamenya ibirimwo mu butumwa ariko arashirako umukono. Ariko iyo sinyatire irashobora rero kugenzurwa n’ubutumwa bw’intango. Ubu buhinga bwateguwe n'umuhinga mu vy'amabanga David Chaum mu 1983.


![BTC204](assets/rn/123.webp)


Reka dufate akarorero k’ishirahamwe ryipfuza kwemeza ko inyandiko y’ibanga, nk’akarorero Contract, ari iy’ukuri, ataco rivuze. Iyo sosiyete ikoresha uburyo bwo gupfuka inyandiko y’intango mu buryo bushobora gusubirwamwo. Iyo nyandiko yahinduwe yoherezwa ku kigo kijejwe kwemeza, kigashirako umukono w’impumyi ataco kizi ku birimwo. Iyo sosiyete imaze kwakira iyo nyandiko yashizweko umukono, irafungura iyo nyandiko yashizweko umukono. Ico bivamwo ni inyandiko y’umwimerere yemejwe n’umukono w’ubutegetsi, ata butegetsi bwigeze bubona ibirimwo vy’umwimerere.


Imikono ya Chaum rero ishobora kwemeza ko inyandiko ari iyo ukuri ata muntu azi ibirimwo, gutyo bikaba bituma amakuru y’uwuyikoresha aba ibanga be n’uko iyo nyandiko yashizweko umukono izoba ari iyo kwizera.


### Amafaranga y'i Chaumian


Ivyo bita "Chaumian" coinjoins bifatanya gukoresha imikono ya Tor na David Chaum kugira ngo umuhuzabikorwa ntashobore kumenya igisohoka ari ic'uwukoresha.


Ivy’ubwubatsi bw’ibikorwa vya CoinJoin birimwo intambwe 3 nyamukuru: kwandika ivyinjijwe, kwandika ivy’isohoka n’ugushirako umukono ku bikorwa. Reka turabe iyo nzira biciye ku karorero ka Alice, umwe mu bari muri CoinJoin. Abandi bose bari muri iyo nama bakurikiza intambwe nk’izo Alice ikoresha, umwe wese ku giti ciwe.


**Intambwe ya 1: Kwiyandikisha**




- Alice irungikira umuhuzabikorwa UTXO yipfuza gukoresha nk’inyungu mu gucuruza, hamwe n’ivyo kwakira Address yipfuza gukoresha nk’isohoka kugira ngo aronke ama bitcoins yiwe. Umuhuzabikorwa rero nta buryo afise bwo kumenya Address ya Alice. Ibona gusa verisiyo yiwe y’impuzu:


![BTC204](assets/rn/124.webp)




- Umuhuzabikorwa arasuzuma ko ivyo bintu vyinjijwe ari ukuri, hanyuma agashira umukono ku Alice Address ipfutse n’urufunguzo rwiwe rw’ibanga. Asubiza umukono w’impumyi kuri Alice:


![BTC204](assets/rn/125.webp)


**Intambwe ya 2: Ivyanditswe bisohoka**




- Alice arashobora gufungura Address yiwe, ubu ikaba yashizweko umukono n’urufunguzo rw’ibanga rw’umuhuzabikorwa. Azoshinga uruja n’uruza rushasha munsi y’akaranga ka Tor gatandukanye. Umuhuzabikorwa ntashobora kumenya ko ari Alice ariko arahuza munsi y'akaranga gashasha:


![BTC204](assets/rn/126.webp)




- Alice yohereza Address itagira igipfukisho n’umukono ku muhuzabikorwa (uwutaramenya ko ari Alice):


![BTC204](assets/rn/127.webp)


**Intambwe ya 3: Gusinya amasezerano**




- Mu buryo nk’ubwo, umuhuzabikorwa aratora ibisubizo bitagira amabara ku bari muri iyo nama bose. Biciye ku mikono ijana, arashobora kugenzura ko igisohoka cose yashikirijwe ata wuzi izina ryashizweko umukono n’urufunguzo rwiwe rw’ibanga imbere y’igihe, gutyo akamenya ko ari ivy’ukuri. Araheza rero yiteguriye kwubaka iyo nzira ya CoinJoin, akayirungikira abayigize kugira ngo bayishireko umukono:


![BTC204](assets/rn/128.webp)




- Alice, nk’abandi bari muri iyo nama, arasuzuma ko ivyo yinjiza n’ivyo asohora bishizwe neza mu bikorwa vyubatswe n’umuhuzabikorwa. Iyo vyose bishimishije, yohereza umukono ufungura inyandiko yiwe y’inyungu ku muhuzabikorwa:


![BTC204](assets/rn/129.webp)




- Amaze gukusanya imikono y’abaje muri CoinJoin bose, umuhuzabikorwa arashobora gutangaza iyo nzira ku rubuga rwa Bitcoin, kugira ngo ishobore kwongerwa ku gice.


Muri iyo nzira, umuhuzabikorwa ntashobora guhuza ikintu yinjijwe n’ikintu kinaka gisohoka. Ikindi, ntashobora kwifatira amahera y’abaje mu nama, kuko atigera aronka imfunguruzo z’ibanga zikenewe kugira ngo afungure UTXO zabo. Mu gihe cose, gushika ku mpera y’intambwe ya 3, na we nyene ntashobora gushika ku mikono. Iyo Alice n’abandi bari muri iyo nama bashize umukono ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kw’isi yose, bamaze kugenzura ko vyose bimeze neza, umuhuzabikorwa ntashobora kuzosubira guhindura iyo nzira, harimwo n’ibisohoka, atayihinduye ubusa. Ivyo bituma umuhuzabikorwa adashobora kwiba ama bitcoins.


Ubwa nyuma, igihe yandika umusaruro wiwe mu gucuruza, uwukoresha CoinJoin yipfuza kugira ivyemezo bisa n’ivy’umunyagihugu atora mu matora. Hariho ububiri hagati y’ivyo bikorwa vya bose n’ivy’abikorera ku giti cabo. Ku ruhande rumwe, hari ico ushaka gukingira: ku mutora, ntashaka ko urupapuro rwiwe rw’itora rujanye n’akaranga kiwe; ku mukoresha wa CoinJoin, ntashaka ko igisohoka ciwe gifatanywa n'ico yinjiza. Nkako, iyo umuhuzabikorwa, canke uwundi muntu uwo ari we wese, ashoboye gushinga isano hagati y’ivyo yinjiza n’ivyo asohora, CoinJoin iratakaza inyungu yose. Nk’uko vyasiguwe haruguru, CoinJoin itegerezwa gukora nk’akaruhuko mu mateka ya Coin. Ivyo bihagarara neza na neza kubera ko bidashoboka gufatanya ikintu kinaka n’igisohoka kinaka mu gucuruza CoinJoin (imbere anonset) n’ibihushanye n’ivyo (anonset inyuma).


Ku rundi ruhande, hariho n’ivy’abantu bose: uwutora ashaka kumenya neza ko urupapuro rwiwe rw’itora ruri mu gasandugu k’itora; na vyo nyene, uwukoresha CoinJoin ashaka kumenya neza ko umusaruro wiwe uri mu gucuruza CoinJoin. Nkako, abaje muri CoinJoin bategerezwa kuba bashoboye kugenzura ko umusaruro wabo uriho imbere yo gusinya iyo nzira, ahandi ho umuhuzabikorwa yoshobora kwiba ayo mahera.


Ni vyo nyene ivyo bice 2 vya Leta n’ivy’abikorera ku giti cabo, bishobozwa n’ugukoresha imikono y’impumyi ya David Chaum, bitanga icemezo c’abaje mu bikorwa vya Chaumian coinjoins ko bitcoins zabo zitazokwibwa, kandi ko amahera yabo adashobora gukurikirana.


### Ni nde yahinguye iciyumviro ca CoinJoin?


Ni Hard kuvuga ata gukeka uwabanje gushiramwo iciyumviro ca CoinJoin kuri Bitcoin, n’uwaje n’iciyumviro co gukoresha imikono y’impumyi ya David Chaum muri iki gihe. Kenshi vyiyumvirwa ko ari Gregory Maxwell yabivuze ubwa mbere muri [ubutumwa bwo kuri BitcoinTalk mu 2013](279249.0):


> *"Gukoresha imikono y'impumyi ya Chaum: Abakoresha binjira bagatanga inyishu (n'amaderesi ya Exchange) hamwe n'uburyo bw'ibanga bwa blinded bwa Address bipfuza koherezako UTXO zabo bwite; the server. Server ishobora kubona ko ibisohoka vyose vyashizweko umukono na yo kandi ko, kubera ivyo, ibisohoka vyose biva ku baje mu nama babereye Mu nyuma, abantu barasubira kwifatanya maze bagashirako umukono."*
Maxwell, G. (2013, 22 Myandagaro). *CoinJoin: Bitcoin ubuzima bwite bw'isi nyakuri*. Ihuriro ry'Ibiganiro vya Bitcoin. 279249.0
