![BTC204](assets/rn/130.webp)


Ariko rero, hariho n’ibindi vyavuzwe imbere y’aho, vyose ku mikono ya Chaum nka UTXO y’uguvanga, ariko kandi ku bijanye n’ama coinjoins. [Muri Ruheshi 2011, Duncan Townsend yashize ahabona ku rubuga rwa BitcoinTalk) igikoresho co guvanga gikoresha imikono ya Chaum mu buryo busa cane n’ubw’amafaranga y’iki Chaum yo muri iki gihe.


Muri iyo nkuru nyene, turashobora gusanga [ubutumwa buvuye kuri hashcoin mu kwishura Duncan Townsend] (https. Inzira idondora muri ubu butumwa ni co nyene coinjoins zivuga. Kuvuga uburyo busa n’ubwo birashobora no kuboneka muri [ubutumwa bwa Alex Mizrahi mu 2012](https://github.com/killerstorm/6f843e1d38191aebca67d483bd88#file-laundry) nk’uko mu nyuma ararema Litecoin. Mbere n'ijambo "CoinJoin" ubwaryo bavuga ko ritavuzwe na Greg Maxwell, ahubwo ko ryavuye mu ciyumviro ca Peter Todd.


![BTC204](assets/rn/131.webp)


### Ihuriro rya Zero


Zerolink ni umurongo w’uguvanga wuzuye ushiramwo amafaranga y’i Chaumian n’ingene abakoresha batamenyekana ku buryo bwinshi bwo gusesangura uruhererekane, cane cane mu kugabanya amakosa ajanye n’uburongozi bwa Wallet. Iyi porotokole [yashizweho na nopara73 na TDevD mu 2017].


![BTC204](assets/rn/132.webp)


Nk’uko izina ryayo rivyerekana, ingingo ngenderwako y’inyuma ya Zerolink ni uguhingura amasezerano ya CoinJoin atuma amasano hagati y’ivyo yinjiza n’ivyo asohoka adashobora gukurikirana. Ivyo bishikwako mu kumenya neza ko ibisohoka vyose bifise ingero zisa neza.


![BTC204](assets/rn/133.webp)


Ingingo ihambaye yo kwirinda yafashwe na Zerolink ni ugutuma UTXO zitavanzwe zitandukanye rwose n’izivanzwe hakoreshejwe amafunguro atandukanye y’ubuhinga bwa none, canke mbere n’amasakoshi atandukanye. Ivyo bitandukanya "*pre-mix*" Wallet, igenewe UTXOs imbere y'uko zivangwa, n'"*post-mix*" Wallet, yagenewe UTXOs zavanzwe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/134.webp)


Ukwo gutandukanya gukomeye kw'ama UTXO gufasha canecane gukingira amashirahamwe y'impanuka hagati ya UTXO ivanze n'ita UTXO ivanze. Nkako, iyo mwene ayo mahuriro abayeho, ubushobozi bwa CoinJoin ku UTXO ivanze burakurwaho ata n’umwe ayikoresha abizi, gutyo bikaba bituma ibanga ry’i UTXO yiyumvira ko yacitse intege rihungabana. Ivyo bihuza bishobora kubaho biciye mu gusubira gukoresha Address ku gucungera UTXO ivanze n’iyindi itavanze, canke biciye mu gukoresha CIOH (_Common-Input-Ownership Heuristic_), iyo uwukoresha akoresha UTXOs zivanzwe n’izitavanze nk’ibintu vyinjizwa muri same. Mu gutandukanya amasakoshi y’imbere y’uguvanga n’inyuma y’uguvanga, turirinda mwene ayo mashirahamwe y’impanuka kandi tukarinda uwukoresha amakosa atagamije.


![BTC204](assets/rn/135.webp)


Ukwo gutandukanya kandi gutanga ubushobozi bwo gukoresha amategeko atandukanye hagati y’amasakoshi y’imbere y’uguvanga n’inyuma y’uguvanga ku rugero rwa porogarama ya Wallet. Nk’akarorero, mu gihe c’inyuma y’uguvanga Wallet, porogarama irashobora kubuza gufatanya UTXOs mu bikoresho vy’injiza kugira ngo ntihagire uwukoresha CIOH ikoreshwa, ivyo bikaba vyotuma anonset y’uwukoresha ihungabana. Birashoboka kandi guhuza ikoreshwa ry’inyandiko n’uburyo bwo gukoresha (nk’akarorero, raporo ya RBF) kugira ngo umuntu ntamenyekane n’ibimenyetso vy’intoke vya Wallet.


Ubu, Whirlpool ni yo yonyene ikoresha CoinJoin ikoresha cane umurongo wa Zerolink. Mu gice gikurikira, turaza kuraba uburyo butandukanye bwo gushirwa mu ngiro kwa CoinJoin buriho, n’ivyiza n’ibibi vya buri kimwe cose.


## CoinJoin gushirwa mu ngiro


<chapterId>e37ed073-9498-4e4f-820b-30951e829596</chapterId>



**Mu mwaka w'2024, turiko turabona amahinduka akomeye mu bikoresho biriho ku bakoresha bipfuza gukora coinjoins kuri Bitcoin. Ubu turi mu gihe c'ihinduka, kandi isoko rya CoinJoin ririko rihindurwa cane. Iki gice nta gukeka ko kizosubirwamwo uko igihe kigenda kirarenga**


Kugeza ubu hariho ahanini 3 bitandukanye CoinJoin gushirwa mu ngiro kuri Bitcoin:




- Whirlpool;
- Ababisabi;
- Injira mw'Isoko.


Imwe muri izo nzira zigamije guca amateka y’ama UTXO biciye mu bikorwa vya CoinJoin. Ariko rero, uburyo bikoreshwa buratandukanye cane. Ni ngombwa rero gutahura ingene kimwe cose gikora, kugira ngo ushobore guhitamwo uburyo bubereye ivyo ukeneye.


### Kwinjira mw'isoko


JoinMarket, yashinzwe mu 2015 na Adam Gibson na Chris Belcher, iratandukanye cane n’izindi nzira za CoinJoin kubera uburyo bwayo bwihariye bwo guhuza abakoresha. Ubuhinga bushingiye kw'isoko rya P2P Exchange aho abakoresha bamwebamwe, "abakora", batuma amafaranga yabo ya bitcoins ashobora gukoreshwa mu guvanga, mu gihe abandi, "abafata", bakoresha ayo mahera kugira ngo bakore ama coinjoins mu gusubiza amahera.


![BTC204](assets/rn/136.webp)


Muri iki kigereranyo, "abahinguzi" baratuma ama bitcoins yabo ashikirizwa "abayafata" kandi bagaronka amahera y'igikorwa cabo. Ababifata na bo nyene bariha kugira ngo bakoreshe amafaranga y’abahinguzi kugira ngo bakore ibikorwa vyabo vy’ubudandaji vya CoinJoin. Amafaranga y'ibikorwa aratandukanye bivanye n'uruhara umuntu afise: "abakora" barundanya amafaranga yo gutanga amafaranga, mu gihe "abafata" bariha amafaranga. Isoko rikora mu mwidegemvyo, ata n’itegeko ryo gukoresha.


Kimwe mu bitera ingorane nyinshi JoinMarket ni uko ikoreshwa neza, ivyo bikaba bisaba urugero runaka rw’uguhumurizwa n’ibikoresho vyo gukoresha kugira ngo ikore neza. Naho ivyo bigoranye atari intambamyi ku muntu azi gukoresha, birashobora gutuma abantu bose badashobora kubironka. Ariko rero, ubu hakaba hariho urubuga rwa Interface rwitwa JAM, rwatumye rworoha gatoyi gukoresha.


![BTC204](assets/rn/137.webp)


Inkomoko: [JAM](https://github.com/isoko-ry'urubuga/jam/ibara/iterambere/inyandiko/itunga/ishusho-ry'umwiza.urubuga)


Ariko rero, intambamyi y’ubuhinga iracari intambamyi ikomeye. Mu bidukikije vya CoinJoin, aho ibanga rikomezwa n’umubare w’abaje mu nama, uburenganzira bwose bugabanya ubushobozi bwo kuronka amakuru buragira ingaruka zitaziguye ku mahera ariho, ari co kintu gihambaye cane mu gutuma iyo nzira ikora neza. Bitcoin, kuba isanzwe ari ikibanza mu bikorwa vy’amahera, ibona ko ikoresha coinjoins nk’ikibanza gitoyi, kandi JoinMarket iserukira mbere n’igice kidasanzwe cayo, ivyo rero bikaba bigabanya ubushobozi bwayo bwo kwongera anonsets z’abakoresha bayo.


Naho ifise ubuhinga bushasha bwo guhuza P2P ku ba coinjoiners, JoinMarket irafise ingorane zikomeye, cane cane mu bijanye n’imiterere y’ibikorwa. Udakunze izindi nzira zo gushirwa mu ngiro nka Whirlpool, JoinMarket ntiyizera uburinganire butunganye hagati y’ibisohoka, kandi birashoboka gukurikirana amasano y’ivy’ubuhinga hagati y’ibisohoka n’ibisohoka. Ikindi kandi, nta bikoresho ifise vyo kubuza ko ama UTXO amaze kuvangwa hamwe yosubira kuvangwa, ivyo bikaba vyoshobora gutuma ibanga abakoresha barondera rihungabana.


Ubwa nyuma, naho iciyumviro ca JoinMarket gishimishije cane cane ku bakunda isoko ry’amahera ry’inguvu, intege nke zaryo z’imiterere n’ubuhinga bwaryo butoroshe bituma, mu vyiyumviro vyanje, kidashimishije cane abashasha n’abahinga barondera ugushirwa mu ngiro kwa CoinJoin.


### Wabisabi


Wabisabi ni uwundi murongo wa CoinJoin, ufise uburyo bushira hamwe uguhuza ibikorwa. Ico kigereranyo cavumbuwe na Ádám Ficsór (nopara73), Yuval Kogman, Lucas Ontivero, na István András Seres mu 2021, hanyuma gishirwa muri porogarama ya Wasabi 2.0 umwaka wakurikiyeho. Wabisabi ni iterambere ry'ubuhinga bwa Wasabi CoinJoin bwatangujwe mu 2018.


![BTC204](assets/rn/138.webp)


Mu mpera z'imyaka ya 2010, Wasabi yaremeye uburyo bwo gucuruza butandukanye cane na CoinJoin n'ubwa Whirlpool. Wasabi yakoresheje amafaranga menshi cane ya CoinJoin arimwo abantu amajana n’amajana kugira ngo yongere amakuru y’abayigize. Mu buryo bunyuranye, Whirlpool yahisemwo gukora ibikorwa bitobito vyinshi, bikaba vyatumye anonsets zikura cane uko inzira igenda irahinduka.


Uburyo bwo gucunga Exchange na bwo nyene bwatandukanije izo nzira zibiri zo gushirwa mu ngiro. Na Whirlpool, ihinduka ryakuwemwo kandi ryitandukanijwe n’ama UTXO imbere y’ingendo za CoinJoin kubera TX0, iciyumviro nzosigura cane mu kigabane gikurikira. Ku rundi ruhande, na Wasabi, iryo hinduka ryaciye rigira kimwe mu biva mu gucuruza CoinJoin, rigumya amasano y’ugushinga intahe hagati y’ibintu bimwebimwe vyinjizwa n’ibisohoka.


![BTC204](assets/rn/139.webp)


Na Wabisabi, Wasabi verisiyo 2.0 yarahinduye uburyo bwayo bwo gukoresha amafaranga kugira ngo ihure n'iya Whirlpool. Naho amafaranga y’ubudandaji ya CoinJoin aguma ari manini cane, ubu birashoboka gukora uruzitiro rw’ingendo nyinshi zikurikirana, hakurikijwe uburyo bwa Whirlpool. n’ugucungera ibiciro vya Exchange vyarashizweho umutima cane: bitandukanye na Wasabi 1.0, aho ihinduka ryari rifitaniye isano n’ivyo abakoresha bashiramwo, Wabisabi irondera gucapura iryo hinduka mu mahera makeyi menshi, agabanywemwo amashengero angana ku bari muri iyo nama bose.


Reka tubigereranye n'akarorero koroshe karimwo abakoresha 2 gusa: Alice yipfuza kuvanga 115.000 Sats na Bob, 210.000 Sats. Ukwirengagiza amafaranga, na Wasabi 1.0, ugucuruza kwa CoinJoin kwari gutuma haba ibisubizo 3 vy'ama Sats 100.000, hakongerwako ihinduka 1 ry'ama Sats 15.000 ku Alice n'ihinduka 1 ry'ama Sats 10.000 ku Sats. Ihinduka ry'ibisohoka ryoba rigihuye n'ivyo kwinjiza:


![BTC204](assets/rn/140.webp)


Mu gihe ca Wabisabi, iyo nzira nyene yari gutuma haba ibisohoka 3 vy’amashanyarazi 100.000 Sats n’ibisohoka 5 vy’amashanyarazi 5.000 Sats, gutyo bigatuma iryo hinduka rishira ku buryo ritashobora guhuzwa ata guca ku ruhande n’inyungu yihariye:


![BTC204](assets/rn/141.webp)


Ku bwanje, mbona ko uburongozi bw’amahinduka bwa Wabisabi bufise ingorane nyinshi zishobora gutuma bukora nabi mu bijanye n’ibanga:




- Iyo uwukoresha atanga UTXO nini cane kuruta iyo abandi bari muri iyo nama, nta kabuza aheza akagira amahera y’ihinduka azohuzwa n’ivyo atanga. Ivyo bihushanye n’intumbero y’intango y’iyo porotokole, ari yo gukuraho amahinduka yose ashobora kumenyekana;
- Ukwiyongera kw’amashengero n’intumbero yo guca ibice ihinduka birashobora kuba bibi mu buryo buteye ubwoba ku bijanye n’uguvanga neza. Ivyo bishobora gutuma habaho ukugabanya anonsets ku bisohoka bimwebimwe, uko bigenda vyoroshe kumenyekana;
- Ubu buryo kandi buratuma habaho UTXO z’agaciro gato zitera ingorane y’uburongozi ku wukoresha. Izo UTXO ntoya, iyo zizimvye cane ku buryo zidashobora gukoreshwa mu bijanye n'agaciro kazo, zishobora kuba "Dust". Ico kintu gituma uwukoresha afatanya UTXO nyinshi mu vyo gukoresha mu gukora ibikorwa vyo muri kazoza, canke akabifatanya. Muri ivyo bihe vyose, kubera CIOH, ivyo birashobora kugabanya amakuru y’ibanga yaronswe, canke bikakuraho burundu inyungu z’ibanga zaronswe na CoinJoin ya mbere.


Udakunze Whirlpool, ishira mu ngiro umurongo wa ZeroLink utuma habaho itandukaniro rikomeye hagati y’imbere y’uguvanga n’inyuma y’uguvanga, Wabisabi ntigumya ukwo gutandukanya gukomeye. Hari kandi ingorane zo gusubira gukoresha Address n’abaguzi bamwebamwe ba Wasabi, ivyo bikaba bigaragara ko bitera ingorane cane uwuyikoresha.


Mu verisiyo ya Wasabi 2.0, hashizweho ingingo nshasha y’amahera CoinJoin. Kuva ubu, amafaranga y’umuhuzabikorwa ashirwa kuri 0,3% ku ma UTXO ari hejuru ya 0,01 Bitcoin, mu gihe ku ma UTXO mato, ayo mafaranga atangwa mu buryo bushitse. Ikindi, guhindura indirimbo z’izo UTXO ntoyi ni ubuntu, naho amafaranga Mining aguma arihwa n’uwukoresha ku bikorwa vyose, harimwo n’uguhindura indirimbo.


Ivyo bitandukanye n’ingingo ya Whirlpool, aho amahera aguma ari amwe, ata kuraba ubunini bw’ama annonsets abonetse. Na Wasabi 2.0, naho amafaranga y’umuhuzabikorwa arekurwa ku ma UTXO mato, uwukoresha aracari ategerezwa kwishura amafaranga Mining ku bikorwa vyose, harimwo n’ivyo guhindura.


Uko ndiko ndandika iyi mirongo, ikoreshwa ry’ururimi rwa Wabisabi ryarateye imbere cane kubera ibintu biherutse kuba. Inyuma y’aho abashinze Samourai Wallet bafashwe, zkSNACKs, ishirahamwe ritanga amahera kandi rirongora iterambere rya Wasabi, ryatangaje ko igikorwa caryo co guhuza ibikorwa vya CoinJoin kizohagarara kw’igenekerezo rya 1 Ruheshi 2024.


Kubera ko uwo muhuzabikorwa mukuru ahagaritse, abakoresha ubu bategerezwa kwifatanya n’abahuzabikorwa bashasha bigenga. Iryo hinduka rituma habaho ivyiyumviro bitari bike: ku ruhande rumwe, abahuzabikorwa bashasha boshobora kutagira amahera ahagije, bikagabanya ubushobozi bw’ama coinjoins mu bijanye n’ibanga. Ku rundi ruhande, hariho ingorane yo guhura n’umuhuzabikorwa w’umunyaruyeri. Ivyo birongereza ingorane nshasha zikomeye ku barondera gukoresha Wabisabi.


Uretse ibibazo vy’ubuhinga, ingingo ya zkSNACKs, ishirahamwe riri inyuma ya Wasabi, yo gukoresha ubuhinga bw’ishirahamwe ry’ugusesangura imirongo kugira ngo icungurure abaje muri CoinJoin, iravyura ibibazo bikomeye bijanye n’inyifato runtu n’ingene ingamba zizokorwa. Iciyumviro ca mbere cari co kubuza abagizi ba nabi gukoresha ama coinjoins kuri Wasabi, ivyo bikaba ari ibintu bishobora gusa n’ibibereye. Ariko rero, biravyura ikintu kidasanzwe: kwishura amahera umuhuzabikorwa afise igikorwa nyamukuru co gukomeza ibanga ry’abakoresha, gusa kugira ngo ashobore gufasha ishirahamwe rifise intumbero yo guhungabanya iryo banga nyene.


N’ikindi giteye amaganya ni ingingo ngenderwako y’ugucungera, itandukanye cane n’ubuhinga bwa Bitcoin bwo gutanga uburyo bw’ivy’ubutunzi bufunguye kandi butagenzurwa. Naho vyosa n’ibibereye gushaka gukuraho ibikorwa vy’ubugizi bwa nabi, ukwo kuyungurura kwoshobora kandi gukora ku bantu ibikorwa vyabo, naho nyene bifatwa nk’ibitemewe n’amategeko mu bihe bimwebimwe, bishobora kuba bifise ishingiro mu vy’inyifato runtu canke bifise akamaro ku kibano. Akarorero ka Edward Snowden karerekana neza iyo ntambara: abonwa n’intwaro zimwe zimwe nk’umugizi wa nabi kubera ivyo yahishuriwe, abandi bamubona nk’umuntu atangaza amakuru y’abantu, akora ibintu ku bw’inyungu za bose. Ivyo bigoranye birashimika ku kaga gashobora guterwa n’ukuyungurura, naho nyene bifise intumbero nziza, bishobora gutuma uburenganzira n’umutekano w’abakoresha bibereye bihungabana. Nari gushobora no kuvuga abaharanira uburenganzira bw’abantu n’abanyamakuru batotezwa n’intwaro zimwe zimwe z’ubutegetsi bw’agahomerabunwa.


Nk'uko muzoba mwabikoranye ubu, ivyo nkunda ni vy'ukuri Whirlpool model ku coinjoins kuri Bitcoin. Uwo murongo uratandukanye n’uwukomeye cane kandi uratanga ivyizigiro vyiza kuruta ibindi vyose vy’uko umuntu azoba afise ibanga. Ni ryo ryonyene kandi ritanga uruvange rubonwa ko rutunganye mu bijanye n’imibare. Mu vyiyumviro vyanje, iki kigereranyo kigereranya kazoza k'ama coinjoins kuri Bitcoin. Ndabatumiye ngo musuzume iyo nzira mu buryo bwimbitse mu kigabane gikurikira.


## Uko Whirlpool ikora


<chapterId>bdbd7109-e36d-4b4f-a3c6-928df4e9bfda</chapterId>



Igitandukanya Whirlpool n'ubundi buryo bwa CoinJoin ni ugukoresha ibikorwa vya "_ZeroLink_", bituma ata sano ry'ubuhinga rishoboka hagati y'ibintu vyose vyinjizwa n'ibisohoka. Uwo muvumba utunganye ushikwako biciye mu nzira aho umwe wese mu bari muri iyo nama atanga umubare ungana (uretse amafaranga y’ama Mining), bikaba bitanga umusaruro w’amahera angana neza.


Ubwo buryo bwo kubuza ivyinjizwa buha ibikorwa vya Whirlpool vya CoinJoin ikintu kidasanzwe: ukubura kwose kw’amasano y’ivyinjira hagati y’ibishirwamwo n’ibisohoka. Mu yandi majambo, igisohoka cose gifise amahirwe angana yo gushirwa ku muntu wese afise uruhara, ugereranije n’ibindi bisohoka vyose biri mu gucuruza.


![BTC204](assets/rn/142.webp)


### Uko Whirlpool ikora


Mu ntango, igitigiri c’abaje muri Whirlpool CoinJoin imwe imwe cari 5, harimwo abashasha 2 n’abasubiramwo 3 (ivyo vyiyumviro tuzobisigura mu nyuma). Ariko rero, ukwo kwiyongera kw’amahera y’ugucuruza On-Chain kwabonetse mu 2023 kwatumye amashirahamwe ya Samourai asubira kwiyumvira uburyo bwabo bwo gutuma ibanga ry’abantu ryiza mu gihe bagabanya ibiciro. Gutyo, hakurikijwe uko isoko ry’amahera rimeze be n’umubare w’abazoja muri iyo nama, umuhuzabikorwa arashobora ubu gutegura ama coinjoins harimwo abazoja muri iyo nama 6, 7 canke 8. Ivyo biganiro vy'iterambere bizwi nka "Imirongo y'Ivyiyumviro". Ni vyiza kumenya ko, uko imiterere yoba iri kwose, hama hariho gusa 2 bashasha binjira muri Whirlpool coinjoins.


Gutyo, ibikorwa vya Whirlpool birangwa n’umubare usa w’ibintu vyinjizwa n’ibisohoka, bishobora kuba:




- 5 vyinjizwa n’ibisohoka 5;


![BTC204](assets/rn/143.webp)




- 6 vyinjizwa n’ibisohoka 6;


![BTC204](assets/rn/144.webp)




- 7 vyinjizwa n’ibisohoka 7;


![BTC204](assets/rn/145.webp)




- 8 vy’injiza n’ivy’isohoka 8.


![BTC204](assets/rn/146.webp)


Icogereranyo ca Whirlpool gishingiye ku bikorwa bitobito vya CoinJoin. Udakunze Wabisabi na JoinMarket, aho ubukomezi bw’ibimenyetso bishingiye ku bwinshi bw’abaje mu nzinguzingu imwe (canke ku nzinguzingu nkeyi), Whirlpool yizigira urutonde rw’inzinguzingu ntoyi nyinshi.


Muri iki kigereranyo, abakoresha bariha amahera gusa igihe babanza kwinjira mu kidengeri, bikaba bituma bashobora kuja mu bikorwa vyinshi vy’ugusubiramwo ataco baciye. Abashasha binjira bariha amahera ya Mining ku ba remixer.


Igihe cose CoinJoin yongeweko igice kimwe kirimwo, hamwe n’urunganwe rwaco rwahuye na rwo mu bihe vya kera, anonsets zizokura cane. Intumbero ni ugukoresha neza izo remixes z’ubuntu, igihe cose zishitse, zifasha mu gukomeza uburemere bw’ama anonsets ajanye n’igice cose kivanze.


![BTC204](assets/rn/147.webp)


Whirlpool yakozwe ifise mu muzirikanyi ibintu bibiri bihambaye bisabwa:




- Ugushika ku gushirwa mu ngiro ku bikoresho vy’amaboko, kubera ko Samourai Wallet ari mbere na mbere porogarama ya telefone ngendanwa;
- Ivyiyumviro vyihuta vyo gusubiramwo kugira ngo biteze imbere ukwiyongera gukomeye kw’ibihimba vy’umubiri.


Ivyo bintu vy’ingenzi ni vyo vyarongoye amahitamwo yakozwe n’abahinguzi ba Samourai Wallet mu guhingura Whirlpool, bituma bafata ingingo yo guhagarika abazoja muri iyo nama ku rugero rutoyi ku nzinguzingu. Bake cane bari gutuma ubushobozi bwa CoinJoin buhungabana, bagagabanya cane anonsets ziterwa n’ingendo, mu gihe benshi cane boba barateye ingorane z’uburongozi ku bikorwa vy’amatelefone ngendanwa no gutuma ingendo igenda neza.


Ubwa nyuma, nta nkenerwa yo kugira umubare munini w'abaje mu nama ku CoinJoin kuri Whirlpool, kuko anonsets zikorwa ku kwirundanira kw'ingendo nyinshi za CoinJoin. Ingingo ngenderwako ihambaye cane aha ni uguhuza kw’ama UTXO y’abaje mu nama bose, kuko ivyo bituma habaho ukuvanga gutunganye, bigatuma habaho inyungu yuzuye mu nzira zo kuvanga no gusubira kuvanga.


### CoinJoin ibidengeri n'amahera


Kugira ngo izo nzira nyinshi zongere anonsets z’ama UTXO avunganye, birakenewe ko habaho uburyo bumwe bwo kugabanya ingano z’ama UTXO akoreshwa. Whirlpool isobanura ibidengeri bitandukanye.


Igikarabiro giserukira umugwi w’abakoresha bipfuza guvanga hamwe, bemeranya ku rugero rw’ama UTXO azokoreshwa mu gutuma uburyo bwa CoinJoin bugenda neza mu gihe bagumana ubumwe butunganye bwa UTXO. Ico kigega cose kigaragaza umubare udahinduka wa UTXO, uwo uwukoresha ategerezwa kwubahiriza kugira ngo agire uruharamwo. Rero, kugira ngo ukore coinjoins na Whirlpool, ukeneye guhitamwo ikidengeri. Ivyo bidengeri bikurikira biraboneka ubu:




- 0.5 amafaranga y’ibiceri;
- 0,05 Bitcoin;
- 0,01 Bitcoin;
- 0,001 Bitcoin (= 100.000 Sats).


Iyo winjiye mu kidengeri n’amahera yawe ya bitcoins, azogabanywa gushika ku generate UTXOs zihuye neza n’iz’abandi bari muri ico kidengeri. Buri kidengeri gifise urugero rwo hejuru, rero ku mafaranga arenga uwo mupaka, uzobwirizwa gukora ivyinjizwa bibiri bitandukanye mu kidengeri kimwe, canke wimukire mu kindi kidengeri gifise umubare munini:


| Pool (bitcoin) | Maximum amount per entry (bitcoin) |
|----------------|------------------------------------|
| 0.5            | 35                                 |
| 0.05           | 3.5                                |
| 0.01           | 0.7                                |
| 0.001          | 0.025                              |

UTXO ifatwa nk'iy'ikidengeri iyo yiteguye gushirwa muri CoinJoin. Ariko rero, ivyo ntibisigura ko uwuyikoresha atakaza uburenganzira bwo kuyigira. Nk’uko twabibonye mu bice vya mbere vy’iki gice, biciye mu nzira zitandukanye zo guvanga, uguma ufise ububasha bwose ku mfunguruzo zawe, kandi, kubera ivyo, ku ma bitcoins yawe. Ivyo ni vyo bitandukanya ubuhinga bwa CoinJoin n’ubundi buhinga bwo guvanga bushizwe hamwe.


Kugira ngo winjire mu gice ca CoinJoin, ukeneye kwishura amahera y’ibikorwa n’amahera ya Mining. Amafaranga y’ibikorwa arashirwaho ku kidengeri cose kandi agamije guhemba amashirahamwe ashinzwe gutegura no gucungera Whirlpool.


Amafaranga y’ibikorwa vyo gukoresha Whirlpool arihwa rimwe gusa iyo winjiye mu kidengeri. Iyo umaze kwinjira, urashobora kuja mu bikorwa vy’ugusubiramwo ibintu bitagira aho bigarukira ataco wishuye. Akira amafaranga adahinduka y’ubu ku kidengeri cose:


| Pool (bitcoin) | Entry fee (bitcoin) |
|----------------|---------------------------------|
| 0,5 | 0,0175 |
| 0,05 | 0,00175 |
| 0.01 | 0.0005 (50,000 sats) |
| 0.001 | 0.00005 (5,000 sats) |

Aya mahera akora nk'itike yo kwinjira mu kidengeri wahisemwo, utitaye ku mahera ushize muri CoinJoin. Rero, waba winjiye muri pool ya 0.01 ufise neza na neza 0.01 BTC canke 0.5 BTC, amafaranga azoguma ari amwe mu buryo bushitse.


Imbere yo gukomeza na Whirlpool coinjoins, umukoresha ashobora guhitamwo hagati y'ingene 2:




- Hitamwo ikidengeri gitoyi kugira ngo agabanye amafaranga y’ibikorwa, azi ko azoronka UTXO ntoyi nyinshi mu gusubiza;
- Canke uhitemwo ikidengeri kinini, ushaka kwishura amahera menshi, gusa ugaheza ukagira umubare mutoyi w’ama UTXO y’agaciro kanini.


Muri rusangi si vyiza gufatanya UTXO nyinshi zivanzwe inyuma y'ingendo za CoinJoin, kuko ivyo bishobora gutuma ibanga ryaronswe rihungabana, cane cane kubera inyungu rusangi ya Ownership (CIOH: *Common-Input-Ownership-Heuristic*). Ku bw’ivyo, bishobora kuba vyiza guhitamwo ikidengeri kinini, naho ivyo vyoba bisobanura kwishura vyinshi, kugira ngo ntihagire ama UTXO menshi cane y’agaciro gatoyi mu vyo asohora. Uwukoresha ategerezwa gusuzuma ivyo bihembo kugira ngo ahitemwo ikidengeri akunda.


Uretse amahera y’ibikorwa, amahera ya Mining yihariye ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kwose kwa Bitcoin na yo nyene ategerezwa gufatwa mu mutwe. Nk'ukoresha Whirlpool, uzosabwa kwishura amafaranga Mining ku bijanye n'ugutegura (`Tx0`) hamwe n'amahera ya CoinJoin ya mbere. Ivyo vyose bizokurikira bizoba ari ubuntu, bivuye ku citegererezo ca Whirlpool gishingiye ku kwishura abashasha binjira.


Nkako, muri Whirlpool CoinJoin imwe imwe, abakoresha 2 mu vyo bashiramwo ni abashasha binjira. Ibindi bishirwamwo biva ku ba remixer. Ivyo bituma amafaranga y’indirimbo za Mining ku bantu bose bari muri iyo nzira y’ugucuruza yishurwa n’abo bashasha 2, na bo nyene bagashobora kwungukira ku vyo guhindura indirimbo ku buntu:


![BTC204](assets/rn/148.webp)


Kubera iyo nzira y’amahera, Whirlpool vy’ukuri iratandukanye n’izindi nzira za CoinJoin, kuko anonsets za UTXOs zidahuye n’igiciro umuntu akoresha yishuye. Ivyo bituma bishoboka ko umuntu ashika ku rwego rwo hejuru cane rwo kutamenyekana mu kwishura gusa amahera yo kwinjira mu kidengeri n’amahera ya Mining ku bikorwa 2 (ivyo `Tx0` n’ivy’intango).


Ni vyiza kumenya ko uwukoresha azobwirizwa kandi kwishura amahera ya Mining kugira ngo akure UTXOs ziwe mu kidengeri amaze kurangiza coinjoins ziwe nyinshi, kiretse yahisemwo `mix to` option, itanga Address yo hanze izoronka amahera ataco akoresheje CoinJoin, ata transaction.


### Konti za HD Wallet


Kugira ngo ureme CoinJoin biciye kuri Whirlpool, Wallet itegerezwa generate amakonti menshi atandukanye. Iryo ni ryo hame riri inyuma y’itegeko rya ZeroLink. Inkuru, mu rwego rwa HD (*Hierarchical Deterministic*) Wallet, igize igice gitandukanye rwose n’ibindi, ukwo gutandukana kuba ku rugero rw’uburebure bwa gatatu bw’ubukuru bwa Wallet, ni ukuvuga ku rugero rwa `xpub`.


![BTC204](assets/rn/149.webp)


HD Wallet ishobora mu vyiyumviro gushika ku `2^(31)` inkuru zitandukanye. Konti y'intango, ikoreshwa ku buryo busanzwe ku bikoresho vyose vya Bitcoin, ihuye n'urutonde rwa `0'`.


Ku bikoresho vy’amahera bihuye na Whirlpool, amakonti 4 arakoreshwa kugira ngo haboneke ivya nkenerwa mu nzira ya ZeroLink:




- Konti ya **ibiziga**, igaragazwa n'urutonde `0'`;
- Konti ya **banki mbi** (canke "ihinduka rya doxxic"), igaragazwa n'urutonde `2.147.483.644'`;
- Konti ya **imbere**, igaragazwa n'urutonde `2 147 483 645'`;
- Konti ya **inyuma**, igaragazwa n'urutonde `2 147 483 646'`.


Imwe muri izo nkuru irarangura igikorwa kinaka mu nzira ya CoinJoin, ivyo tuzobisuzuma mu bice bikurikira.


Izo konti zose zihuye na seed imwe, zituma uwuzikoresha ashobora gusubira kuronka amafaranga yiwe yose akoresheje ijambo ryiwe ryo gusubira kuronka, aho bishoboka, passphrase yiwe. Ariko rero, mu gihe c’igikorwa co gusubiza ibintu, iyo porogarama itegerezwa kumenyeshwa urutonde rw’amakonti atandukanye yakoreshejwe.


Reka turabe intambwe zitandukanye z’igikoresho ca Whirlpool CoinJoin muri izo nkuru.


### Ivyo TX0.


Intango ya Whirlpool CoinJoin iyo ari yo yose ni konti ya **ibiziga**. Iyi ni konti ukoresha ubwawe iyo uremye Bitcoin Wallet nshasha. Iyi konti izokenera gushirwamwo ama bitcoins wipfuza guvanga.


Tx0" ni intambwe ya mbere mu nzira yo guvanga Whirlpool. Intumbero yayo ni ugutegura no kuringaniza UTXOs za CoinJoin, kuzigabanya mu bice bihuye n'ingero y'ikidengeri catowe, kugira ngo habeho ukuvanga guhuye. As UTXOs rero ziringanijwe ni **the**mi ntishobora kwinjira mu kidengeri, itandukanijwe muri konti yihariye: **banki mbi** (canke "ihinduka rya doxxic").


Iryo soko rya mbere `Tx0` rikoreshwa kandi mu kwishura amahera y’ibikorwa akwiye guhabwa umuhuzabikorwa wa CoinJoin. Mu buryo butandukanye n’intambwe zikurikira, iyo nzira y’ugucuruza ntabwo ari iyo gukorana, rero uwuyikoresha ategerezwa kwikorera igiciro cose ca Mining:


![BTC204](assets/rn/150.webp)


Muri aka karorero k’ugucuruza `Tx0`, inyungu ya `372,000 Sats` iva kuri konti yacu ya **deposit** igabanywamwo UTXO nyinshi zisohoka, zica zigabanywa gutya:




- Amafaranga `5.000 Sats` ku muhuzabikorwa ku mafaranga y’ibikorwa, ahuye n’injira mu kidengeri `100.000 Sats`;
- 3 UTXOs zateguwe kugira ngo zivanzwe, zisubirwamwo kuri konti yacu ya **premix** zigaca ziyandikisha ku muhuzabikorwa. Izo UTXO zingana ku `108.000 Sats` imwe yose, kugira ngo zishobore kwishura amafaranga Mining y’umuvango wazo w’intango wo muri kazoza;
- Ivyo bisigaye, bidashobora kwinjira mu kidengeri kubera ko ari bito cane, bifatwa nk’ihinduka ry’ubumara. Irungikwa kuri konti yayo yihariye. Aha, iryo hinduka rishika kuri `40.000 Sats`;
- Ubwa nyuma, hariho `3.000 Sats` zisigaye, zitari umusaruro, ariko ni ibiciro vya Mining bisabwa kugira ngo umuntu yemeze `Tx0`.


Nk’akarorero, ng’iyi Whirlpool Tx0 nyayo (si iyanje): [edef60744f539483d868caff49d4848e5cc6e805d6cdc8d0f9bdbbaedcb5fc46](https://GW- 851.ikibanza/tx/edef60744f539483d868caff49d4848e5cc6e805d6cdc8d0f9bdbbaedcb5fc46)


![BTC204](assets/rn/151.webp)


### Ivyo doxxic birahinduka


Ivyo bitari bishobora gushirwa muri iyo nzira, aha bingana na `40.000 Sats`, birungikwa kuri konti ya **banki mbi**, izwi kandi kw'izina rya "doxxic change", kugira ngo habeho ugutandukana gukomeye n'izindi UTXO ziri muri Wallet.


Iyi UTXO irateye akaga ku ibanga ry’uwuyikoresha, kuko ntabwo iguma ifatanye n’ivya kera vyayo gusa, kandi rero bishoboka ko ifatanye n’akaranga ka nyen’iyo UTXO, ariko kandi igaragara ko ari iy’uwuyikoresha yakoze CoinJoin.


![BTC204](assets/rn/152.webp)


Iyo iyo UTXO ifatanijwe n’ibisohoka bivanze, iyo ya nyuma izotakaza ibanga ryose ryaronswe mu gihe c’ingendo za CoinJoin, cane cane bivuye kuri CIOH (*Common-Input-Ownership-Heuristic*). Iyo ifatanijwe n’ibindi bihinduka vya doxxic, uwuyikoresha arashobora gutakaza ibanga, kuko izohuza ivyinjizwa bitandukanye vy’ingendo ya CoinJoin. Ni co gituma rero umuntu akwiye gufatwa n’ubwenge. Tuzoja mu buryo burambuye ku bijanye n’uburongozi bw’izo UTXOs doxxic mu gice ca nyuma c’iki gice.


### Ivangura ry'intango


Inyuma ya `Tx0`, UTXOs zingana zirungikwa kuri konti yacu ya Wallet **premix**, ziteguye gushirwa mu nzira ya mbere ya CoinJoin, izwi kandi nk'"imivumba y'intango". Iyo, nk’uko biri mu karorero kacu, `Tx0` ivyara UTXO nyinshi zo guvanga, imwe yose muri zo izoshirwa mu mvange y’intango itandukanye.


Ivyo bivanze vya mbere biheze, konti ya **premix** izoba iri ubusa, mu gihe ibiceri vyacu, bimaze kwishura amafaranga y’i Mining y’iyi CoinJoin ya mbere, bizohindurwa neza neza ku rugero rwasobanuwe n’ikidengeri catowe. Mu karorero kacu, UTXO zacu za mbere za `108.000 Sats` zizoba zagabanutse zibe nyazo `100.000 Sats`.


![BTC204](assets/rn/153.webp)


### Gusubiramwo


Inyuma y’imivumba ya mbere, ama UTXO aca yimurirwa kuri konti ya **postmix**. Iyi konti ikorakoranya ama UTXO amaze guvangwa n’ayo arindiriye gusubira kuvangwa. Iyo umukiriya wa Whirlpool ariko arakora, UTXO ziri muri konti ya **postmix** zica ziboneka ubwazo kugira ngo zisubirwemwo kandi zizotorwa mu buryo bw’impfagusa kugira ngo zigire uruhara muri izo nzira nshasha.


Nk’ukwibutsa, remixs rero ziraba ku buntu 100%: nta yindi mice y’ibikorwa canke amahera ya Mining asabwa. Kugumiza UTXOs muri konti ya **postmix** rero bituma agaciro kazo kagumaho, kandi bigatuma anonsets zazo zitera imbere muri ico gihe nyene. Ni co gituma bihambaye kwemera ko ivyo biceri bigira uruhara mu nzira nyinshi za CoinJoin. Ntaco bigutwara na gato, kandi birongereza ingero zabo zo kutamenyekana.


Iyo ufashe ingingo yo gukoresha UTXOs zivanzwe, ushobora kubikora uhereye kuri iyi konti ya **postmix**. Turaguhanura ko woguma ufise ama UTXO avanze muri iyi konti kugira ngo wungukire ku ma remix y’ubuntu no kuyabuza kuva mu nzira ya Whirlpool, ivyo bishobora kugabanya ibanga ryayo.


### None ama postmix yanyu muyacungera gute?


Inyuma yo gukoresha inzinguzingu za CoinJoin, ubuhinga bwiza ni ugutuma UTXO zawe ziguma muri konti ya **postmix**, urindiriye gukoreshwa muri kazoza. Ni vyiza mbere ko ubireka bikagira remix ubuziraherezo gushika ukeneye kubikoresha.


Abakoresha bamwe bamwe boshobora kwiyumvira kwimurira amafaranga yabo ya bitcoins ku Wallet icungiwe na Hardware Wallet. Ivyo birashoboka, ariko birahambaye gukurikiza neza impanuro za Samourai Wallet kugira ngo ntihagire uwuhungabanya ibanga ryaronswe.


Gufatanya ama UTXO ni ryo kosa risanzwe. Kugira ngo wirinde CIOH (*Ivyinjira-Rusangi-Ownership-Heuristic*), utegerezwa kwirinda gufatanya UTXO zivanzwe n’izitavanze mu gucuruza kumwe. Ivyo bisaba gucunga neza ama UTXO yawe ari muri Wallet yawe, cane cane mu bijanye no gushirako amazina.


![BTC204](assets/rn/154.webp)


Hategerezwa kandi kwitwararikwa igihe umuntu ariko arashiramwo ama UTXO avunganye. Gushiramwo ibintu bimwe bimwe birashoboka iyo UTXO zawe zivanzwe zifise anonsets zihambaye, ariko ivyo bizogabanya ata kabuza ibanga ry’ama UTXO yawe. Raba neza ko ugushiramwo ibintu bitari vyinshi cane, canke ngo bikorwa inyuma y’umubare udahagije w’ibintu bisubirwamwo, mu kaga ko gushinga amasano ashobora gukurwako hagati y’ama UTXO yawe imbere n’inyuma y’ingendo za CoinJoin. Iyo ufise amakenga ku bijanye n’ivyo bikoresho, igikorwa ciza ni ukudashiramwo ama UTXO y’inyuma, ahubwo ni ukuyarungika imwe imwe kuri Hardware Wallet yawe, ugatanga Address nshasha y’ubusa igihe cose. Na none, wibuke kwandika kuri UTXO yose uronka.


Si vyiza kandi kwimurira ama UTXO yawe ya postmix kuri Wallet ukoresheje inyandiko zidakoreshwa cane. Nk'akarorero, niwinjiza Whirlpool uvuye kuri Multisig Wallet ukoresheje inyandiko `P2WSH`, nta mahirwe make yo kuvangwa n'abandi bakoresha bari bafise ubwoko bumwe bwa Wallet. Iyo usubiye guvanga ama postmixes yawe kuri iyi Multisig Wallet nyene, urugero rw’ibanga ry’ama bitcoins yawe yavanzwe ruzogabanywa cane. Uretse inyandiko, hariho n’ibindi bimenyetso vyinshi vy’intoke vya Wallet bishobora kugukinira.


Nk'uko bigenda ku bikorwa vyose vya Bitcoin, birahambaye kandi ko udasubira gukoresha Address yakira. Igihe cose umuntu atanga amafaranga, ategerezwa kwakirwa ku rupapuro rushasha rwa Address rudafise ikintu.


Umuti woroshe kandi utekanye ni ugusiga UTXO zawe zivanzwe ziruhutse muri konti yabo ya **postmix**, ukazireka zikora remix kandi ukazikorako gusa kugira ngo zikoreshe. Samurai na Sparrow wallets zifise uburinzi bwongereweko ku bibazo vyose vyo gusesangura uruzitiro. Ivyo bintu bigukingira biragufasha kwirinda gukora amakosa.


### None muvyifatamwo gute mu gucungera amahinduka y’ubumara?


Igikurikira, uzokenera kwitwararika uburongozi bwawe bw’ihinduka rya doxxic, ihinduka ritashitse mu kidengeri ca CoinJoin. Izo UTXO zitera ubumara, ziterwa n’ugukoresha Whirlpool, zitera ingorane ubuzima bwite bwawe, kuko zishinga ubucuti hagati yawe n’uwukoresha CoinJoin. Ni ngombwa rero ko tuzicungera neza kandi ntituzifatanye n’izindi UTXO, cane cane UTXO zivanzwe.


Akira ingamba zimwe zimwe zo kubikoresha:




- Bivange mu bidengeri bitobito: Nimba UTXO yawe y'ubumara ari nini cane ku buryo ishobora kwinjira mu kidengeri gitoyi ubwayo, nuzirikane kuyivanga. Akenshi ivyo ni vyo vyiza kuruta ibindi vyose. Ariko rero, si vyiza gufatanya UTXO nyinshi zitera ubumara kugira ngo ushikire ikidengeri, kuko ivyo bishobora guhuza ivyinjijwe vyawe bitandukanye;
- Bishireko ikimenyetso c'uko "bidashobora gukoreshwa": Ubundi buryo ni ukubihagarika, ubishireko ikimenyetso c'uko "bidashobora gukoreshwa" muri konti yabo yihariye, na HODL gusa. Ivyo bituma udashobora kubikoresha mu mpanuka. Iyo agaciro ka Bitcoin kaduze, ibidengeri bishasha bibereye cane UTXO zawe zitera ubumara birashobora guseruka;
- **Gutanga intererano:** Niwiyumvire gutanga intererano, naho yoba ari nto gute, ku bahinga bakora kuri Bitcoin n'amaporogarama ajanye na yo. Ushobora kandi gutanga amahera ku mashirahamwe yemera BTC. Nimba gucunga UTXO zawe zitera ubumara bisa n'ibigoye cane, urashobora gusa kuzikuramwo maze ugatanga intererano;
- **Gura amakarita y'ingabirano:** Ivyuma nka [Bitrefill](https://www.bitrefill.com/) biguha uburenganzira bwo gukoresha amafaranga Exchange ku makarita y'ingabirano ashobora gukoreshwa ku badandaza batandukanye. Ivyo bishobora kuba uburyo bwo gutandukana n'ama UTXO yawe y'ubumara utatakaje agaciro kajana;
- Bishire hamwe kuri Monero: **Samourai Wallet** itanga ubuhinga bwo guhindura atome hagati ya BTC na XMR. Ivyo ni vyiza cane mu gucunga UTXOs zitera ubumara mu kuzishira kuri Monero, ataco zihinduye ku ibanga ryawe biciye kuri CIOH, imbere yo kuzisubiza kuri Bitcoin. Ariko rero, iyo nzira ishobora gutwara amahera menshi mu bijanye n'amahera ya Mining n'amahera y'imbere kubera ingorane z'amahera;
- Birungike kuri Lightning Network: Kwimurira izo UTXO kuri Lightning Network kugira ngo zironke inyungu ku mahera y'ugucuruza agabanutse birashobora kuba uburyo bukwegera. Ariko rero, ubu buryo burashobora guhishura amakuru amwamwe bivanye n'ingene ukoresha Lightning, kandi rero ukwiye kubukoresha witonze.


### Nokoresha gute Whirlpool?


Inyuma y’aho abashinze Samourai Wallet bafashwe, bagafata ama server yabo ku wa 24 Ndamukiza 2024, igikoresho ca Whirlpool ntikigikora, mbere n’abafise Dojo yabo bwite. Mbere, yari iboneka ku ndege za Samourai Wallet na Sparrow wallet.


![BTC204](assets/rn/155.webp)


Ariko rero, birashoboka ko ico gikoresho cosubira gukoreshwa mu ndwi ziza, bivanye n’ivyo ibigeragezo bizovamwo, canke kigasubira gukoreshwa mu buryo butandukanye. Uko biri kwose, sinibaza ko isoko rya Bitcoin CoinJoin rizoba ritagira Supply igihe kirekire, kuko ubukene buriho. Ikindi, nk’uko uburyo bwa Whirlpool ari bwo buteye imbere cane mu bijanye n’ibanga, nta gukeka ko buzoba uburyo bwo guhitamwo ku bindi bikorwa vyo gushirwa mu ngiro muri kazoza.


Turaguma twihweza cane iki kibazo n'iterambere mu bikoresho bijanye naco. Nimwizere ko tuzoba turiko turasubiramwo iri shure uko amakuru mashasha azoba ariko araboneka.


Mu gice gikurikira, tuzomenya ivyo "anonsets" ari vyo, ingene ivyo bimenyetso biharurwa, n'ingene bishobora kudufasha kugereranya ubushobozi bw'ingendo za CoinJoin.




https://planb.network/tutorials/privacy/on-chain/coinjoin-samourai-wallet-e566803d-ab3f-4d98-9136-5462009262ef



## Ivy'ukutamenyekana


<chapterId>be1093dc-1a74-40e5-9545-2b97a7d7d431</chapterId>



Tumaze kwiga ingene coinjoins zikora n’ibibazo bijanye no guvanga neza, ubu tugiye kumenya ingene twopima ubushobozi bwazo. Twomenya gute nimba uburyo bwo gukorana n’abandi bwabaye bwiza, kandi ni urugero rungana iki UTXO yaronse mu kutamenyekana? Ivyo nivyo tuzomenya muri iki gice n'ibice vy'amazina canke "anonsets".


### Ivyibutsa akamaro ka CoinJoin .


Akamaro ka CoinJoin kari mu bushobozi bwayo bwo gutanga ukwihakana kwemewe, mu gushiramwo UTXO yawe mu mugwi w’ama UTXO adashobora gutandukanywa. Intumbero y’ico gikorwa ni uguca amahuzu y’ugukurikirana, kuva muri kahise gushika muri iki gihe, kuva muri iki gihe gushika muri kahise.


Mu yandi majambo, umusesanguzi azi igikorwa cawe ca mbere (`Tx0`) ku kwinjira kw’ingendo za CoinJoin ntakwiye kuba ashoboye kumenya ata gukeka UTXO yawe ku gusohoka kw’ingendo za remix (isesengura ry’injira ry’ingendo gushika ku gusohoka kw’ingendo).


![BTC204](assets/rn/156.webp)


Ku rundi ruhande, umusesanguzi azi UTXO yawe ku gusohoka kw’ingendo za CoinJoin ategerezwa kuba adashobora kumenya igikorwa c’intango ku kwinjira kw’ingendo (isesengura ry’isohoka ry’ingendo gushika ku kwinjira kw’ingendo).


![BTC204](assets/rn/157.webp)


Kugira ngo dusuzume ingene bigoye umusesanguzi guhuza kahise n’ubu n’ibihushanye n’ivyo, turakeneye gupima ubunini bw’imigwi y’ama UTXO amwe UTXO yawe yihishije. Ico gipimo kitubwira ingene isesengura ryinshi rifise ubushobozi bumwe. Rero, iyo isesengura ryiza ryorohamye hagati y’izindi isesengura 3 zifise ubushobozi bungana, urugero rwawe rwo kwihisha ruri hasi cane. Ku rundi ruhande, iyo isesengura ryiza riboneka mu rwego rw’isesengura 20.000 rishobora kuba ringana, UTXO yawe iranyegejwe neza cane. Ubwinshi bw'ayo matsinda bugereranya ibimenyetso bizwi nka "anonsets".


### Gutahura ibintu bitamenyekana


Anonsets zikoreshwa nk'ibimenyetso vyo gusuzuma urugero rw'ibanga rya UTXO. Mu buryo butomoye, bapima igitigiri c’ama UTXO adashobora gutandukanywa mu gice kirimwo UTXO iriko irigwa. Igisabwa kugira ngo habeho umugwi umwe w’ama UTXO bisigura ko anonsets zisanzwe ziharurwa ku nzira za CoinJoin. Ikoreshwa ry’ivyo bimenyetso rirahambaye cane cane ku bipimo vya Whirlpool, kubera ukuntu bihuye.


Niba ari ngombwa, anonsets zishobora gukoreshwa mu gucira urubanza uburyo coinjoins zimeze. Anonset nini bisigura urugero rwo hejuru rw’ukutamenyekana, kuko bigorana gutandukanya UTXO yihariye mu rwego rw’ibintu bimwe.


2 ubwoko bw'ibimenyetso bihari:




- Imbere anonset;
- gusubira inyuma.


### Imbere anonset


Ivyo bimenyetso vyerekana ubunini bw’umugwi UTXO yigishijwe mu mpera y’ingendo yihishije, bishingiye kuri UTXO mu ntango, ni ukuvuga umubare w’ama UTXO adashobora gutandukanywa ari muri uwo mugwi. Izina ry'iki kigereranyo ni "ibipimo vy'imbere".


Ico kigereranyo gipima ukuntu ibanga ry’icumba rishobora guhangana n’isesengura ry’ivya kera n’ivya none (input-to-output).


![BTC204](assets/rn/158.webp)


Iyi metric ikoreshwa mu kugereranya urugero UTXO yawe irindwako ku kugerageza gusubira kwubaka amateka yayo kuva aho yinjira gushika aho isohokera mu nzira ya CoinJoin.


Nk'akarorero, nimba igikorwa cawe cagize uruhara mu nzira ya mbere ya CoinJoin kandi izindi nzira zibiri zimanuka zikaba zarangiye, imbere ya Coin yawe yoba `13`:


![BTC204](assets/rn/159.webp)


Nk'akarorero, reka twiyumvire ko Coin yacu mu ntango y'ingendo ya CoinJoin ifise anonset y'imbere ya `86,871`. Mu majambo y’ibikorwa, ivyo bisigura ko ryihishijwe mu `86.871` UTXO zidashobora gutandukanywa. Ku muntu yihweza hanze azi iyo Coin mu ntango z’ingendo za CoinJoin akagerageza gukurikirana aho isohoka, azohura n’ibishobora kuba UTXO `86.871`, imwe yose ikaba ifise ubushobozi busa n’ubwo yo kuba ari yo Coin ariko ararondera.


![BTC204](assets/rn/160.webp)


### Ivyo gusubira inyuma


Inyuma anonset yerekana umubare w’amasoko ashoboka ku UTXO yatanzwe, kumenya UTXO ku mpera y’ingendo. Iki kigereranyo gipima ukuntu ibanga rya UTXO rishobora guhangana n’isesengura ry’ubu n’ivya kera (isohoka-ku-injiza), ni ukuvuga ingene bigoye umusesanguzi gukurikirana UTXO yawe gushika aho yakomotse, imbere y’ingendo za CoinJoin. Izina ry'iki kimenyetso ni "ugusubira inyuma", canke "ibipimo vy'inyuma".


![BTC204](assets/rn/161.webp)


Mu kumenya UTXO yawe ku gusohoka kw’ingendo, anonset y’inyuma igena umubare w’ibikorwa vya Tx0 bishobora kuba vyatumye winjira mu nzira za CoinJoin. Mu kigereranyo kiri aha hepfo, ivyo bihuye n’umubare w’ibibumbano vyose vy’umukara.


![BTC204](assets/rn/162.webp)


Nk'akarorero, reka twiyumvire ko CoinJoin UTXO yacu ifise `42,185`. Mu majambo y'ukuri, ivyo bisigura ko hariho `42.185` amasoko ashobora gukoreshwa muri iyi UTXO. Iyo umuntu wo hanze abona iyo Coin ku mpera y’ingendo maze akarondera gukurikirana inkomoko yayo, azohura n’amasoko ashoboka `42.185`, yose afise amahirwe angana yo kuba ari yo nkomoko ironderwa.


![BTC204](assets/rn/163.webp)


### None muharura gute ama anonsets?


Birashoboka kubara anonsets n'amaboko ukoresheje Block explorer ku bice bitobito. Ariko rero, ku bimenyetso bininibinini, gukoresha igikoresho kidasanzwe biraba ngombwa cane. Nk’uko ndabizi, porogarama imwe rudende ishobora gukora ico gikorwa ni *Whirlpool Stats Tool*, igikoresho ca Python cakozwe n’imigwi ya Samourai na OXT. Ikibabaje ni uko ubu iki gikoresho kitagikora inyuma y’ugufatwa kw’abashinze Samourai no guhagarika OXT, yakoreshwa mu gukura amakuru muri Blockchain.


![BTC204](assets/rn/164.webp)


Nk’uko twabibonye muri iki kigabane, anonsets zishobora kubarwa gusa iyo hariho ubumwe bumwe bumwe mu miterere ya CoinJoin. Mu kigabane gikurikira, tuzobona ingene twogereranya ubwo bumwe ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kwa Bitcoin, yaba ari ugucuruza kwa CoinJoin canke ugucuruza kwa kera.




## Entropi


<chapterId>e4fe289d-618b-49a2-84c9-68c562e708b4</chapterId>



Nk’uko twabibonye muri iki gice ku bijanye n’ama coinjoins, ubumwe bw’ama UTXO mu vyo kwinjiza no mu gusohora birafise uruhara runini mu gutuma ibanga ry’ugucuruza rya Bitcoin ritera imbere. Iyi parametere irema uguhakana gushobora kwemerwa mu gihe c’isesengura rya Blockchain. Uburyo bwinshi burashobora gukoreshwa mu gupima ubwo bumwe, ariko bumwe mu bukora neza cane, mu vyiyumviro vyanje, ni ugukoresha ibimenyetso bitangwa n’igikoresho ca *Boltzmann*, categuwe n’imigwi ya OXT na Samourai Wallet, na cane cane entropie y’ugucuruza. Ivyo nivyo tuzoba turiko turaraba mu buryo burambuye muri iki kigabane.


Mu buryo butandukanye n’ama anonsets, abarirwa ku rutonde rw’ibikorwa, ibimenyetso vyerekanywe ngaha vyibanda ku bikorwa bimwe, haba CoinJoin canke ibikorwa vya kera.


### Umubare w'insobanuro


Ikimenyetso ca mbere gishobora kubonwa ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kwa Bitcoin ni umubare wose w’insobanuro zishoboka zihura n’isesengura rivuye ku muntu yihweza hanze. Hakurikijwe agaciro k’ama UTXO ari muri iyo nzira, iki kigereranyo kirerekana umubare w’uburyo ivyo kwinjiza bishobora gufatanywa n’ivyo gusohoka. Mu yandi majambo, igena umubare w’insobanuro zishoboka igikorwa gishobora gutanga mu nzira za Bitcoin zivuye ku mbonerahamwe y’umuntu wo hanze ariko arayisuzuma.


Nk'akarorero, igikorwa co kwishura gisanzwe gifise inyungu 1 n'inyungu 2 kizogira insobanuro imwe gusa, ni ukuvuga ko inyungu #0 itanga amafaranga umusaruro #0 n'inyungu #1. Nta yindi nsobanuro ishoboka:


![BTC204](assets/rn/165.webp)


Ku rundi ruhande, imfuruka ya Whirlpool 5x5 ifise $1\,496$ y’imigwi ishoboka:


![BTC204](assets/rn/166.webp)


Igikoresho ca Whirlpool gifise insobanuro zishoboka:


![BTC204](assets/rn/167.webp)


### Entropi


Dufatiye ku mubare w’insobanuro z’isoko rya Bitcoin, turashobora kubara entropie yaryo.


Mu bijanye n’ubuhinga bwo gukingira amakuru n’amakuru, entropi ni ingero y’ingero y’ukudakeka canke ukudashobora kumenya imbere y’igihe bifitaniye isano n’inkomoko y’amakuru canke inzira y’imburakimazi. Mu yandi majambo, entropie ni uburyo bwo gupima ingene amakuru agoye gutegekanya canke gutekereza ku bintu.


Mu bijanye n’isesengura rya Blockchain, entropi ni izina ry’ikigereranyo, rikomoka ku entropi ya Shannon kandi [yavumbuwe na LaurentMT], gishobora kubarwa ku nzira ya GW-54.


Iyo igikorwa c’ugucuruza kigaragaje insobanuro nyinshi zishoboka, kenshi birabereye cane kwerekeza ku ntungamubiri zaco. Ico kigereranyo gipima ubukene bw’ubumenyi bw’abasesangura ku bijanye n’imiterere nyayo y’ugucuruza. Mu yandi majambo, uko entropie igenda irakura, ni ko bigorana ko abasesangura bamenya ingene amafaranga y’ibice vy’agaciro (bitcoins) agenda hagati y’ivyo yinjiza n’ivyo asohoka.


Mu bikorwa, entropi ihishura nimba, uhereye ku mbonerahamwe y’umuntu wo hanze, igikorwa gitanga insobanuro nyinshi zishoboka, zishingiye gusa ku mibare y’injiza n’isohoka, ataco zizirikana ku bindi bigereranyo vyo hanze canke vyo mu mutima n’ubuhinga bwo kumenya ibintu. Entropie nini rero ni co kimwe n’ibanga ryinshi ry’ugucuruza.


Entropie isobanurwa nk’umubare w’ibintu bishobora guhurizwa hamwe. Ehe formule ikoreshwa na $E$ entropie y'ugucuruza na $C$ umubare w'insobanuro zishoboka:


$$
E = \log_2(C)
$$


Mu mibare, logarithme ya binaire (logarithme ya base-2) ni igikorwa gihinduka c’ugutera imbere kwa 2. Mu yandi majambo, logarithme ya binaire ya $x$ ni igiharuro $2$ itegerezwa guterwako kugira ngo umuntu aronke $x$. Ico kimenyetso rero kigaragazwa mu bice.


Reka dufate akarorero k’uguharura entropie ku gikorwa ca CoinJoin gitunganijwe hakurikijwe uburyo bwa Whirlpool 5x5, nk’uko vyavuzwe mu gice ca mbere, bufise umubare w’insobanuro zishoboka z’amadolari 1\,496$:


$$
\begin{align*}
C &= 1\,496 \\
E &= \log_2(1\,496) \\
E &= 10.5469 \text{ bits}
\end{align*}
$$


Gutyo, iyo nzira ya CoinJoin ifise entropie y’ibice vy’amadolari 10,5469$, ivyo bikaba bibonwa ko bishimishije cane. Uko ako gaciro karushiriza kuba kanini, ni ko n’insobanuro zitandukanye iyo nzira yemera, gutyo bigakomeza urugero rw’ibanga ryayo.


Ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kwa CoinJoin 8x8 n’insobanuro z’amadolari 9\,934\,563$, entropi yoba:


$$
\begin{align*}
C &= 9\,934\,563 \\
E &= \log_2(9\,934\,563) \\
E &= 23.244 \text{ bits}
\end{align*}
$$


Reka dufate akandi karorero n'ugutanga amahera kwa kera, n'injiza 1 n'isohoka 2: 1b1b0c3f0883a99f1161c64da19471841ed12a1f78e77fab128c69a5f578ccce] 950.ikibanza/tx/1b1b0c3f0883a99f1161c64da19471841ed12a1f78e77fab128c69a5f578ccce)


![BTC204](assets/rn/168.webp)


Mu bijanye n'iyi nzira, insobanuro yonyene ishoboka ni: `(Mu.0) > (Inyuma.0; Inyuma.1)`. Ku bw’ivyo, entropie yayo ni $0$:


$$
\begin{align*}
C &= 1 \\
E &= \log_2(1) \\
E &= 0 \text{ bits}
\end{align*}
$$


### Umwimbu


Hashingiwe ku entropie y’isoko, turashobora kandi kubara ubushobozi bwaryo mu bijanye n’ibanga. Ico kigereranyo gisuzuma ubushobozi bw’ugucuruza mu kugereranya n’ugucuruza kwiza kwoshobora gutegurwa mu ntunganyo isa.


Ivyo bituma tugera ku ciyumviro c’uburemere burengeye ubundi bwose, buhuye n’uburemere burengeye ubundi bwose umubumbe w’ubudandaji wihariye ushobora gushikako mu vyiyumviro. Ubushobozi bw’ugucuruza buraheza buharurwa mu kugereranya iyo entropie n’intropie nyayo y’ugucuruza biriko birasesangurwa.


Formule ikoreshwa ni iyi ikurikira na:




- $e_R$: entropie nyayo y'ugucuruza igaragazwa mu bice;
- $e_M$: entropie ishoboka cane ku miterere y'ibikorwa, nayo igaragazwa mu bice;
- $Ef$: ubushobozi bwo gucuruza mu bice:


$$
Ef = E_R - E_M
$$


Nk’akarorero, ku gishushanyo ca Whirlpool 5x5 CoinJoin, uburemere burengeye ubundi bwose ni $10.5469$:


$$
\begin{align*}
E_R &= 10.5469 \\
E_M &= 10.5469 \\
Ef &= E_R - E_M \\
Ef &= 10.5469 - 10.5469 \\
Ef &= 0 \text{ bits}
\end{align*}
$$


Ico kigereranyo na co nyene kigaragazwa nk’ijanisha. Uburyo bukoreshwa ni ubu::




- $c_R$: umubare w'insobanuro nyazo zishoboka;
- $c_M$: umubare munini w'insobanuro zishoboka z'imiterere imwe;
- $Ef$: ubushobozi bugaragazwa nk'ijanisha:


$$
\begin{align*}
E_f &= \frac{C_R}{C_M} \\
E_f &= \frac{1\,496}{1\,496} \\
E_f &= 100 \%
\end{align*}
$$


Ubushobozi bw’amadolari 100$ bwerekana ko iyo nzira iriko irakoresha neza ubushobozi bwayo bwo kuba ibanga, bivanye n’imiterere yayo.


### Uburemere bwa entropi


Entropie ni ikimenyetso ciza co gupima ibanga ry’isoko, ariko bivana n’igice c’umubare w’ibintu vyinjizwa n’ibisohoka mu gikorwa. Kugira ngo tugereranye entropie y’ibikorwa 2 bitandukanye n’imibare itandukanye y’ibintu vyinjizwa n’ibisohoka, turashobora kubara uburemere bw’entropie. Ico kigereranyo kiratanga iciyumviro ku bijanye n’uburemere bw’ibintu (entropie) bujanye n’ivyo umuntu yinjiza canke asohora vyose vy’ugucuruza. Uburemere ni ngirakamaro mu gusuzuma no kugereranya ubushobozi bw’ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji vy’ubunini butandukanye.


Kugira ngo tuyiharure, tugabanya gusa entropie yose y’isoko n’umubare wose w’ibintu vyinjizwa n’ibisohoka biri muri iyo soko:




- $e_D$: uburemere bw'uburemere bugaragazwa mu bice;
- $e$: entropie y'ugucuruza igaragazwa mu bice;
- $t$: umubare wose w'ibintu vyinjijwe n'ibisohoka mu gucuruza:


$$
E_D = \frac{E}{T}
$$


Reka dufate akarorero k’indege y’umuyagankuba 5x5:


$$
\begin{align*}
T &= 5 + 5 = 10 \\
E &= 10.5469 \\
E_D &= \frac{E}{T} \\
E_D &= \frac{10.5469}{10} \\
E_D &= 1.054 \text{ bits}
\end{align*}
$$


Reka kandi tubaze uburemere bw’uburemere bw’ibintu 8x8 Whirlpool CoinJoin:


$$
\begin{align*}
T &= 8 + 8 = 16 \\
E &= 23.244 \\
E_D &= \frac{E}{T} \\
E_D &= \frac{23.244}{16} \\
E_D &= 1.453 \text{ bits}
\end{align*}
$$


Mu gusuzuma uburemere bw'uburemere bw'ubwo bwoko bubiri bwa CoinJoin, biragaragara ko, mbere n'igihe umuntu asanura entropi n'umubare wa Elements, "Surge Cycle 8x8" CoinJoin itanga ukudakeka kwinshi ku bijanye n'isesengura.


### Igitego ca Boltzmann


Iyindi nkuru isesengurwa mu gucuruza ni igiharuro ca Boltzmann c’ikintu cose kigereranywa n’ikindi. Iyi ni imbonerahamwe y’uguhuza ibishoboka hagati y’ibishirwamwo n’ibisohoka. Iyi mbonerahamwe yerekana, biciye ku manota ya Boltzmann, ubushobozi bw’ibintu vy’uko ikintu kinaka gifitaniye isano n’igisohoka. Ni ingero rero y’ingero y’ibishoboka vy’uko hariho isano hagati y’inyungu n’isohoka mu gucuruza, rishingiye ku rugero rw’umubare w’ibintu vyiza vyabaye muri ico kintu n’umubare wose w’ibintu bishobora kuba, mu rutonde rw’insobanuro.


Ukoresheje akarorero ka Whirlpool CoinJoin, imbonerahamwe y’ibishoboka yoshobora kwerekana amahirwe y’ihuriro hagati y’ivyo umuntu yinjiza n’ivyo asohora, igatanga ingero y’ingero y’ukudasobanuka kw’amashirahamwe mu gucuruza:


| %       | Output 0 | Output 1 | Output 2 | Output 3 | Output 4 |
| ------- | -------- | -------- | -------- | -------- | -------- |
| Input 0 | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      |
| Input 1 | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      |
| Input 2 | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      |
| Input 3 | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      |
| Input 4 | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      | 34%      |


Biragaragara ko ikintu cose umuntu yinjiza gifise amahirwe angana yo gufatanya n’ikintu cose gisohoka, ivyo bikaba bikomeza ibanga ry’ivyo bicuruzwa.


Igitigiri ca Boltzmann giharurwa mu kugabanya igitigiri c’insobanuro ikintu kinaka kibamwo n’igitigiri cose c’insobanuro ziriho. Gutyo, kugira ngo tumenye igiharuro gihuza inyungu #0 n’isohoka #3 (ikintu kiri mu nsobanuro z’amadolari 512$), duca dukora gutya:


$$
\begin{align*}
\text{Interpretations (IN.0 > OUT.3)} &= 512 \\
\text{Interpretations totales} &= 1496 \\
\text{Score} &= \frac{512}{1496} \\
\text{Score} &= 34 \%
\end{align*}
$$


Nitwafata akarorero k’Igikoresho ca Whirlpool 8x8 CoinJoin, imeza ya Boltzmann yoba imeze gutya:


| OUT.0 | OUT.1 | OUT.2 | OUT.3 | OUT.4 | OUT.5 | OUT.6 | OUT.7 |
|-------|-------|-------|-------|-------|-------|-------|-------|
| IN.0  | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   |
| IN.1  | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   |
| IN.2  | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   |
| IN.3  | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   |
| IN.4  | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   |
| IN.5  | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   |
| IN.6  | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   |
| IN.7  | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   | 23%   |


Ariko rero, ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kworoshe gufise ikintu kimwe co kwinjiza n’ivyo gusohora 2, ibintu biratandukanye:


| Output 0 | Output 1 |
|----------|----------|
| Input 0  | 100%     | 100%    |


Aha, turabona ko ubushobozi bw’isohoka ryose riva ku nkuru #0 ari 100%. Gutyo, ubushobozi buke bwerekana ibanga rikomeye, bugatuma amasano ataziguye hagati y’ivyo yinjiza n’ivyo asohoka agenda aragabanuka.


### Amahuza y'ivyemezo


Turashobora kandi kubara umubare w’amahuza y’ivy’ubuhinga mu gucuruza. Ico kigereranyo kigaragaza ingene amasano ari hagati y’ivyo yinjiza n’ivyo asohoka mu bikorwa vy’ubudandaji vyasuzumwe ataco ashidikanyako, afise ubushobozi bwo gushika ku 100%. Ico kigereranyo gishobora rero kurangira mu kubara igipimo c’amahuza y’ivy’ubuhinga. Ico kigereranyo gitanga iciyumviro ku buremere bw’ayo mahuza y’ivy’ubuhinga mu mahuza yose y’ugucuruza.


Nk’akarorero, igikorwa ca Whirlpool CoinJoin nta sano ry’ivy’imbere hagati y’ibintu vyinjizwa n’ibintu bisohoka, rero kigaragaza ikimenyetso c’amasano 0 n’igipimo ca 0%. Ku rundi ruhande, mu bikorwa vyacu vya kabiri vy’ukwishura vyoroshe vyasuzumwe (n’inyungu imwe n’isohoka 2), ikimenyetso kitubwira ko hariho amahuzu 2 y’ugushinga intahe, kandi igiharuro kigera ku 100%. Mu yandi majambo, ikimenyetso ca zero kigaragaza ibanga ryiza cane, bivuye ku kutagira amasano ataziguye kandi atagira aho ahengamiye hagati y’ivyo umuntu yinjiza n’ivyo asohora.


### None ivyo bimenyetso mubiharura gute?


Guharura ivyo bimenyetso n’amaboko hakoreshejwe ingano natanze biragoye cane. Ingorane iri ahanini mu kumenya igitigiri c’insobanuro zishoboka z’ugucuruza. Ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kwa kera, iyo mibare ishobora gukorwa n’ukuboko. Ariko rero, ku ndege yitwa CoinJoin, ico gikorwa kiragoye cane kuruta.


Mbere, hariho igikoresho ca Python citwa _Boltzmann Calculator_, cakozwe n’imigwi ya OXT na Samourai, kikaba cari giharura ubwaco ivyo bimenyetso vyose ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kwa Bitcoin:


![BTC204](assets/rn/169.webp)


Vyari bishoboka kandi gukoresha urubuga rwa KYCP.org kugira ngo hakorwe izo nseguro:


![BTC204](assets/rn/170.webp)


Ikibabaje ni uko inyuma y’aho abashinze Samourai bafashwe, ivyo bikoresho ntibigikora.


Ubu ko twavuze coinjoins mu buryo burambuye, turaza kuraba ubundi buryo bwo gukingira ubuzima bwite buboneka kuri Bitcoin mu gice ca nyuma c’inyigisho yacu. Tuzoba turiko turaraba payjoins, ubwoko bwihariye bw’ibikorwa vy’ubuhinga bwa pseudo-CoinJoin, amasezerano ya Address adahinduka, hamwe n’ingero zo gukomeza ibanga atari ku rugero rw’ibikorwa ubwavyo, ariko ku rugero rw’uruzitiro rw’ibice.


https://planb.network/tutorials/privacy/analysis/boltzmann-entropy-738e45af-18a6-4ce6-af1a-1bf58e15f1fe

# Gutahura ingorane z'ubundi buryo buteye imbere bwo gukingira ibanga .


<partId>19989ae6-d608-4acf-b698-2cf1e7e5e6ae</partId>


## Ibikorwa vya PayJoin


<chapterId>c1e90b95-f709-4574-837b-2ec26b11286f</chapterId>



CoinJoin ubu ni uburyo bwiza bwo kwinjiza ukudakeka mu gukurikirana UTXOs mu gusesangura uruhererekane. Nk’uko twabibonye mu bice vyabanje, kugira ngo umuntu aronke uruvange rukora cane, ivyo yinjiza n’ivyo asohora bitegerezwa kuba bimwe uko bishoboka kwose. Ikindi, birahambaye ko UTXOs zishirwa mu mugwi munini uko bishoboka kwose kugira ngo anonsets zibe nyinshi. Rero, kugira ngo coinjoins zibe nziza, zitegerezwa kuba zirimwo umubare munini w’ama UTXO amwe. Ivyo bisabwa vyinshi bisigura ko amasezerano ya CoinJoin afise urutonde rukomeye cane: amafaranga ashirwaho imbere y’igihe, kandi abaje mu nama bose bategerezwa kuyakurikiza kugira ngo uburyo bwo gukora bube bumwe. Ikindi, coinjoins zisaba ko haba uguhuza hagati y’abaje mu nama bose n’umuhuzabikorwa mu gihe c’ubwubatsi bw’ibikorwa.


Ivyo bisabwa bituma CoinJoin idakwiriye kwishurwa ataco ihinduye. Nk’akarorero, nimba ufise 1M Sats Coin mu kidengeri ca CoinJoin, kuyikoresha ataco uhinduye nk’ukwishura vyoba bigoye. Vyosaba gukorana n’abandi bari muri iyo nama be n’umuhuzabikorwa kugira ngo wubake igikorwa co gukorana neza na neza mu gihe ukeneye kwishura, kandi amahera yo kugura yobwirizwa guhura neza n’agaciro k’igitabu cawe ca Coin, ivyo bikaba ari ibintu bidashoboka. Ibikorwa vya CoinJoin rero ni ibikorwa vy'ugukubura vy'ubufatanye, ni ukuvuga ko akenshi ari bo nyene bafise ivyo twinjiza dusanga mu bisohoka.


Ariko rero, vyoba vyiza hagizwe imiterere y’ugucuruza ituma amahera ashobora kwishurwa mu buryo bukora, mu gihe nyene bizana amakenga mu gusesangura uruhererekane. Ivyo nyene ni vyo tuzoba turiko turaraba muri iki kigabane no mu kindi gikurikira.


### None igikorwa ca PayJoin ni iki?


PayJoin ni uburyo bwihariye bwo gukoresha Bitcoin butera imbere ubuzima bwite bw’abakoresha igihe bakoresha amahera mu gukorana n’uwuronka amahera.


Mu mwaka w'2015 niho LaurentMT yavuga ubwa mbere kuri ubwo buryo mw'izina rya "*ibikorwa vy'ubudandaji*", nk'uko bigaragara mu nyandiko iriho . [hano] (aha] (inyandiko y'ivyo bikoresho). Ubu buhinga bwaje gukoreshwa n’indege yitwa Samourai Wallet, mu mwaka w’2018 ni yo yabaye umukiriya wa mbere yabushize mu ngiro akoresheje igikoresho ca Stowaway. Iciyumviro ca PayJoin kiraboneka kandi muri [BIP79], [BIP78](Ubg.Bitcoin/BIPs/blob/master/BIP-0078.mediawiki), na [BIP77](Ubg-979.org/docs/ingene-bikora/PayJoin-v27W-G). Amajambo menshi rero arakoreshwa mu kwerekeza kuri PayJoin:



- PayJoin;
- Umunyabiziga;
- P2EP (*Ukwishura-ku-Iherezo*);
- Ivy’ugucuruza ivy’ubuhinga.


Ikintu kidasanzwe ca PayJoin kiri mu bushobozi bwayo bwo gukora generate igikorwa kigaragara nk’igisanzwe iyo ukibonye ubwa mbere, ariko mu vy’ukuri ni mini CoinJoin hagati y’abantu babiri. Kugira ngo ivyo bishoboke, urutonde rw’ugucuruza rushiramwo uwuronka amahera mu vyo yinjiza iruhande y’uwurungika vy’ukuri. Uwuronka rero ashiramwo amahera yishura hagati mu vyo akora ivyo ubwavyo bikaba bimushoboza kwishurwa.


Reka dufate akarorero kugira ngo dutahure neza iyo nzira. Alice igura umukate ku 4.000 Sats ikoresheje UTXO y’10.000 Sats maze ihitamwo PayJoin. Umutetsi wiwe, Bob, yongerako UTXO y'ama Sats 15.000 yari yiwe nk'ivyo yinjiza, akayigarura yose nk'ivyo asohora, yongerako 4.000 Sats ya Alice.


![BTC204](assets/rn/171.webp)


Muri aka karorero, Bob umutetsi yinjira 15.000 Sats mu kwinjira agasohoka afise 19.000 Sats, itandukaniro rikaba ari 4.000 Sats nyavyo, ni ukuvuga igiciro c’umukate w’umukate. Ku ruhande rwa Alice, yinjira 10.000 Sats agaheza akagira 6.000 Sats mu vyo akora, ivyo bikaba bigereranya -4.000 Sats, ni ukuvuga igiciro c’inyama z’ingurube. Kugira ngo nshobore kworohereza akarorero, narakuyeho n’ibigirankana amafaranga y’i Mining muri iki gikorwa.


### PayJoin ni iyaki?


Iryo soko rya PayJoin rirangura intumbero zibiri, rikaba rituma abakoresha bashobora kwongerera ibanga ry’amahera bariha.


Ica mbere, PayJoin ifise intumbero yo kuzimiza umuntu wo hanze yihweza mu kurema uruyeri mu gusesangura uruhererekane. Ivyo bishobozwa n’ubuhinga bwa CIOH (*Ubuhinga bwa Ownership bw’Injiza Rusangi*). Nk’uko twabibonye mu gice ca 3, kenshi, iyo igikorwa co gucuruza kuri Blockchain gifise ibintu vyinshi vyinjizwa, bifatwa ko ivyo bintu vyose ari ivy’ikigo kimwe canke umukoresha umwe.


Rero, iyo umuhinga mu vy’ugusesangura asuzuma igikorwa ca PayJoin, aca ajana mu kwizera ko ivyo vyose biva ku muntu umwe. Ariko rero, iyo nzira ni mbi, kuko uwuhembwa na we nyene atanga umusanzu ku vyo yinjiza iruhande y’uwuhembwa nyawe. Isesengura ry’uruzitiro rero rihindurwa rikaja ku nsobanuro ihinduka ikinyoma.


Reka dufate akarorero kacu k’ugucuruza PayJoin ku bijanye no kwishura umukate:


![BTC204](assets/rn/172.webp)


Kubona iyo nzira kuri Blockchain, umuntu wo hanze akurikije ubuhinga busanzwe bwo gusesangura Blockchain yoshobora gutanga insobanuro ikurikira: "*Alice yashize hamwe UTXO 2 nk'ivyo kwinjiza mu nzira kugira ngo yishure 19.000 GW*6-1010".


![BTC204](assets/rn/173.webp)


Ivyo bisobanuro biragaragara ko ataco bimaze, kuko nk’uko musanzwe mubizi, izo UTXO zibiri ziri mu vyo kwinjiza ntiziri iz’umuntu umwe. Imwe iva kuri Alice, uwugura baguette, iyindi iva kuri Bob, uwukora imikate.


![BTC204](assets/rn/174.webp)


Muri ubwo buryo, isesengura ry’uwubibona wo hanze rirongorwa ku nsozero itari yo, bigatuma ibanga ry’abafatanyabikorwa rizigama.


### Ivyo gucuruza


Intumbero ya kabiri ya PayJoin ni ukuzimiza umuntu wo hanze ariko arabibona ku bijanye n’ingero nyayo y’amahera yatanzwe. Mu gusuzuma ingene iyo nzira y’ugucuruza iteye, uwo musesanguzi yoshobora kwiyumvira yuko iyo nkunga ingana n’ingero y’imwe mu nzira zisohoka.


Nitwasubira ku karorero kacu k’ugugura umukate, umusesanguzi azokwiyumvira ko amahera yo kwishura ahuye n’amahera y’ama UTXO y’ama Sats 6.000, canke n’ama UTXO y’ama Sats 19.000. Muri ivyo, umusesanguzi azohitamwo kwiyumvira ko amahera yo kwishura ari 19.000 Sats, kuko hariho UTXO 2 mu bisohoka, n’imiburiburi imwe muri yo ikaba nini kuruta 6.000 Sats (nta mpamvu yumvikana yo gukoresha single UTXO 2 kugira ngo umuntu yishure 6.000 GW a-1000). vyari bihagije kugira ngo bihaze iyo nshumbusho).


![BTC204](assets/rn/175.webp)


Ariko mu vy’ukuri, iyo nseguro irafise amakosa. Igitigiri c’amahera yo kwishura ntigihuye n’ivyo bivako vyose. Ni mu vy’ukuri itandukaniro riri hagati ya UTXO y’uwuronka mu vyo asohora n’ivyo uwuronka UTXO mu vyo yinjiza.


![BTC204](assets/rn/176.webp)


Muri ivyo, igikorwa ca PayJoin kigwa mu rwego rw’ubuhinga bwa steganography. Bituma umubare nyawo w’ibintu bigurishwa uhishwa mu gicuruzwa c’ikinyoma gikora nk’uruyeri.


Steganography ni ubuhinga bwo guhisha amakuru mu yandi makuru canke mu bindi bintu, kugira ngo ukubaho kw’ayo makuru yanyegejwe ntikuboneke. Nk’akarorero, ubutumwa bw’ibanga burashobora guhishwa mu kadomo mu nyandiko zidafitaniye isano, bigatuma butaboneka n’ijisho ry’umuntu (ubu ni ubuhinga bwa [microdot](https://fr.wikipedia.org/wiki/Micropoint)).


Mu buryo butandukanye n’ugushiramwo amakuru, ivyo bikaba bituma amakuru adashobora gutahurwa ata rufunguzo rwo gufungura amakuru, steganography ntihindura amakuru. Iguma yerekanwa mu nyandiko zitomoye. Ahubwo intumbero yayo ni iyo guhisha ukubaho kw’ubutumwa bw’ibanga ubwabwo, mu gihe guhisha amakuru ahishijwe bigaragaza neza ko hariho amakuru yihishije, naho nyene ata rufunguruzo umuntu yoyaronka. Ni co gituma izina ry'intango rya PayJoin ryari "ibikorwa vy'ubudandaji".


Igereranyo rishobora gufatwa hagati y'ubuhinga bwo gucapura na CoinJoin, no hagati y'ubuhinga bwo gucapura na PayJoin. CoinJoin ifise ibintu bisa n’ivyo gushiramwo amakuru: uburyo buramenyekana, ariko amakuru ntashobora gusobanurwamwo. Ku rundi ruhande, PayJoin isa n’ivyo steganography: amakuru arashobora gushikwako mu vyiyumviro, ariko kubera ko uburyo bwo kuyahisha butamenyekana, araba uwudashobora gushikira.


### None PayJoin noyikoresha gute?


Porogarama zizwi cane zifasha PayJoin harimwo Sparrow wallet, Wasabi Wallet, Mutiny, BitMask, BlueWallet na JoinMarket, hamwe n’umuhinga wo kwishura BTCPay.


![BTC204](assets/rn/177.webp)


Ishirwa mu ngiro rya PayJoin ryari ryiza cane ryari Stowaway gusa kuri Samourai Wallet. Ariko rero, kuva abashinze iyo porogarama bafatwa, ubu ico gikoresho kirakora gusa igice. Ivyiza vya Stowaway ni uko ari umurongo wuzuye, woroshe gukoresha, ushigikira kwakira no kohereza ama payjoins. amafaranga afise umukono w’igice ashobora guhindurwa n’amaboko mu gucapura amakode menshi ya QR, canke agahindurwa ubwayo na Tor biciye kuri Soroban. Iryo hitamwo rya nyuma ryo guhanahana amakuru ubu ntaco rikora.


![BTC204](assets/rn/178.webp)


Ingorane yo gukoresha PayJoin iri mu kuba ivana n’uruhara rw’umucuruzi. Nk’umukiriya, ntushobora gukoresha PayJoin iyo umucuruzi atayishigikiye. Ivyo vyongera ku yindi ngorane ku bijanye n’ugugura: ntibigoye gusa kuronka abacuruzi bemera Bitcoin, ariko iyo urondeye n’abashigikiye payjoins, birarushiriza kugorana.


Umuti umwe woba ari ugukoresha imiterere y’ugucuruza izana ubusobanuro butari bwo mu gusesangura uruhererekane ataco bisaba ubufatanye bw’uwuronka. Ivyo vyotuma dushobora gutuma ivyo twishura biguma ari ibanga ata kwizigira uruhara rw’abadandaza. Ivyo nyene ni vyo tuzoba turiko turaraba mu kigabane gikurikira.




https://planb.network/tutorials/privacy/on-chain/payjoin-samourai-wallet-48a5c711-ee3d-44db-b812-c55913080eab

## Ukwishura guto-CoinJoin


<chapterId>300777ee-30ae-43d7-ab00-479dac3522c1</chapterId>



Igihe ushaka gukora igikorwa co kwishura mu gihe uguma ufise ibanga ry’urugero runaka, PayJoin ni uburyo bwiza. Ariko nk’uko twabibonye, ​​PayJoin isaba ko uwuyironka agira uruharamwo. None wokora iki iyo uwuronka iyo mpapuro yanse kuja mu gikorwa ca PayJoin, canke iyo uhisemwo gusa kutabagiramwo uruhara? Imwe mu nzira ni ugukoresha uruhome rw’amabuye canke uruhome rw’amabuye x2. Reka twihweze neza ubwo bwoko bubiri bw’ugucuruza.


### Ubucuruzi bwa Stonewall


Stonewall ni uburyo bwihariye bwo gukoresha Bitcoin bugenewe kwongerera ibanga ry’abakoresha igihe bakoresha amahera mu kwigana pseudo-CoinJoin hagati y’abantu babiri, ataco mu vy’ukuri ari umwe. Nkako, iyo nzira y’ugucuruza si iyo gukorana. Uwukoresha arashobora kuyubaka ku giti ciwe, akoresheje gusa ama UTXO afise nk’ivyo yinjiza. Ushobora rero gukora igikorwa ca Stonewall ku musi mukuru uwo ari wo wose, udakeneye gukorana n’uwundi muntu canke uwuronka.


Igikoresho ca Stonewall gikora gutya: nk’inyungu mu gikorwa, uwutanga akoresha UTXO 2 ziwe. Ku bijanye n’isohoka, iyo nzira y’ugucuruza itanga UTXO 4, 2 muri zo zikaba zingana neza na neza. Ibindi 2 UTXO nivyo bizogira ihinduka. Mu bisohoka 2 vy’amahera amwe, kimwe gusa ni co kizoja mu vy’ukuri ku wuzohembwa.


Rero hariho gusa uruhara 2 mu gucuruza Stonewall:




- Uwutanga, ni we ariha;
- Uwuronka, yoshobora kuba atazi kamere yihariye y’ivyo bicuruzwa kandi akaba yiteze gusa ko uwumurungikiye ariha.


Reka dufate akarorero kugira ngo dutahure iyo nzira y’ugucuruza. Alice ija kuri Bob umutetsi kugira ngo agure umukate wiwe, ugura 4.000 Sats. Ashaka kwishura mu bitcoins, mu gihe agumana uburyo bumwe bumwe bw’ibanga ku bijanye n’ukwishura kwiwe. Ni co gituma afata ingingo yo kwubaka ikibanza co gukoreramwo Stonewall kugira ngo ashobore kwishura.


![BTC204](assets/rn/179.webp)


Dusuzumye iyo nzira, turashobora kubona ko Bob umutetsi mu vy’ukuri yaronse 4.000 Sats mu kwishura iyo baguette. Alice yakoresheje UTXO 2 nk'ivyo gukoresha: imwe y'amashanyarazi 10.000 Sats n'iyindi y'amashanyarazi 15.000 Sats. Mu bikorwa, yararonse ama UTXO 3: imwe y'amashanyarazi 4.000 Sats, iyindi y'amashanyarazi 6.000 Sats n'iyindi y'amashanyarazi 11.000 Sats. Alice rero ifise amafaranga -4.000 Sats kuri iyo nzira, ivyo bikaba bihuye n’igiciro c’iyo baguette.


Muri aka karorero, narasuzuguye n’ibigirankana amafaranga y’i Mining kugira ngo vyorohe gutahura. Mu vy’ukuri, amahera y’ugucuruza yishurwa yose n’uwutanga.


### Ni izihe ntumbero z’ugucuruza Stonewall?


Igishushanyo ca Stonewall congeramwo entropie nyinshi cane ku bijanye n’ugucuruza, kigatuma imirongo y’isesengura ry’uruzitiro igaragara neza. Iyo umuntu abonye hanze, mwene ukwo gucuruza kwoshobora gusobanurwamwo ko ari mini-CoinJoin hagati y’abantu babiri. Ariko mu vy’ukuri, ni ukwishurwa. Ubwo buryo rero buratuma habaho ukudakeka mu gusesangura uruhererekane, canke mbere bukajana ku nzira z’ibinyoma.


Reka dufate akarorero ka Alice kuri Bob y’umutetsi. Ivyo gucuruza kuri Blockchain vyosa n’ibi:


![BTC204](assets/rn/180.webp)


Umuntu wo hanze yizigiye ubuhinga bwo gusesangura uruhererekane yoshobora gushika ku ciyumviro kitari co c'uko "*abantu babiri bakoze CoinJoin ntoyi, ifise UTXO imwe mu vyo yinjiza n'ibindi bibiri UTXOs mu vyo yinjiza*". Gusuzuma iyo nzira y’ubudandaji uhereye hanze ntibituma hakoreshwa CIOH, kuko kubaho kw’ibisohoka bibiri vy’umubare umwe bigaragaza uburyo bwa CoinJoin. Uvuye hanze, CIOH rero ntishobora gukoreshwa muri iki kibazo kidasanzwe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/181.webp)


Iyi nsobanuro ntabwo ari yo, kuko nk’uko mubizi, UTXO imwe yarungitswe kuri Bob umutetsi, izo 2 UTXO zavuye kuri Alice, aca asubirana 3 z’ihinduka.


![BTC204](assets/rn/182.webp)


Kandi ikintu gishimishije cane ku bijanye n’imiterere y’isoko rya Stonewall ni uko, umuntu abona hanze, risa n’iry’isoko rya Stonewall x2 mu buryo bwose.


### Ivy’ugucuruza kw’Ibuye x2.


Stonewall x2 ni ubundi buryo bwihariye bw’ugucuruza Bitcoin na bwo bugamije kwongerera ibanga ry’abakoresha igihe bakoresha amahera, ariko ubu mu gukorana n’umuntu wa gatatu atagira uruhara muri ayo mafaranga. Ubwo buryo bukora nk’ubuhinga bwa pseudo-CoinJoin hagati y’abantu babiri bari muri iyo nama, mu gihe nyene bariha umuntu agira gatatu.


Ibikorwa vy’ugucuruza Stonewall x2 birasanzwe: dukoresha urupapuro rwa UTXO dufise kugira ngo twishure, kandi tugasaba imfashanyo y’uwundi muntu na we nyene atanga n’urupapuro rwa UTXO rwiwe. Iryo soko rirangizwa n’ibisohoka bine: bibiri muri vyo mu mahera angana, kimwe kigenewe Address y’uwuhembwa, ikindi kigenewe Address y’uwukorana. UTXO ya gatatu isubizwa ku yindi Address y’uwo mufatanyabikorwa, bikamushoboza gusubirana amahera ya mbere (igikorwa kitagira aho kigarukira kuri we, modulo igiciro ca Mining), UTXO ya nyuma igasubizwa ku Address ihinduka ari iya twebwe.


Uruhara rutatu rutandukanye rero rurasobanurwa mu bikorwa vya Stonewall x2:




- Uwutanga, ni we ariha vy’ukuri;
- Uwuronka, ashobora kuba atazi uburyo bwihariye bw’ivyo bicuruzwa kandi akaba yiteze gusa ko uwumurungikiye amwishura;
- Uwo mufatanyabikorwa, atuma bitcoins ziboneka kugira ngo ashire amakenga ku bijanye n’isesengura ry’ivyo akora, mu gihe asubiza amahera yiwe yose ku mpera (igikorwa kitagira aho kigarukira kuri we, modulo the Mining costs).


Reka dusubire ku karorero kacu na Alice, ari kuri Bob umutetsi kugira ngo agure umukate wiwe, ugura 4.000 Sats. Ashaka kwishura mu bitcoins, mu gihe agumana urugero runaka rw’ibanga ku bijanye n’ukwishura kwiwe. Ni co gituma ahamagara umugenzi wiwe Charles, azomufasha muri ivyo.


![BTC204](assets/rn/183.webp)


Dusuzumye iyo nzira, turabona ko Bob umutetsi mu vy’ukuri yaronse 4.000 Sats mu kwishura iyo baguette. Alice yakoresheje 10.000 Sats mu vyo yinjiza, igarura 6.000 Sats mu vyo isohora, ni ukuvuga ko -4.000 Sats, bihuye n’igiciro c’iyi baguette. Na Charles we, yatanze 15.000 Sats mu vyo yinjiza, aronka n’ibindi bibiri: kimwe ca 4.000 Sats ikindi ca 11.000 Sats, bitanga umubare w’amazi 0.


Muri aka karorero, narasigaye n’ibigirankana amafaranga kugira ngo vyorohe gutahura. Mu vy’ukuri, amahera ya Mining muri rusangi asangizwa kimwe hagati y’uwutanga amahera n’uwutanga.


### Ni izihe ntumbero z’ugucuruza Stonewall x2?


Cokimwe n’imiterere ya Stonewall, imiterere ya Stonewall x2 yongerako entropie nyinshi ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kandi igatera urujijo mu gusesangura uruhererekane. Iyo umuntu abonye hanze, mwene ukwo gucuruza gushobora gusobanurwamwo ko ari aga CoinJoin gatoyi hagati y’abantu babiri. Ariko mu vy’ukuri, ni ukwishura. Ubwo buryo rero buratuma habaho ukudakeka mu gusesangura uruhererekane, canke mbere bikajana ku nzira z’ibinyoma.


Reka dufate akarorero ka Alice, Bob umukate w’imikate na Charles. Ivyo gucuruza kuri Blockchain vyosa n’ibi:


![BTC204](assets/rn/184.webp)


Umuntu wo hanze yizigiye ubuhinga bwo gusesangura uruhererekane yoshobora gushika ku ciyumviro kitari co c'uko "*Alice na Charles bakoze CoinJoin ntoyi, hariho UTXO imwe mu vyo yinjiza n'ibindi bibiri UTXOs mu vyo asohoka*". Na none, gusuzuma iyo nzira y’ugucuruza uvuye hanze ntibituma hakoreshwa ICOH, kuko kubaho kw’ibisohoka bibiri vy’umubare umwe bigaragaza uburyo bwa CoinJoin. Uvuye hanze, CIOH rero ntishobora gukoreshwa muri iki kibazo kidasanzwe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/185.webp)


Iyi nsobanuro ntabwo ari yo, kuko nk’uko mubizi, UTXO imwe yarungitswe kuri Bob umutetsi, Alice ifise igisohoka kimwe gusa co guhindura, Charles na we afise ibiri.


![BTC204](assets/rn/186.webp)


Kandi na none, ikintu gishimishije cane ku bijanye n’imiterere y’isoko rya Stonewall x2 ni uko, umuntu abona ibintu hanze, risa n’iry’isoko rya Stonewall mu buryo bwose.


### Ni itandukaniro irihe riri hagati y'Ibuye n'Ibuye x2?


Igikoresho ca StonewallX2 gikora neza neza nk’igikoresho ca Stonewall, kiretse ko ica mbere ari ugukorana, mu gihe ica kabiri kitakora. Nk’uko twabibonye, ​​igikorwa ca Stonewall x2 gifise uruhara rw’umuntu agira gatatu (Charles), ari hanze y’ukwishyura, kandi azotuma amafaranga yiwe y’ibice bita bitcoins aboneka kugira ngo yongere ibanga ry’igicuruzwa. Mu gucuruza kwa kera kwa Stonewall, uruhara rw’umufatanyabikorwa rufatwa n’uwurungitse.


![BTC204](assets/rn/187.webp)


Umuntu aravye hanze, uburyo bwo gucuruza ni nk’ubwo nyene.


![BTC204](assets/rn/188.webp)


Kuba izo nzira zibiri z'ubudandaji zisangiye neza neza uburyo bumwe bisigura ko naho umuntu wo hanze yoshobora kumenya uburyo bwa "Stonewall(x2)", ntazogira amakuru yose. Ntazoshobora kumenya uwuhe muri izo UTXO zibiri z’amahera amwe ahuye n’ivyo yishuye. Ikindi kandi, ntazoshobora kumenya nimba izo UTXO zibiri zifise inputs zivuye ku bantu babiri batandukanye (Stonewall x2) canke nimba ari iz’umuntu umwe yazihuje (Stonewall).


Iyi ngingo ya nyuma iterwa n’uko amafaranga y’i Stonewall x2 akurikira neza na neza uburyo bumwe n’ubw’amafaranga y’i Stonewall. Uravye hanze, kandi ata makuru y’inyongera, ntibishoboka gutandukanya igikorwa ca Stonewall n’igikorwa ca Stonewall x2. Ivya mbere si ibikorwa vy’ubufatanye, mu gihe ivya nyuma ari vyo. Ivyo birongereza mbere amakenga ku bijanye n’ugusuzuma kimwe muri ivyo bicuruzwa.


### Ni ryari amafaranga y’amabuye n’amabuye x2 akwiye gukoreshwa?


Ivyiyumviro bikwiye kuba ibi bikurikira igihe ushaka gukoresha igikoresho c’ibanga ku bijanye n’amahera:




- Nk’ivyo dushira imbere, turashobora guhitamwo gukora PayJoin;
- Iyo umucuruzi adashigikiye payjoins, igikorwa co gukorana gishobora gukorwa n’uwundi muntu hanze y’ukwishyura hakoreshejwe ubuhinga bwa Stonewall x2;
- Niwaba udashobora kuronka umuntu wo gukora igikorwa ca Stonewall x2, urashobora gukora igikorwa ca Stonewall gusa, kizokwigana inyifato y’igikorwa ca Stonewall x2.


### Nokoresha gute amafaranga y’amabuye n’amabuye x2?


Ivy’ugucuruza vy’amabuye n’ivy’amabuye x2 biraboneka kuri porogarama ya Samourai Wallet no kuri porogarama ya Sparrow wallet.


![BTC204](assets/rn/189.webp)


Ariko nk’uko biri ku bijanye n’ama payjoins, inyuma y’ugufatwa kw’abashinze Samourai, ubu amafaranga y’ubudandaji ya Stonewall x2 akora gusa mu guhinduranya ama PSBT n’amaboko hagati y’ababifisemwo uruhara. Ikibabaje ni uko Exchange yikora biciye kuri Soroban itagihari.


Birashoboka kandi gukora ubwo bwoko bw’ugucuruza n’amaboko ukoresheje porogarama iyo ari yo yose ya Bitcoin Wallet.


Mu kigabane gikurikira, turaza kuraba ubundi buryo bwo gukingira ibanga butazwi cane, ariko bufise akamaro kanini nk’inyongera y’ivyo twamaze kwiga.


https://planb.network/tutorials/privacy/on-chain/stonewall-033daa45-d42c-40e1-9511-cea89751c3d4

https://planb.network/tutorials/privacy/on-chain/stonewall-x2-05120280-f6f9-4e14-9fb8-c9e603f73e5b

## Ivyo bikoko


<chapterId>db9a20ac-a149-443d-884b-ea6c03f28499</chapterId>



Ikoreshwa ry’imiterere y’ubucuruzi ya Bitcoin yongera ubusobanuro ku gusesangura uruhererekane, nka CoinJoin, ni ngirakamaro cane cane ku bijanye no kurinda ubuzima bwite. Ariko nk’uko twabibonye mu kigabane kivuga ku bijanye n’ama payjoins, amafaranga CoinJoin aramenyekana mu buryo busanzwe ku ruzitiro. Ibuka isano twashize hagati y’ugushiramwo amakuru n’ugushiramwo amakuru: iyo dosiye ipfutse, uwundi muntu agira gatatu abonye iyo dosiye ipfutse ntashobora gushika ku birimwo, ariko arashobora kumenya neza ko iyo dosiye yahinduwe kugira ngo ihishe ibirimwo. Ivyo ni ko biri no kuri CoinJoin: iyo umusesanguzi asuzuma igikorwa ca CoinJoin, naho adashobora gushinga amasano ataziguye hagati y’ivyo yinjiza n’ivyo asohoka (n’ibihushanye n’ivyo), arashobora kwemera ko igikorwa abonye ari CoinJoin.


Bivanye n’ingene wipfuza gukoresha UTXO yawe inyuma y’ingendo za CoinJoin, kuba yaciye muri iyo nzira birashobora kuba ingorane. Nk’akarorero, nimba utegura kugurisha Coin yawe ku rubuga rwa Exchange rutegekanijwe, ariko ikaba iherutse guca muri CoinJoin, igikoresho co gusuzuma uruzitiro rw’urubuga kizomenya ico kintu. Iryo koraniro rishobora rero kwanka kwemera UTXO yawe coinjoined, canke mbere rigusaba insobanuro, bikaba bishobora gutuma konti yawe ihagarara canke amahera yawe agahagarara. Mu bihe bimwe bimwe, iyo nzira irashobora kandi kumenyesha inyifato yawe ubutegetsi bwa Leta (ivyo ni nk’akarorero, ivyo TRACFIN isaba aba PSAN mu Bufaransa, canke Ishirahamwe ry’Igihugu ry’Ivyaha vy’Ivy’Imari (FinCEN) rikora muri Amerika).


![BTC204](assets/rn/190.webp)


Hariho igikoresho gishobora gupfuka ibimenyetso vy’ivya kera vya Bitcoin Coin, kugira ngo bisubire ku buryo bumwe bumwe bw’uguhinduka. Ivyo ni vyo nyene ricochet igamije.


![BTC204](assets/rn/191.webp)


### Ricochet ni iki?


Ricochet ni ubuhinga bugizwe no gukora ibikorwa vyinshi vy'ibinyoma ku muntu (sweep) kugira ngo yigane ukwimurira Bitcoin Ownership. Ico gikoresho gitandukanye n’ibindi bice vy’ubudandaji twavuganye, kuko kitaronka ukutamenyekana kw’imbere, ahubwo kironka uburyo bwo kutamenyekana kw’inyuma. Mu vy’ukuri, ricochet irapfuka ibintu vyihariye bishobora gutuma Bitcoin Coin idakora neza kubera kahise kayo.


Kugira ngo ricochet ikore ibikorwa bine bikurikirana aho uwuyikoresha yirungikira amahera ku ma aderesi atandukanye.


![BTC204](assets/rn/192.webp)


Inyuma y’uru rukurikirane rw’ibikorwa, igikoresho ca ricochet kiraheza kigatuma ama bitcoins aja aho aja, nk’urubuga rwa Exchange.


![BTC204](assets/rn/193.webp)


Intumbero ni ugutuma habaho urugendo rugira ico rukoze ku bushobozi bwa Coin, nk’ugucuruza kwa CoinJoin, n’igikorwa ca nyuma c’ugukoresha amahera, coshobora kwanka iyi Coin kubera kahise kayo. Gutyo, ibikoresho vyo gusesangura uruhererekane vyoshobora gushika ku ciyumviro c’uko kumbure hariho ihinduka rya Ownership inyuma y’ico kintu, maze bikabona ko iyo Coin ishobora guhinduka. Ku bijanye na CoinJoin, ibikoresho vyo gusesangura Blockchain vyoshobora rero kwiyumvira ko atari we muntu nyene yarungitse izo bitcoins kandi akagira CoinJoin, kandi ko rero ata co bimaze gufata ingingo ku muntu yarungitse.


![BTC204](assets/rn/194.webp)


### Ni kuki bikora?


Umuntu ahanganye n’ubwo buryo bwa ricochet, yoshobora kwiyumvira ko porogarama yo gusesangura uruzitiro yoshobora gutuma isuzuma ryayo rirushiriza gusubira inyuma incuro zine. Ariko rero, izo nzira zihura n’ingorane yo gutuma urugero rwo kumenya ibintu rugenda neza. Bategerezwa gushinga urugero rw’umubare w’ibipfunsi hanyuma bakemera ko hariho ihinduka ry’umutungo, kandi ko isano n’ikintu cabaye imbere (nk’i CoinJoin) rikwiye kwirengagizwa.


![BTC204](assets/rn/195.webp)


Ariko rero, gushinga iyo nzira ni akaga: ukwaguka kwose kw’umubare w’ibisimbuka vyerekanwa kwongerekana cane kw’ivyiza vy’ibinyoma, ni ukuvuga abantu bashizweko ikimenyetso c’uko ari abaje mu kintu, mu gihe mu vy’ukuri igikorwa cakozwe n’uwundi muntu. Ivyo bishobora gutuma ayo mashirahamwe agira ingorane nyinshi, kuko ivyiza bitari vyo bituma abantu badashira akanyota, ivyo bikaba bishobora gutuma abakiriya bashikiwe n’ingorane baja mu mahiganwa. Mu gihe kirekire, urugero rwo kumenya rwo hejuru cane rutuma urubuga rutakaza abakiriya benshi kurusha abaruhanganye, ivyo bikaba vyoshobora gutuma ubuzima bwarwo buhungabana. Biragoye rero ko izo nzira zongerera umubare w’ibisubizo vyerekanwa, kandi 4 akenshi ni umubare uhagije wo guhangana n’isesengura ryazo.
