- Bob ibara urufunguzo rw’ibanga rujanye n’urwo rufunguzo rwa bose rw’igihe gito mu kwongerako urufunguzo rw’ibanga rw’umukobwa wiwe ruva kuri kode yiwe yo kwishura n’ibanga basangiye.


![BTC204](assets/rn/239.webp)


Kubera ko Alice idashobora kuronka $b$ (urufunguzo rw’ibanga rwa Bob), ntashobora kumenya $k0$ (urufunguzo rw’ibanga rujanye n’ukwakira BIP47 kwa Address Address). Mu buryo bw'igishushanyo, turashobora guserura ibara ry'ibanga ry'abantu bose $S$ nk'uko bikurikira:


![BTC204](assets/rn/240.webp)


Igihe ibanga ry’abantu bose ribonetse na ECDH, Alice na Bob baharura urufunguzo rwa bose rwo kwishura BIP47 $K0$, na Bob na yo iharura urufunguzo rw’ibanga rujanye n’ivyo $k0$:


![BTC204](assets/rn/241.webp)


### Gusubizwa amahera ya BIP47


Kubera ko Bob azi kode ya Alice yo gusubira gukoresha, arasanzwe afise amakuru yose akeneye kugira ngo amurungikire amahera. Ntazosubira guhamagara Alice kugira ngo asabe amakuru yose. Arakeneye gusa kumumenyesha n’ugutanga amakuru, kugira ngo ashobore kuronka amaderesi yiwe ya BIP47 n’impapuro ziwe za seed, hanyuma ashobore no kumurungikira amahera ashika kuri `2^32`.


Ivyo gusubiza amahera ni vyo vyihariye kuri BIP47 kandi ni kimwe mu vyiza vyayo kuruta ubundi buryo, nk’Ukwishura mu gacerere, ivyo tuzobiraba mu bice bizokurikira.


Bob ashobora rero kwishura Alice mu buryo bumwe nyene yamurungikiye amahera. Uruhara rurahindurwa:


![BTC204](assets/rn/242.webp)


*Turakoze cane [Fanis Michalakis](https://x.com/FanisMichalakis) ku gukosora n'impanuro z'abahinga ku ngingo yatumye ndiko ndandika iki gice!*


https://planb.network/tutorials/privacy/on-chain/paynym-bip47-a492a70b-50eb-4f95-a766-bae2c5535093

## Ukwishyura mu gacerere


<chapterId>2871d594-414e-4598-a830-91c9eb84dfb8</chapterId>



BIP47 yaranezwe cane kubera ukuntu idakora neza. Nk’uko vyasiguwe mu kigabane c’imbere, bisaba ko habaho igikorwa co kumenyesha umuntu wese azoronka. Ivyo bica bihinduka bike iyo duteguye gushinga umurongo w’ukwishura uramba n’uwo muronka. Nkako, igikorwa kimwe co kumenyesha kirategura inzira y’umubare hafi utagira uko ungana w’amahera ya BIP47 akurikira.


Ariko rero, mu bihe bimwebimwe, ugucuruza kw’imenyekanisha birashobora kuba intambamyi ku wubikoresha. Reka dufate akarorero k’intererano y’igihe kimwe ku muntu ayihawe: n’iyi Bitcoin Address ya kera, igikorwa kimwe gusa kirahagije kugira ngo umuntu arangize iyo mpano. Ariko kuri BIP47, bisaba ko haba amafaranga abiri: rimwe ry’imenyekanisha, irindi ry’ukwishura nyavyo. Iyo ugusaba umwanya w’amabarabara ari hasi kandi amafaranga y’ugucuruza ari make, iyo ntambwe y’inyongera ntabwo ari ingorane kenshi. Ariko rero, mu bihe vy’uguhagarara, amahera yo gukoresha arashobora kuba menshi cane ku kwishura rimwe, bikaba bishobora gutuma uwukoresha atanga incuro zibiri ugereranije n’ugukoresha Bitcoin, ivyo bikaba bishobora gutuma uwukoresha atavyemera.


Ku bihe aho uwukoresha ategura gutanga amahera makeyi gusa ku kimenyetso kidahinduka, hariho ibindi bisubizo vyateguwe. Ivyo birimwo n’Ivyishyurwa Bicereje, bivugwa muri [BIP352]( Iyi porotokole ituma bishoboka gukoresha ikimenyetso kidahinduka kugira ngo umuntu aronke amahera ataco akora kugira ngo Address isubire gukoreshwa, kandi ataco asaba gukoresha amafaranga y’imenyekanisha. Reka turabe ingene iyo protocole ikora.


---
*Kugira ngo utahure neza iki gice, ni ngombwa ko umenya neza ingene ECDH (Elliptic Curve Diffie-Hellman) ikora be n’ingene urufunguzo rwo mu rwego rwo hejuru rukora mu gitabu ca HD Wallet. Ivyo vyiyumviro vyari vyaravuzwe mu buryo burambuye mu kigabane ca mbere ku vyerekeye BIP47. Sinzobisubiramwo hano. Nimba utaramenya neza ivyo vyiyumviro, ndagusavye ko wobanza kuraba igice ca mbere imbere y’uko ukomeza n’iki. Sinzosubira ku ngorane zijanye n’ugusubira gukoresha amaderesi y’ukwakira, canke akamaro ko kugira ikimenyetso kidasanzwe co kwakira amahera.* Nzovuga gusa ingingo nkeyi noshima gushiramwo ngaha .


---
### Kubera iki utokwimurira iryo tangazo?


Nk’uko vyavuzwe mu kigabane ca BIP47, igikorwa co kumenyesha gifise ibikorwa bibiri nyamukuru:




- Iramenyesha uwuyironka;
- Irungika kode y’ukwishura y’uwuyirungitse.


Umuntu yoshobora kwiyumvira ataco yiyumvira ko iyo nzira yo kumenyesha yoshobora gukorwa off-chain. Mu vyiyumviro, birashoboka neza: uwuronka ivyo yoba akwiye gukora vyose ni ukwerekana uburyo bwo guhanahana amakuru kugira ngo aronke amakode y’ukwishura ya BIP47 avuye ku barungitse. Ariko rero, hari ingorane zibiri zikomeye ziri muri iyo nzira:




- Ica mbere, vyotuma uburyo bwo gutanga kode buja ku yindi nzira yo guhanahana amakuru. Ibibazo bijanye n’igiciro n’ibanga rya Exchange vyogumaho, ariko vyokwimurirwa gusa muri iyo porotokole nshasha. Ku bijanye n'ibanga, ivyo bishobora kandi gutuma habaho isano hagati y'akaranga k'ukoresha n'igikorwa co ku rubuga, ivyo ni vyo turondera kwirinda mu gukora itangazo ku Blockchain. Ikindi kandi, gukora iryo tangazo hanze ya Blockchain vyozana ingorane zo gucengera (nk’uguhagarika amahera) zitari kuri Bitcoin;
- Ica kabiri, ivyo vyotuma haba ingorane yo gukira. Na BIP47, uwuyironka ategerezwa kumenya amakode y’ukwishura y’abarungitse kugira ngo ashobore kuronka ayo mahera. Ivyo ni ukuri iyo umuntu yakiriye, ariko kandi iyo amahera yosubizwa biciye ku seed iyo Wallet yatakaye. Hamwe n'amatangazo y'uruzitiro, ivyo bishobora kwirindwa, kuko uwukoresha ashobora kuronka no gusobanura amakuru y'amatangazo mu kumenya gusa seed yiwe. Ariko rero, iyo itangazo rikorewe hanze ya Blockchain, uwuriko arakoresha yobwirizwa kuguma afise ububiko bukomeye bw’amakode yose y’ukwishyura yaronse, ivyo bikaba bidashoboka ku muntu asanzwe akoresha.


Ivyo vyose bituma gukoresha itangazo ry'uruzitiro biba ngombwa kuri BIP47. Ariko rero, Silent Payments irondera kwirinda iyo ntambwe yo kumenyesha onchain kubera igiciro cayo. Umuti wemejwe rero si ukwimurira itangazo, ahubwo ni ukurikuraho burundu. Kugira ivyo bishoboke, bitegerezwa kwemerwa ikintu co gusenyera ku mugozi umwe: gucapura. Udakunze BIP47, aho uwukoresha amenya neza aho yoronka amahera yiwe biciye ku bikorwa vy’imenyekanisha, n’Ivyishyurwa vy’Iceceka, uwukoresha ategerezwa gusuzuma amahera yose ariho ya Bitcoin kugira ngo amenye amahera yose yagenewe kumuha. Kugira ngo uwo muzigo w’ibikorwa ugabanuke, ubushakashatsi bw’Ivyishyurwa Bicereje bugarukira gusa ku bikorwa bishobora kuba birimwo ivyo vyishyurwa, ni ukuvuga ivyo bifise n’imiburiburi umusaruro umwe wa Taproot P2TR. Iryo scanner kandi ryibanda cane ku bikorwa vy’ubudandaji kuva kw’itariki Wallet yaremeweko (nta nkenerwa yo gupima ibikorwa vy’ubudandaji kuva mu 2009 nimba Wallet yaremwe mu 2024).


Ushobora rero kubona igituma BIP47 na Silent Payments, naho zigamije intumbero imwe, zirimwo uguhuza ibintu bitandukanye rero **mu vy’ukuri zihuye n’ibintu bitandukanye bikoreshwa**. Ku bijanye n’amahera yishurwa rimwe gusa, nk’intererano zitangwa rimwe gusa, Silent Payments ni zo zibereye cane kubera ko zigura amahera make. Ku rundi ruhande, ku bijanye n’ugucuruza ubudasiba ku muntu umwe, nk’uko biri ku bibanza vya Exchange canke ku bidengeri vya Mining, BIP47 yoshobora guhitamwo.


Reka turabe ingene Silent Payments ikora mu buryo bw’ubuhinga kugira ngo dutahure neza ico kiriko kiraba. Kugira ivyo tubishikeko, ndasaba ko dufata uburyo bumwe n’ubw’inyandiko y’insobanuro ya BIP352. Buhoro buhoro tuzoca ducapura imibare izokorwa, ikintu ku kindi, dushingira intahe ivyongeweko bishasha vyose.


### Ivyiyumviro bikeyi vyo gutahura


Imbere yo gutangura, birahambaye kugaragaza ko Ukwishura mu gacerere kwizigira gukoresha ubwoko bw'inyandiko P2TR (*Ishura kuri Taproot*) gusa. Udakunze BIP47, si ngombwa gukura amaderesi y'ukwakira mu mfunguruzo za bose z'abana biciye mu gukora hashing. Mu rugero rwa P2TR, urufunguzo rwa bose rwahinduwe rukoreshwa ataco ruvuze kandi rudashizwemwo amakuru muri Address. Rero Taproot yakira Address ni urufunguzo rwa bose rufise amakuru amwamwe. Urufunguzo rwa bose rwahinduwe ni ugukoranya izindi mfunguruzo zibiri za bose: imwe ishoboza gukoresha amahera ataco akora, mu buryo busanzwe biciye ku musinya woroshe, iyindi iserukira Merkle Root ya MAST, yemerera gukoresha amahera hakurikijwe ukunyurwa kw’imwe mu ngingo zishobora kwandikwa muri Merkle Tree.


![BTC204](assets/rn/243.webp)


Hari impamvu zibiri nyamukuru zatumye hafatwa ingingo yo guhagarika amahera y’ugutanga amahera gusa kuri Taproot:




- Ica mbere, biroroshe cane gushirwa mu ngiro no guhindura muri kazoza porogarama ya Wallet, kubera ko hariho ingingo ngenderwako imwe gusa ikeneye kwubahirizwa;
- Ica kabiri, ubu buryo burafasha gutuma abakoresha bamenya neza mu kubaremesha kutigabanya hagati y’ubwoko butandukanye bw’inyandiko, izo generate zitandukanye Wallet ibimenyetso vy’intoke mu gusesangura uruzitiro (kugira ngo umenye vyinshi ku bijanye n’ico ciyumviro, raba igice ca 4 c’igice ca 2).


### Ugukomoka ku rufunguzo rwa bose rw'ukwishura mu gacerere


Reka dutangure n’akarorero koroshe kugira ngo tuje mu mutima w’ingene SPs (Silent Payments) zikora. Reka dufate Alice na Bob, abakoresha Bitcoin babiri. Alice yipfuza kohereza ama Bitcoins kuri Bob ku nzira y'ubusa yakira Address. Hariho intumbero zitatu z’ivyo bikorwa:




- Alice ategerezwa kuba ashoboye generate Address y’ubusa;
- Bob itegerezwa kuba ishoboye kumenya amahera yoherejwe kuri iyo Address yihariye;
- Bob arakeneye kumenya kuronka urufunguzo rw’ibanga rujanye n’uwo Address kugira ngo ashobore gukoresha amahera yiwe.


Alice ifise UTXO mu nzu yiwe itekanye Bitcoin Wallet ifise urufunguzo rubiri rukurikira:




- $a$: urufunguzo rw'ibanga;
- $A$: urufunguzo rwa bose ($A = a \cdot G$)


Bob afise SP Address yasohoye kuri internet afise:




- $b$: urufunguzo rw'ibanga;
- $B$: urufunguzo rwa bose ($B = b \cdot G$)


Mu kugarura Address ya Bob, Alice irashobora kubara Address nshasha y’ubusa ari iya Bob ikoresheje ECDH. Reka twite iyi Address $P$:


$$ P = B + \umwandiko {Hash}(a \cakadomo B) \cakadomo G $$


Muri iyi nkuru, Alice yaharuye gusa igiharuro c'urufunguzo rwiwe rw'ibanga $a$ n'urufunguzo rwa bose rwa Bob $B$. Yaciye atanga ico ciyumviro mu gikorwa ca Hash kizwi na bose. Agaciro kavuyemwo rero kagwizwa n'intangamarara $G$ y'umurongo w'uruzitiro `secp256k1`. Ubwa nyuma, Alice yongerako ikintu kiva ku rufunguzo rwa bose rwa Bob $B$. Igihe Alice ifise iyo Address $P$, ayikoresha nk’igisubizo mu gucuruza, ni ukuvuga ko ayirungikira ama bitcoins.


> *Mu bijanye n'Ivyishyurwa Bicereje, igikorwa ca "Hash" gihuye n'igikorwa ca SHA256 Hash gifise ikimenyetso c'uko `BIP0352/SharedSecret`, kigaragaza ko ama hashes yashizweho ari ay'umwihariko muri iyi porotokole kandi adashobora gusubira gukoreshwa mu bindi bice vy'uburinzi bw'ikimenyetso c'amatangazo. Iryo tegeko rihuye n’iryo [ryerekanwa muri BIP340 ku mikono ya Schnorr] (ku rubuga rwa `secp256k1`.*
Kubera imiterere y’umurongo w’uruzitiro ECDH ishingiyeko, turazi ko:


$$ a \cakadomo B = b \cakadomo A $$


Bob rero izoshobora kubara Address yakira iyo Alice yarungikiyeko ama bitcoins. Kugira ngo abikore, akurikirana amafaranga yose ya Bitcoin ahuye n’ingingo ngenderwako y’Ivyishyurwa vy’Iceceka, agakoresha iyi mibare ikurikira kuri buri kimwe muri vyo kugira ngo arabe nimba ivyo vyishyurwa bimurungikiye (*scanning*):


$$ P' = B + \umwandiko {Hash}(b \cakadomo A) \cakadomo G $$


Iyo asuzumye igikorwa ca Alice, abona ko $P'$ ingana na $P$. Arazi rero ko iyo nshumbusho igenewe we:


$$ P' = B + \umwandiko{Hash}(b \cakadomo A) \cakadomo G = B + \umwandiko{Hash}(a \cakadomo B) \cakadomo G = P $$


Havuye hano, Bob izoshobora kubara urufunguzo rw'ibanga $p$ rutuma Address $P$ ikoreshwa:


$$ p = (b + \umwandiko {Hash}(b \cdot A)) \bmod n $$


Nk'uko ushobora kubibona, kugira ngo ubaze uru rufunguzo rw'ibanga $p$, utegerezwa kuba ufise urufunguzo rw'ibanga $b$. Bob yonyene ni yo igira urufunguzo rw'ibanga $b$. Ni we rero azoba ari we wenyene azoshobora gukoresha amafaranga y’ama bitcoins yoherejwe kuri Silent Payments Address yiwe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/244.webp)


*Umugani:*




- $B$: Urufunguzo rwa bose/rudahinduka Address rwasohowe na Bob
- $b$: Urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwa Bob
- $A$: Urufunguzo rwa bose rwa Alice rwa UTXO rukoreshwa nk'inyungu y'ibikorwa
- $a$: Urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwa Alice
- $G$: Igiharuro c'umurongo w'umurongo `secp256k1`
- $\umwandiko{SHA256}$: Umurimo wa SHA256 Hash washizweko ikimenyetso na `BIP0352/Ibanga ryasangiwe`
- $s$: Ibanga rusangi rya ECDH
- $P$: Urufunguzo rwa bose/Address yihariye yo kwishura Bob


Ehe uburyo bwo gutangura butari bwiza bwo gukoresha Bob Address, izwi $B$, kugira ngo ubone Address $P$ yihariye yo koherezako bitcoins. Ariko rero, ubwo buryo burasanzwe cane kandi burafise utunenge twinshi dukwiye gukosorwa. Ikibazo ca mbere ni uko, muri iki gikorwa, Alice idashobora kurema ibisohoka vyinshi kuri Bob mu gihe c’ugucuruza kumwe.


### None noshobora gute kurema ibisohoka vyinshi?


Mu karorero kari mu gice ca mbere, Alice irema igisohoka kimwe kizoja kuri Bob ku Address $P$ yiwe yihariye. Hamwe n'inyungu imwe yatowe, ntibishoboka ko Alice irema aderesi zibiri zitandukanye z'ubusa za Bob, kuko uburyo bukoreshwa bwokwama bujana ku gisubizo kimwe kuri $P$, ni ukuvuga Address imwe. Ariko rero, hariho ibintu vyinshi bishika aho Alice yipfuza kugabanya amahera yishuye Bob mu bice bitobito vyinshi, gutyo bigatuma habaho UTXO nyinshi. Ni ngombwa rero kurondera uburyo bwo kubishikako.


Kugira ngo ivyo bishoboke, tugiye guhindura gatoyi ibara Alice ikora kugira ngo ibone $P$, kugira ngo ashobore generate aderesi zibiri zitandukanye za Bob, ni ukuvuga $P_0$ na $P_1$.


Kugira ngo uhindure ibara maze ubone aderesi 2 zitandukanye, wongereko gusa umubare wose uhindura igisubizo. Gutyo, Alice azokwongerako $0$ ku biharuro vyiwe kugira ngo aronke Address $P_0$ na $1$ kugira aronke Address $P_1$. Reka twite uyu mubare wose $i$:


$$ P_i = B + \umwandiko{Hash}(a \cdot B \umwandiko{‖ } i) \cdot G $$


Uburyo bwo kubara ntibwahindutse ku buryo bwa kera, kiretse ko ubu Alice izofatanya $a \cdot B$ na $i$ imbere yo gukomeza na Hash. Ushobora rero guhindura $i$ kugira uronke Address nshasha y'ivya Bob. Nk'akarorero:


$$ P_0 = B + \umwandiko{Hash}(a \cakadomo B \umwandiko{‖} 0) \cakadomo G $$


$$ P_1 = B + \umwandiko{Hash}(a \cakadomo B \umwandiko{‖} 1) \cakadomo G $$


Igihe Bob asuzuma Blockchain ku bijanye n’Ivyishurwa vy’Iceceka vyamugenewe, atangura akoresheje $i = 0$ ku Address $P_0$. Iyo ata n’imwe abonye yishurwa kuri $P_0$, aca afata ingingo y’uko iyo transaction ata n’imwe irimwo Silent Payments yagenewe we, maze agaheba iyo scanner. Ariko iyo $P_0$ ari ngirakamaro kandi irimwo amahera amuhevye, abandanya na $P_1$ muri iyo nzira nyene kugira ngo asuzume nimba Alice yakoze amahera ya kabiri. Iyo $P_1$ igaragara ko ataco imaze, ihagarika kurondera iyo nzira; ahandi ho, irabandanya igerageza agaciro ka $i$ gakurikirana:


$$ P_0 = B + \umwandiko {Hash}(b \cdot A \umwandiko{‖ } 0) \cdot G $$


$$ P_1 = B + \umwandiko {Hash}(b \cdot A \umwandiko{ ‖ } 1) \cdot G $$


Kubera ko Bob ihagarara ubwo nyene kuri $i = 0$ iyo $P_0$ idakora, gukoresha uyu mubare wose ntivyongera hafi umuzigo w'ibikorwa wongerewe kuri Bob ku ntambwe yo gupima ibikorwa.


Bob ishobora rero kubara imfunguruzo z'ibanga mu buryo bumwe:


$$
p_0 = (b + \text{hash}(b \cdot A \text{ ‖ } 0)) \bmod n
$$


$$
p_1 = (b + \text{hash}(b \cdot A \text{ ‖ } 1)) \bmod n
$$


![BTC204](assets/rn/245.webp)


*Umugani:*




- $B$: Urufunguzo rwa bose/rudahinduka Address rwasohowe na Bob
- $b$: Urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwa Bob
- $A$: Urufunguzo rwa bose rwa Alice rwa UTXO rukoreshwa nk'inyungu y'ibikorwa
- $a$: Urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwa Alice
- $G$: Igiharuro c'umurongo w'umurongo `secp256k1`
- $\umwandiko{SHA256}$: Umurimo wa SHA256 Hash washizweko ikimenyetso na `BIP0352/Ibanga ryasangiwe`
- $s_0$: Ibanga rya mbere rusangi ECDH
- $s_1$: Ibanga rya kabiri rusangi rya ECDH
- $P_0$: Urufunguzo rwa mbere rwa bose / Address yihariye yo kwishura Bob
- $P_1$: Urufunguzo rwa kabiri rwa bose / Address yihariye yo kwishura Bob


N’ubu buryo, turiko turatangura kuronka umurongo mwiza, ariko haracariho ingorane nkeyi zo gutsinda, n’ugukingira Address gusubira gukoreshwa.


### Ni gute twokwirinda gusubira gukoresha Address?


Nk'uko twabibonye mu bice vyabanje, Alice ikoresha urufunguzo rubiri rukingira UTXO yiwe, izokoresha mu kubara ibanga ECDH isangiye na Bob. Iryo banga rituma ashobora kuronka Address $P_0$ idasanzwe. Ariko rero, urufunguzo rubiri ($a$, $A$) rwakoreshejwe na Alice rurashobora gukingira UTXO nyinshi nimba yasubiyemwo iyo Address incuro nyinshi. Mu gihe Alice yotanga amahera abiri kuri Bob ya Address $B$ ikoresheje UTXO zibiri zikingiwe n'urufunguzo rumwe $A$, ivyo vyotuma Address isubira gukoreshwa kuri Bob.


> *Address gusubira gukoresha ni umugenzo mubi cane mu bijanye n'ibanga ry'abakoresha. Kugira ngo umenye igituma, ndaguhanura ngo usubiremwo ibice vya mbere vy’iri shure.*
Nkako, kuko Address $P_0$ yihariye ikomoka kuri $A$ na $B$, rero nimba Alice ikomoka kuri Address ya kabiri ku kwishura ubwa kabiri kuri $B$, n'urufunguzo rumwe $A$, azoheza kuri Address $P_$0 imwe nyene. Kugira ngo twirinde iyo ngorane kandi ntihagire Address isubira gukoreshwa mu gihe c’Ivyishyurwa vy’Iceceka, tuzokenera guhindura gatoyi imibare yacu.


Ico twipfuza ni uko UTXO yose ikoreshwa na Alice nk’injiza mu kwishura kugira ngo itange Address yihariye ku ruhande rwa Bob, naho UTXO nyinshi zoba zikingiwe n’urufunguzo rumwe. Rero ico dukeneye gukora n'ukwongerako ivyerekeye UTXO igihe tubarura Address $P_0$ yihariye. Iyi nzira izoba gusa Hash ya UTXO ikoreshwa nk'inyungu:


$$ \umwandiko {injizaHash} = \umwandiko{Hash}(\umwandiko{isohoka} \umwandiko{‖ } A) $$


Kandi Alice izokwongerako iyi nsiguro ku vyo yinjije mu kubara kwiwe kw'ibara ry'umwihariko Address $P_0$:


$$ P_0 = B + \umwandiko{Hash}(\umwandiko{Hash y'injiza} \cdot a \cakadomo B \umwandiko{ ‖ } 0) \cdot G $$


Igihe ariko arapima, Bob arashobora kandi kwongerako $\text{inputHash}$, kuko ivyo ategerezwa gukora vyose ni ukwihweza igikorwa kugira ngo akuremwo $\text{isohoka}$:


$$ P_0 = B + \umwandiko{Hash}(\umwandiko{Hash y'injiza} \cdot b \cdot A \umwandiko{ ‖ } 0) \cdot G $$


Iyo ibonye $P_0$ ibereye, ishobora kubara urufunguzo rw'ibanga $p_0$ ruhuye:


$$
p_0 = (b + \text{hash}(\text{inputHash} \cdot b \cdot A \text{ ‖ } 0)) \bmod n
$$


![BTC204](assets/rn/246.webp)


*Umugani:*




- $B$: Urufunguzo rwa bose/rudahinduka Address rwasohowe na Bob
- $b$: Urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwa Bob
- $A$: Urufunguzo rwa bose rwa Alice rwa UTXO rukoreshwa nk'inyungu y'ibikorwa
- $a$: Urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwa Alice
- $H$: UTXO Hash ikoreshwa nk'inyungu
- $G$: Igiharuro c'umurongo w'umurongo `secp256k1`
- $\umwandiko{SHA256}$: Umurimo wa SHA256 Hash washizweko ikimenyetso na `BIP0352/Ibanga ryasangiwe`
- $s_0$: Ibanga rya mbere rusangi rya ECDH
- $P_0$: Urufunguzo rwa mbere rwa bose / Address yihariye yo kwishura Bob


Kugeza ubu, imibare yacu yiyumvira ko Alice ikoresha input imwe ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kwiwe. Ariko rero, akwiye kuba ashoboye gukoresha ibintu vyinshi. Ku bw’ivyo, ku ruhande rwa Bob, ku bijanye n’ugucuruza kwose kurimwo ibintu vyinshi, akwiye guharura mu buryo bw’ivyiyumviro ECDH ku bintu vyose kugira ngo amenye nimba hari ivyo yishuye. Ubwo buryo ntibushimishije, rero turakeneye kurondera umuti wo kugabanya umuzigo w’akazi!


### Guhindura imfunguruzo za bose mu vyinjijwe


Kugira ngo dutorere umuti iki kibazo, aho gukoresha urufunguzo rubiri rukingira inyungu yihariye ku ruhande rwa Alice, tuzokoresha umubare w'urufunguzo rwose rukoreshwa mu vyo kwinjiza vy'ugucuruza. Ico kigereranyo kizoca gifatwa nk’urufunguzo rushasha. Ubu buhinga buzwi nka "tweaking".


Nk’akarorero, reka twiyumvire ko igikorwa ca Alice gifise ibintu 3 vyinjizwa, kimwe cose kikaba gikingijwe n’urufunguzo rutandukanye:




- $a_0$ ikoreshwa mu gukingira inyungu #0;
- $a_1$ ikoreshwa mu gukingira inyungu #1;
- $a_2$ icungera inyinjizo #2.


![BTC204](assets/rn/247.webp)


Dukurikije uburyo bwavuzwe mbere, Alice yobwirizwa guhitamwo urufunguzo rumwe muri $a_0$, $a_1$, na $a_2$ kugira ngo abare ibanga rya ECDH na generate ukwishyura kumwe Address $P$ kuva kuri sta ya Bob-$6. Ariko rero, ubu buryo busaba ko Bob agerageza ubushobozi bwose bukurikirana, atangura na $a_0$, hanyuma $a_1$, n'ibindi, gushika abonye umugwi utanga $P$ Address ibereye. Ivyo bisaba ko Bob ikoresha ibara rya ECDH ku bintu vyose vyinjizwa mu bikorwa vyose, ivyo bikaba vyongera cane umuzigo w’ibikorwa vyo gupima.


Kugira ngo ivyo ntibibeho, tuzosaba Alice kubara $P$ ikoresheje umubare w'imfunguruzo zose z'inyungu. Dukoresheje akarorero kacu, urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwahinduwe $a$ rwobarwa gutya:


$$ a = a_0 + a_1 + a_2 $$


Mu buryo nk'ubwo, Alice na Bob barashobora kubara urufunguzo rwa bose rwahinduwe:


$$ A = A_0 + A_1 + A_2 $$


Ukoresheje ubu buryo, Bob ikeneye gusa kubara umubare w’imfunguruzo za bose z’isoko, hanyuma igaharura ibanga rya ECDH kuva kuri $A$ gusa, ivyo bikaba bigabanya cane umubare w’imibare isabwa ku ntambwe yo gupima.


Ariko rero, niwibuke igice c’imbere. Twari twongeyeko $\text{inputHash}$ Hash ku biharuro vyacu, ikoreshwa nk'iyi Nonce kugira ngo twirinde gusubira gukoresha Address:


$$ \umwandiko {injizaHash} = \umwandiko{Hash}(\umwandiko{isohoka} \umwandiko{‖ } A) $$


Ariko iyo ufise ivyinjizwa vyinshi mu gucuruza, ukeneye kumenya $\text{outpoint}$ yatowe muri iki giharuro. Dushingiye kuri BIP352, ikigereranyo co guhitamwo $\text{outpoint}$ kizokoreshwa ni uguhitamwo gitoyi kuruta ibindi vyose mu buryo bw’inkoranyabumenyi, ivyo bikaba bisobanura guhitamwo UTXO iboneka ubwa mbere mu buryo bw’inyuguti. Ubwo buryo burahuza UTXO izotorwa mu bikorwa vyose. Nk'akarorero, iyo iyi $\text{isohoka}$ ntoyi cane mu rurimi rw'inkoranyabumenyi ari $\text{isohoka}_L$, ibara rya $\text{inputHash}$ rizoba:


$$ \umwandiko{injizaHash} = \umwandiko{Hash}(\umwandiko{isohoka}_L \umwandiko{‖ } A) $$


Ivyo biharuro rero biguma bimeze nk’ivyo vyashikirijwe mu gice ca mbere, kiretse ko urufunguzo rw’ibanga $a$ n’urufunguzo rwa bose ruhuye n’urwo $A$ bitagikoreshwa mu gucungera inyungu imwe, ariko ubu bigereranya tweak ku migwi yose y’urufunguzo mu vyinjizwa.


### Gutandukanya amafaranga n'imfunguruzo zo gupima


Kugeza ubu, twavuze ku kwishura mu gacerere Address $B$ nk'urufunguzo rwa bose rwihariye. Ibuka, ni uru rufunguzo rwa bose $B$ Alice ikoresha mu kurema ibanga ry'abantu bose ECDH, na ryo rikaba riharura ukwishyura kwihariye Address $P$. Bob ikoresha uru rufunguzo rwa bose $B$ n'urufunguzo rw'ibanga ruhuye $b$ ku ntambwe yo gupima. Ariko azokoresha kandi urufunguzo rw’ibanga $b$ kugira ngo abare urufunguzo rw’ibanga $p$ rushoboza gukoresha amahera kuva kuri Address $P$.


Ikibi c’ubu buryo ni uko urufunguzo rw’ibanga $b$ (rukoreshwa mu kubara urufunguzo rw’ibanga rwose rw’izo aderesi zaronse Silent Payments) na rwo nyene rukoreshwa na Bob mu gucapura amafaranga. Iyi ntambwe isaba ko urufunguzo rwa $b$ ruboneka kuri porogaramu ya Wallet ihuye na internet, ivyo bikaba bituma rushobora kwibwa kuruta kurugumya kuri Cold Wallet. Mu vyiza, vyoba vyiza umuntu ashobora gukoresha neza Silent Payments mu gihe aguma afise urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwa $b$, rugenzura ukuntu umuntu ashobora gushika ku zindi mfunguruzo zose z'ibanga, rutekanye kuri Hardware Wallet. Igishimishije ni uko iyo protocole yahinduwe kugira ngo yemere ivyo nyene.


Kugira ngo ivyo bishoboke, BIP352 isaba ko uwuyikira akoresha imfunguruzo 2 zitandukanye:




- $b_{\text{spend}}$: kubara imfunguruzo z'ibanga z'amaderesi yihariye yo kwishura;
- $b_{\umwandiko{scan}}$: kugira uronke amaderesi yihariye yo kwishura.


Muri ubwo buryo, Bob arashobora kugumya urufunguzo rw’ibanga $b_{\text{spend}}$ kuri Hardware Wallet maze agakoresha urufunguzo rw’ibanga $b_{\text{scan}}$ kuri porogarama yo kuri interineti kugira aronke Ivyishyurwa vyiwe vy’Iceceka, ataco ahishura $b_{\text{spend}}$. Ku rundi ruhande, imfunguruzo za bose $B_{\text{scan}}$ na $B_{\text{spend}}$ zompi zihishurirwa ku mugaragaro, kuko ziri mu Bob zidahinduka Address $B$:


$$ B = B_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \umwandiko{ ‖ } B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}} $$


Kugira ngo ubaze amahera yihariye Address $P_0$ ari aya Bob, Alice ubu izokora iki giharuro gikurikira:


$$ P_0 = B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}} + \umwandiko{Hash}(\umwandiko{injizaHash} \cdot a \cdot B_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \cdot{ ‖ } 0) \cdot G $$


Kugira ngo uronke amahera yamurungikiye, Bob izokora ibi biharuro bikurikira:


$$ P_0 = B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}} + \umwandiko{Hash}(\umwandiko{injizaHash} \cdot b_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \cdot A \umwandiko{ ‖ } 0) \cdot G $$


Nk'uko ushobora kubibona, gushika ubu Bob ntiyakeneye gukoresha $b_{\text{spend}}$, iri kuri Hardware Wallet yiwe. Iyo ashaka gukoresha UTXO ijyanye na $P_0$, ashobora gukora ibiharuro bikurikira kugira aronke urufunguzo rw’ibanga $p_0$:


$$ p_0 = (b_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}} + \umwandiko{Hash}(\umwandiko{injizaHash} \cdot b_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \cdot A \umwandiko{ ‖ } 0)) \bmod n $$


![BTC204](assets/rn/248.webp)


*Umugani:*




- $B_{\umwandiko{gupima}}$: Urufunguzo rwo gupima rusangi rwa Bob (Address idahinduka)
- $b_{\umwandiko{gupima}}$: Urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwa Bob
- $B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}}$: Urufunguzo rwa Bob rwo gukoresha amahera ya Leta (Address idahinduka)
- $b_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}}$: Urufunguzo rw'ugukoresha bwite rwa Bob
- $A$: Umubare w'ibishizwemwo urufunguzo rwa bose (tweak)
- $a$: Urufunguzo rwihariye rujanye n'urufunguzo rwa bose rwahinduwe
- $H$: Hash ya UTXO ntoyi cane (mu rurimi rw'inkoranyabumenyi) ikoreshwa nk'inyungu
- $G$: Igiharuro c'umurongo w'umurongo `secp256k1`
- $\umwandiko{SHA256}$: Umurimo wa SHA256 Hash washizweko ikimenyetso na `BIP0352/Ibanga ryasangiwe`
- $s_0$: Ibanga rya mbere rusangi ECDH
- $P_0$: Urufunguzo rwa mbere rwa bose / Address yihariye yo kwishura Bob


### Gukoresha aderesi za SP zifise ikimenyetso


Bob rero ifise Address $B$ idahinduka ku kwishura mu gacerere nk’uko:


$$ B = B_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \umwandiko{‖ } B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}} $$


Ikibazo kiri muri ubu buryo ni uko butaguha uburenganzira bwo gutandukanya amafaranga atandukanye yoherezwa kuri iyi Address. Nk’akarorero, nimba Bob afise abakiriya 2 batandukanye ku bucuruzi bwiwe, kandi ashaka gutandukanya amahera kuri buri wese, azokenera amaderesi 2 atandukanye adahinduka. Umuti w'ubujuju, n'uburyo buriho ubu, woba ari uko Bob yorema amasakoshi abiri atandukanye, imwe yose ifise Address yayo, canke mbere igashinga aderesi zibiri zitandukanye muri Wallet imwe. Ariko rero, uwo muti usaba gucapura Blockchain yose incuro zibiri (rimwe kuri Address imwe imwe) kugira ngo umenye amahera agenewe kuri Address imwe imwe. Ukwo gupima kabiri birongereza umuzigo w’ibikorwa vya Bob ata co bimaze.


Kugira ngo iki kibazo gitorerwe umuti, BIP352 ikoresha uburyo bwo gushiramwo amazina yemerera amaderesi atandukanye, ataco yongera ku kazi ko kurondera amahera y'amahera kuri Blockchain. Kugira ngo ivyo tubishikeko, twongerako umubare wose $m$ ku rufunguzo rw'amahera ya bose $B_{\text{spend}}$. Uwo mubare wose ushobora gufata agaciro ka $1$ ku Address ya mbere idahinduka, hanyuma $2$ ku ya kabiri, n’ibindi. Imfunguruzo zo gukoresha $B_{\text{spend}}$ ubu zizokwitwa $B_m$ kandi zizoba zubatswe muri ubu buryo:


$$ B_m = B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}} + \umwandiko{Hash}(b_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \umwandiko{‖ } m) \cdot G $$


Nk'akarorero, ku rufunguzo rwa mbere rw'amahera rufise ikimenyetso $1$:


$$ B_1 = B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}} + \umwandiko{Hash}(b_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \umwandiko{‖ } 1) \cdot G $$


Igiharuro ca Address casohowe na Bob ubu kizoba gifise $B_{\umwandiko{gupima}}$ na $B_m$. Nk'akarorero, Address ya mbere idahinduka ifise ikimenyetso $1$ izoba:


$$ B = B_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \umwandiko{‖ } B_1 $$


> *Dutangura gusa n'ikimenyetso 1 kuko ikimenyetso 0 ni co cabikiwe ihinduka.*
Alice, ku ruhande rwiwe, azoronka ukwishyura kumwe Address $P$ mu buryo bumwe n'ubwo mbere, ariko akoresheje $B_1$ nshasha aho gukoresha $B_{\text{spend}}$:


$$ P_0 = B_1 + \umwandiko{Hash}(\umwandiko{injizaHash} \cdot a \cdot B_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \cdot{ ‖ } 0) \cdot G $$


Mu vy'ukuri, Alice ntabwo azi ko Bob ifise ikimenyetso Address, kuko ariko arakoresha gusa igice ca kabiri c'ivyo Address yatanze, kandi muri iki gihe, ni agaciro $B_1$ aho gukoresha $B_{text.${spend}


Kugira ngo ukore scanner y'amahera, Bob azokwama akoresha agaciro k'intango yiwe Address n' $B_{\text{spend}}$ muri ubu buryo:


$$ P_0 = B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}} + \umwandiko{Hash}(\umwandiko{injizaHash} \cdot b_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \cdot A \umwandiko{ ‖ } 0) \cdot G $$


Hanyuma, akuraho gusa agaciro abona kuri $P_0$ ku gisohoka cose kimwe kimwe. Araheza asuzuma nimba kimwe muri ivyo bivuye muri ivyo bikurwako gihuye n'agaciro k'ikimwe mu bimenyetso akoresha kuri Wallet yiwe. Niba, nk'akarorero, igisohoka #4 gihuye n'ikimenyetso ca $1$, ivyo bisigura ko ico gisohoka ari Ukwishura kw'Iceceka gifitaniye isano n'ikimenyetso caco Address $B_1$:


$$ Isohoka_4 - P_0 = \umwandiko {Hash}(b_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \umwandiko{‖ } 1) \cdot G $$


Bikora kuko:


$$ B_1 = B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}} + \umwandiko{Hash}(b_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \umwandiko{‖ } 1) \cdot G $$


Ushimiye ubu buryo, Bob ashobora gukoresha amaderesi menshi adahinduka ($B_1$, $B_2$, $B_3$...), yose akomoka ku ntambara yiwe y'ishimikiro Address ($B = B_{\umwandiko{scan}} \umwandiko{se. } usa


Ariko rero, ndabinginze mumenye ko uku gutandukanya amaderesi adahinduka ari ngirakamaro gusa mu bijanye n’uburongozi bw’umuntu ku giti ciwe Wallet, ariko ntigutandukanya akaranga. Kubera ko zose zifise $B_{\text{scan}}$ imwe, biroroshe cane gufatanya amaderesi yose adahinduka hamwe maze ugaca ubona ko ari ay'ikintu kimwe.


![BTC204](assets/rn/249.webp)


*Umugani:*




- $B_{\umwandiko{gupima}}$: Urufunguzo rwo gupima rusangi rwa Bob (Address idahinduka)
- $b_{\umwandiko{gupima}}$: Urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwa Bob
- $B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}}$: Urufunguzo rwa Bob rwo gukoresha amahera ya Leta (Address y'intango)
- $B_m$: Urufunguzo rw'amahera ya Leta rwa Bob rwanditsweko (Address idahinduka)
- $b_m$: Urufunguzo rw'amahera y'ibanga rwa Bob rwanditsweko
- $A$: Umubare w'ibishizwemwo urufunguzo rwa bose (tweak)
- $a$: Urufunguzo rwihariye rujanye n'urufunguzo rwa bose rwahinduwe
- $H$: Hash ya UTXO ntoyi cane (mu rurimi rw'inkoranyabumenyi) ikoreshwa nk'inyungu
- $G$: Igiharuro c'umurongo w'umurongo `secp256k1`
- $\umwandiko{SHA256}$: Umurimo wa SHA256 Hash washizweko ikimenyetso na `BIP0352/Ibanga ryasangiwe`
- $s_0$: Ibanga rya mbere rusangi rya ECDH
- $P_0$: Urufunguzo rwa mbere rwa bose / Address yihariye yo kwishura Bob
- $p_0$: Urufunguzo rw'ibanga rw'ukwishura kwa mbere kwihariye Address gushika kuri Bob
- $X$: Hash y'urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwo gupima n'ikimenyetso


### None noshobora gute kwubaka Address y’Ivyishyurwa Bicereje?


Kugira ngo wubake Address yihariye ku kwishura mu gacerere, ubanza gukura amafunguro 2 abiri muri Bitcoin HD Wallet yawe:




- Ibiri $b_{\umwandiko{scan}}$, $B_{\umwandiko{scan}}$ kugira ngo urondere amahera yaturungikiye;
- Ivyo bibiri $b_{\igisomwa{gukoresha}}$, $B_{\igisomwa{gukoresha}}$ kugira ngo twiyumvire amafaranga y'ibiceri twaronse.


Ivyo bice bibiri biva hakoreshejwe inzira zikurikira (*Bitcoin Mainnet*):


```text
scan: m / 352' / 0' / 0' / 1' / 0
spend: m / 352' / 0' / 0' / 0' / 0
```


Tumaze kuronka izo mfunguruzo 2, turazifatanya gusa (kuva ku mpera kugeza ku mpera) kugira ngo dukore umuzigo w’inyungu Address:


$$ B = B_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \umwandiko{‖ } B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}} $$


Niba dushaka gukoresha ibimenyetso, tuzosubiriza $B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}}$ na $B_m$:


$$ B = B_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \umwandiko{‖ } B_m $$


N'ikimenyetso $m$:


$$ B_m = B_{\umwandiko{gukoresha}} + \umwandiko{Hash}(b_{\umwandiko{gupima}} \umwandiko{‖ } m) \cdot G $$


Tumaze kuronka uwo muzigo, twongerako HRP (*Igice Gisomwa n’Umuntu*) `sp` na verisiyo `q` (= verisiyo 0). Twongerako kandi igiharuro c’isuzuma maze tugahindura Address ngo ibe bech32m.


Nk'akarorero, ng'iyi Address yanje y'Ivyishyurwa Bicereje:


```text
sp1qqvhjvsq2vz8zwrw372vuzle7472zup2ql3pz64yn5cpkw5ngv2n6jq4nl8cgm6zmu48yk3eq33ryc7aam6jrvrg0d0uuyzecfhx2wgsumcurv77e
```


Iciyumviro gihambaye ku bijanye n’amaderesi adahinduka, ushobora kuba waratahuye mu bice vyabanje, ni uko ayo maderesi ataboneka mu bikorwa vya Bitcoin. Aderesi zo kwishura $P$ zonyene zikoreshwa mu bisohoka ni zo ziboneka kuri Blockchain mu buryo busanzwe bwa Taproot. Rero, uhereye hanze, ntibishoboka gutandukanya igikorwa gifise Silent Payment n’igikorwa gisanzwe hakoreshejwe ibisohoka vya P2TR.


Nk’uko biri kuri BIP47, ntibishoboka gushinga isano hagati ya Address $B$ idahinduka n’ukwishura Address $P$ ikomoka kuri $B$. Nkako, naho Eva, uwushobora gutera, yogerageza gucapura Blockchain akoresheje static $B$ Address ya Bob, ntazoshobora gukora imibare isabwa kugira ngo amenye $P$. Kugira ngo abikore, yokenera urufunguzo rw'ibanga rwa Bob $b_{\text{scan}}$, canke urufunguzo rw'ibanga rw'uwarungitse $a$, ariko vyose ni ivy'ibanga. Birashoboka rero ko umuntu ahuza mu buryo butomoye Address yiwe idahinduka n’uburyo bumwe bw’akaranga k’umuntu.


### Nokoresha gute amahera y’uguceceka?


Iciyumviro co kwishura mu gacerere ni ikintu gishasha kandi cashizwe mu ngiro gusa n’umubare muto cane w’amasakoshi muri iki gihe. Ku bumenyi mfise, hariho gusa ibikoresho 3 vy’amaporogarama bibifasha:




- [Igikapu c'agakate](https://igikapu c'agakate.com/)
- [Uguceceka](https://app.uguceceka.dev/)
- [Igikapu c'Impano] (Igikapu c'Impano)


Tuzoba turiko turaguha inyigisho ido n'ido y'ingene woshiraho amahera yawe bwite y'ugutanga amahera y'agacerere Address.


Kubera ko iki kintu ari gishasha, turaguhanura kwiyubara no kwirinda gukoresha Silent Payments ku mahera menshi kuri Mainnet.


**Kugira ngo nkore iki gice ku vyerekeye Ukwishura mu gacerere, nakoresheje [urubuga rw'insobanuro y'ukwishyura mu gacerere](https://silentpayments.xyz/) na [inyandiko y'insobanuro ya BIP352]**
